    31→#endif
    32→#include "cangjie/Modules/ImportManager.h"
    33→
    34→namespace Cangjie {
    35→using HANDLE = void*;
    36→class GenericInstantiationManager;
    37→class MacroExpansion;
    38→class TypeChecker;
    39→class PackageManager;
    40→class BaseMangler;
    41→class TestManager;
    42→/**
    43→ * Compile util to some stage.
    44→ */
    45→enum class CompileStage {
    46→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
    47→    LOAD_PLUGINS, /**< Load compiler plugins. */
    48→#endif
    49→    PARSE,             /**< Parse the source code. */
    50→    CONDITION_COMPILE, /**< Conditional compile. */
    51→    IMPORT_PACKAGE,    /**< Import packages. */
    52→    MACRO_EXPAND,      /**< Expand macros. */
    53→    AST_DIFF,          /**< Diff the AST to get incremental compilation scope. */
    54→    SEMA,              /**< TypeCheck. */
    55→    DESUGAR_AFTER_SEMA,
    56→    GENERIC_INSTANTIATION, /**< GenericInstantiation. */
    57→    OVERFLOW_STRATEGY,     /**< Overflow strategy. */
    58→    MANGLING,              /**< Mangling all decls. */
    59→    SAVE_CJO,              /**< Save CJO. */
    60→    CHIR,                  /**< CHIR. */
    61→    RELEASE_AST,           /**< Release AST memory after CHIR lowering. */
    62→    CODEGEN,               /**< Generate target code. */
    63→    SAVE_RESULTS,          /**< Save AST and CHIR results to files. */
    64→
    65→    COMPILE_STAGE_NUMBER /**< The number of compile stage  */
    66→};
    67→
    68→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
    69→class CHIRData {
    70→public:
    71→    void InitData(std::unordered_map<unsigned int, std::string>* fileNameMap, size_t threadNum);
    72→
    73→    CHIR::CHIRContext& GetCHIRContext();
    74→
    75→    void AppendNewPackage(CHIR::Package* package);
    76→    std::vector<CHIR::Package*> GetAllCHIRPackages() const;
    77→    CHIR::Package* GetCurrentCHIRPackage() const;
    78→
    79→    void SetImplicitFuncs(const std::unordered_map<std::string, CHIR::FuncBase*>& funcs);
    80→    std::unordered_map<std::string, CHIR::FuncBase*> GetImplicitFuncs() const;
    81→
    82→    void SetConstVarInitFuncs(const std::vector<CHIR::FuncBase*>& funcs);
    83→    std::vector<CHIR::FuncBase*> GetConstVarInitFuncs() const;
    84→
    85→    CHIR::ConstAnalysisWrapper& GetConstAnalysisResultRef();
    86→    const CHIR::ConstAnalysisWrapper& GetConstAnalysisResult() const;
    87→
    88→private:
    89→    CHIR::CHIRContext cctx;
    90→    std::vector<CHIR::Package*> chirPkgs;
    91→    // used by codegen
    92→    std::unordered_map<std::string, CHIR::FuncBase*> implicitFuncs;
    93→    // used by interpreter
    94→    std::vector<CHIR::FuncBase*> initFuncsForConstVar;
    95→    // only for AnalysisWrapper
    96→    CHIR::CHIRBuilder builder{cctx, 0};
    97→    // provide the capability and results of constant analysis, used by cjlint
    98→    CHIR::ConstAnalysisWrapper constAnalysisWrapper{builder};
    99→};
   100→#endif
   101→
   102→/**
   103→ *  The base compiler instance, holds the data which has full compile lifetime.
   104→ */
   105→class CompilerInstance {
   106→    friend class CompileStrategy;
   107→    friend class MacroExpansion;
   108→    friend class MacroEvaluation;
   109→    friend class TypeChecker;
   110→    friend class GenericInstantiationManager;
   111→    friend class FullCompileStrategy;
   112→    friend class IncrementalCompileStrategy;
   113→
   114→public:
   115→    CompilerInstance(CompilerInvocation& invocation, DiagnosticEngine& diag);
   116→    virtual ~CompilerInstance();
   117→
   118→    /**
   119→     * Set different CompileStrategy to do the real compile jobs.
   120→     */
   121→    void SetCompileStrategy(CompileStrategy* newCompileStrategy)
   122→    {
   123→        delete this->compileStrategy;
   124→        this->compileStrategy = newCompileStrategy;
   125→    }
   126→    /**
   127→     * Initialize the compilation flow by
   128→     * 1) check pre-conditions
   129→     * 2) set the action functions in compilation flow
   130→     */
   131→    virtual bool InitCompilerInstance();
   132→
   133→    /**
   134→     * Perform compile to some @p stage.
   135→     */
   136→    virtual bool Compile(CompileStage stage = CompileStage::CHIR);
   137→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   138→    bool PerformPluginLoad();
   139→#endif
   140→
   141→    /**
   142→     * Perform parse.
   143→     */
   144→    virtual bool PerformParse();
   145→
   146→    virtual Ptr<AST::File> GetFileByPath(const std::string& filePath)
   147→    {
   148→        (void)filePath;
   149→        return nullptr;
   150→    }
   151→
   152→    /**
   153→     * Perform conditonal compilation.
   154→     */
   155→    virtual bool PerformConditionCompile();
   156→
   157→    /**
   158→     * Perform import package.
   159→     */
   160→    virtual bool PerformImportPackage();
   161→
   162→    /**
   163→     * Perform macro expand.
   164→     */
   165→    virtual bool PerformMacroExpand();
   166→
   167→    /**
   168→     * Perform AST diff to get incremental compilation scope.
   169→     */
   170→    virtual bool PerformIncrementalScopeAnalysis();
   171→    bool CalculateASTCache();
   172→
   173→    /**
   174→     * Perform typecheck and other semantic check jobs.
   175→     */
   176→    virtual bool PerformSema();
   177→
   178→    /**
   179→     * Perform desugar after sema.
   180→     */
   181→    virtual bool PerformDesugarAfterSema();
   182→
   183→    /**
   184→     * Perform generic instantiation.
   185→     */
   186→    virtual bool PerformGenericInstantiation();
   187→
   188→    /**
   189→     * Perform overflow strategy.
   190→     */
   191→    virtual bool PerformOverflowStrategy();
   192→
   193→    /**
   194→     * Perform Mangle.
   195→     */
   196→    virtual bool PerformMangling();
   197→    bool GenerateCHIRForPkg(AST::Package& pkg);
   198→    virtual bool PerformCHIRCompilation();
   199→
   200→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   201→    std::unordered_map<unsigned int, std::string>& GetFileNameMap()
   202→    {
   203→        return fileNameMap;
   204→    }
   205→#endif
   206→
   207→    /**
   208→     * Dump the parsed tokens for debugging.
   209→     */
   210→    virtual bool DumpTokens();
   211→
   212→    /**
   213→     * Dump the symbols for debugging.
   214→     */
   215→    virtual void DumpSymbols();
   216→
   217→    /**
   218→     * Dump the expanded macro for debugging.
   219→     */
   220→    virtual void DumpMacro();
   221→
   222→    /**
   223→     * Codegen to target code.
   224→     */
   225→    virtual bool PerformCodeGen()
   226→    {
   227→        return true;
   228→    }
   229→
   230→    /**
   231→     * Export AST and generate cjo.
   232→     */
   233→    virtual bool PerformCjoSaving()
   234→    {
   235→        return true;
   236→    }
   237→
   238→    /**
   239→     * Export AST and generate results.
   240→     */
   241→    virtual bool PerformResultsSaving()
   242→    {
   243→        return true;
   244→    }
   245→
   246→    /**
   247→     * Release AST memory after CHIR lowering is complete.
   248→     *
   249→     * @pre  CHIR lowering has completed (CompileStage::CHIR executed).
   250→     * @post AST nodes, ASTContext, and related managers are freed.
   251→     *       GetSourcePackages() returns empty. IsASTReleased() returns true.
   252→     */
   253→    virtual bool PerformASTRelease();
   254→
   255→    /**
   256→     * Check whether AST memory has been released.
   257→     */
   258→    bool IsASTReleased() const
   259→    {
   260→        return astReleased;
   261→    }
   262→
   263→    /**
   264→     * Get raw ptrs of all Packages after Compile.
   265→     *
   266→     * @return empty vector If Parse failed.
   267→     */
   268→    std::vector<Ptr<AST::Package>> GetPackages()
   269→    {
   270→        return pkgs;
   271→    }
   272→
   273→    /**
   274→     * Get raw ptrs of source Packages after Compile.
   275→     *
   276→     * @return empty vector If Parse failed.
   277→     */
   278→    std::vector<Ptr<AST::Package>> GetSourcePackages();
   279→
   280→    /**
   281→     * Get Source Manager.
   282→     */
   283→    SourceManager& GetSourceManager();
   284→    /**
   285→     * Get ASTContext by Package.
   286→     *
   287→     * @param pkg Package pointer.
   288→     * @return ASTContext of the @p pkg, if not found, return nullptr.
   289→     */
   290→    ASTContext* GetASTContextByPackage(Ptr<AST::Package> pkg) const;
   291→
   292→    /**
   293→     * Get dependent package of current package.
   294→     * Information is written in json format.
   295→     */
   296→    const std::vector<std::string>& GetDepPkgInfo()
   297→    {
   298→        return depPackageInfo;
   299→    }
   300→
   301→    /**
   302→     * Import all packages from other libs.
   303→     */
   304→    bool ImportPackages();
   305→
   306→    /**
   307→     * Get ExtendDecl Set from primitive type or Decl.
   308→     * @param type can be primitive type or Decl.
   309→     * @return set of Ptr<ExtendDecl>, if not found, return empty set.
   310→     */
   311→    std::set<Ptr<AST::ExtendDecl>> GetExtendDecls(
   312→        const std::variant<Ptr<AST::Ty>, Ptr<AST::InheritableDecl>>& type) const;
   313→
   314→    /**
   315→     * Obtains the extended members visible to the current file through the type declaration.
   316→     * @param type can be primitive type or Decl.
   317→     * @return vector of Ptr<ExtendDecl>, if not found, return empty set.
   318→     */
   319→    std::vector<Ptr<AST::Decl>> GetAllVisibleExtendMembers(
   320→        const std::variant<Ptr<AST::Ty>, Ptr<AST::InheritableDecl>>& type, const AST::File& curFile) const;
   321→
   322→    /**
   323→     * Get the candidate decls or types of given @p expr in given @p scopeName from sema cache @p ctx.
   324→     * If the @p hasLocal is true, the target will be found from local scope firstly.
   325→     * NOTE: used by lsp.
   326→     * @param ctx cached sema context.
   327→     * @param scopeName the scopeName of current position.
   328→     * @param expr the expression waiting to found candidate decls or types.
   329→     * @param hasLocalDecl whether the given expression is existed in the given scope.
   330→     * @return found candidate decls or types.
   331→     */
   332→    Candidate GetGivenReferenceTarget(
   333→        ASTContext& ctx, const std::string& scopeName, AST::Expr& expr, bool hasLocalDecl) const;
   334→
   335→    bool UpdateAndWriteCachedInfoToDisk();
   336→
   337→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   338→    /**
   339→     * Record the handle for compiler plugin
   340→     */
   341→    void AddPluginHandle(HANDLE handle)
   342→    {
   343→        (void)pluginHandles.emplace_back(handle);
   344→    }
   345→
   346→    /**
   347→     * Unload the handles for all compiler plugins
   348→     */
   349→    bool UnloadPluginHandle()
   350→    {
   351→        metaTransformPluginBuilder = {};
   352→        // plugins should be unloaded after metaTransformPluginBuilder deconstruction.
   353→        for (auto& handle : pluginHandles) {
   354→            if (InvokeRuntime::CloseSymbolTable(handle) != 0) {
   355→                Errorln("close plugin dynamic library failed.");
   356→                return false;
   357→            }
   358→        }
   359→        pluginHandles.clear();
   360→        return true;
   361→    }
   362→#endif
   363→
   364→    /**
   365→     * Infomation written to cached file and needed by incremental compiling
   366→     */
   367→    CompilationCache cachedInfo;
   368→
   369→    /**
   370→     * Infomation generated in CHIR stage
   371→     */
   372→    struct CHIRInfo {
   373→        OptEffectStrMap optEffectMap;
   374→        std::unordered_set<Ptr<const AST::StructTy>> ccTys;
   375→        VirtualWrapperDepMap curVirtFuncWrapDep;
   376→        VirtualWrapperDepMap delVirtFuncWrapForIncr;
   377→        std::set<std::string> ccOutFuncsRawMangle;
   378→        VarInitDepMap varInitDepMap;
   379→    };
   380→    CHIRInfo chirInfo;
   381→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   382→    MetaTransformPluginBuilder metaTransformPluginBuilder;
   383→#endif
   384→    /**

   440→    // Read source code from cache.

   442→    // SrcCodeChangeState
   443→    enum class SrcCodeChangeState : uint8_t {
   444→        UNCHANGED = 0,
   445→        CHANGED = 1,
   446→        ADDED = 2,
   447→        DELETED = 3,
   448→    };
   449→    struct SrcCodeCacheInfo {
   450→        SrcCodeChangeState state{SrcCodeChangeState::ADDED};
   451→        std::string code;
   452→        SrcCodeCacheInfo() = default;
   453→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(SrcCodeCacheInfo&& info) = default;
   454→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(const SrcCodeCacheInfo& info) = default;
   455→        SrcCodeCacheInfo& operator=(SrcCodeCacheInfo&& info) = default;
   456→        SrcCodeCacheInfo& operator=(const SrcCodeCacheInfo& info) = default;
   457→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(const std::string& code) : code(code) {};
   458→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(std::string&& code) : code(std::move(code)) {};
   459→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(SrcCodeChangeState state, const std::string& code) : state(state), code(code) {};
   460→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(SrcCodeChangeState state, std::string&& code) : state(state), code(std::move(code)) {};
   461→    };
   462→    // the source code cache map use for LSP and cjdb. Key is path, Value is source change state and source code.
   463→    std::unordered_map<std::string, SrcCodeCacheInfo> bufferCache;

    48→    // NOTE: since class layout is generated in separate step, we don not need to collect them.
    49→    //       And enum types have fixed layout for non-class or same as class type generation, it also can be ignored.

<details><summary>返回结果 (598 行)</summary>

```
     1→// Copyright (c) Huawei Technologies Co., Ltd. 2025. All rights reserved.
     2→// This source file is part of the Cangjie project, licensed under Apache-2.0
     3→// with Runtime Library Exception.
     4→//
     5→// See https://cangjie-lang.cn/pages/LICENSE for license information.
     6→
     7→/**
     8→ * @file
     9→ *
    10→ * This file implements the IncrementalCompilerInstance.
    11→ */
    12→
    13→#include "cangjie/FrontendTool/IncrementalCompilerInstance.h"
    14→#include <sstream>
    15→
    16→#include "cangjie/AST/Utils.h"
    17→#include "cangjie/Basic/StringConvertor.h"
    18→#include "cangjie/Basic/Version.h"
    19→#include "cangjie/Driver/TempFileManager.h"
    20→#include "cangjie/Modules/ImportManager.h"
    21→#include "cangjie/Modules/PackageManager.h"
    22→#include "cangjie/Parse/ASTHasher.h"
    23→#include "cangjie/Sema/IncrementalUtils.h"
    24→#include "cangjie/Utils/ConstantsUtils.h"
    25→#include "cangjie/Utils/FileUtil.h"
    26→#include "cangjie/Utils/ProfileRecorder.h"
    27→#include "llvm/IR/Constants.h"
    28→#include "llvm/IR/Metadata.h"
    29→#include "llvm/IR/Module.h"
    30→#include "llvm/IRReader/IRReader.h"
    31→#include "llvm/Support/SourceMgr.h"
    32→#include "cangjie/IncrementalCompilation/IncrementalCompilationLogger.h"
    33→
    34→
    35→#if (defined RELEASE)
    36→#include "cangjie/Utils/Signal.h"
    37→#endif
    38→
    39→using namespace Cangjie;
    40→using namespace AST;
    41→
    42→IncrementalCompilerInstance::~IncrementalCompilerInstance()
    43→{
    44→}
    45→
    46→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::InitCompilerInstance()
    47→{
    48→    return CompilerInstance::InitCompilerInstance();
    49→}
    50→
    51→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::SaveCompilationResult(Cangjie::IncreResult&& result)
    52→{
    53→    kind = result.kind;
    54→    rawMangleName2DeclMap = result.mangle2decl;
    55→    switch (kind) {
    56→        case IncreKind::ROLLBACK:
    57→            declsToBeReCompiled.clear();
    58→            [[fallthrough]];
    59→        case IncreKind::INCR:
    60→            cachedInfo = std::move(result.cacheInfo);
    61→            CacheCompileArgs();
    62→            declsToBeReCompiled = std::move(result.declsToRecompile);
    63→            rawIncrRemovedDecls = std::move(result.deleted);
    64→            // Copy a non-const version for 'Sema' usage.
    65→            for (auto& [mangle, decl] : result.mangle2decl) {
    66→                if (!decl->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPORTED)) {
    67→                    mangledName2DeclMap.emplace(mangle, Ptr(const_cast<Decl*>(decl.get())));
    68→                }
    69→            }
    70→            for (auto changed : declsToBeReCompiled) {
    71→                if (changed->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPORTED) && (changed->IsFunc() || IsGlobalOrStaticVar(*changed))) {
    72→                    cacheMangles.EmplaceImportedInlineDeclPtr(*changed);
    73→                } else {
    74→                    Sema::CollectRemovedManglesForReCompile(*changed, cachedInfo.semaInfo,
    75→                        cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls);
    76→                }
    77→            }
    78→            for (auto removed : rawIncrRemovedDecls) {
    79→                Sema::CollectRemovedMangles(removed, cachedInfo.semaInfo, cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls);
    80→            }
    81→            // NOTE: since 'declsToBeReCompiled' and 'rawIncrRemovedDecls' have been process,
    82→            // this loop will only remove the re-boxed built-in types' related decls.
    83→            for (auto typeMangle : result.reBoxedTypes) {
    84→                Sema::CollectRemovedMangles(typeMangle, cachedInfo.semaInfo, cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls);
    85→            }
    86→            break;
    87→        case IncreKind::NO_CHANGE:
    88→            cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName = std::move(result.cacheInfo.bitcodeFilesName);
    89→            break;
    90→        case IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG:
    91→            break;
    92→        case IncreKind::INVALID:
    93→            CJC_ABORT();
    94→            break;
    95→    }
    96→}
    97→
    98→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
    99→namespace {
   100→std::optional<size_t> GetCachedSplitNum(const std::string& cachedCodeGenPath)
   101→{
   102→    std::optional<size_t> splitNum{std::nullopt};
   103→    llvm::SMDiagnostic err;
   104→    auto context = llvm::LLVMContext();
   105→#ifdef _WIN32
   106→    auto tempPath = StringConvertor::NormalizeStringToUTF8(cachedCodeGenPath);
   107→    CJC_ASSERT(tempPath.has_value() && "Incorrect file name encoding.");
   108→    auto module = llvm::parseIRFile(tempPath.value(), err, context);
   109→#else
   110→    auto module = llvm::parseIRFile(cachedCodeGenPath, err, context);
   111→#endif
   112→    if (module == nullptr) {
   113→        Errorln("Illegal cached codegen info detected during incremental compilation.");
   114→        return splitNum;
   115→    }
   116→    auto splitNumMD = module->getNamedMetadata("splitNum");
   117→    for (llvm::MDNode* mdNode : splitNumMD->operands()) {
   118→        auto numMD = llvm::cast<llvm::ConstantAsMetadata>(mdNode->getOperand(0));
   119→        splitNum = llvm::cast<llvm::ConstantInt>(numMD->getValue())->getZExtValue();
   120→    }
   121→    return splitNum;
   122→}
   123→
   124→bool CheckCachedBitcode(const std::string& packageName, size_t splitNum, const GlobalOptions& globalOp)
   125→{
   126→    if (splitNum == 0) {
   127→        return false;
   128→    }
   129→    for (size_t i = 0; i < splitNum; ++i) {
   130→        std::string cachedBcPath =
   131→            globalOp.GenerateCachedPathNameForCodeGen(std::to_string(i) + '-' + packageName, "_cache.bc");
   132→        if (!FileUtil::FileExist(cachedBcPath)) {
   133→            IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   134→                "the cached bitcode file is lost." + cachedBcPath + " index " + std::to_string(i));
   135→            return false;
   136→        }
   137→    }
   138→    return true;
   139→}
   140→
   141→bool CheckCachedBitcodeInfo(const std::string& packageName, const GlobalOptions& options)
   142→{
   143→    auto cgCachePath = options.GenerateCachedPathNameForCodeGen(packageName, ".cgCache");
   144→    if (!FileUtil::FileExist(cgCachePath)) {
   145→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   146→            "load cached codegen info failed, roll back to full compilation");
   147→        return false;
   148→    }
   149→    auto splitNum = GetCachedSplitNum(cgCachePath);
   150→    if (!splitNum.has_value()) {
   151→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn("get cached split num failed, roll back to full compilation");
   152→        return false;
   153→    }
   154→    bool bcCachedGood = CheckCachedBitcode(packageName, splitNum.value(), options);
   155→    if (!bcCachedGood) {
   156→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   157→            "load cached bitcode file failed, roll back to full compilation");
   158→        return false;
   159→    }
   160→    return true;
   161→}
   162→
   163→bool CheckCachedObjFile(const GlobalOptions& options, CompilationCache& cachedInfo)
   164→{
   165→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   166→    for (const auto& fileName : cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName) {
   167→        auto objFile = options.GetHashedObjFileName(fileName) + ".o";
   168→        if (!FileUtil::FileExist(objFile)) {
   169→            logger.LogLn("cached obj file not exist, roll back to full compilation");
   170→            return false;
   171→        }
   172→    }
   173→    return true;
   174→}
   175→
   176→bool CheckCachedBitcodeInfoForLTO(const GlobalOptions& options, CompilationCache& cachedInfo)
   177→{
   178→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   179→    for (const auto& fileName : cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName) {
   180→        auto objFile = options.GetHashedObjFileName(FileUtil::GetFileNameWithoutExtension(fileName)) + ".bc";
   181→        if (!FileUtil::FileExist(objFile)) {
   182→            logger.LogLn("load cached bitcode file for opt failed, roll back to full compilation");
   183→            return false;
   184→        }
   185→    }
   186→    return true;
   187→}
   188→
   189→} // namespace
   190→#endif
   191→
   192→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformIncrementalScopeAnalysis()
   193→{
   194→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   195→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "AST Diff");
   196→    CJC_ASSERT(srcPkgs.size() == 1);
   197→    auto& package = srcPkgs[0];
   198→
   199→    // calculate the AST cache info
   200→    bool res = CalculateASTCache();
   201→    if (!res) {
   202→        return true;
   203→    }
   204→
   205→    auto& options = invocation.globalOptions;
   206→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   207→    if (!options.pluginPaths.empty()) {
   208→        kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   209→        Warningf("`--incremental-compile` is incompatible with `--plugin` and will be ignored.\n");
   210→        return true;
   211→    }
   212→#endif
   213→
   214→    if (!declsWithDuplicatedRawMangleName.empty()) {
   215→        kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   216→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   217→            "illegal source code leads to duplicated raw mangle name, roll back to full compilation");
   218→        return true;
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    auto increRes = IncrementalScopeAnalysis({rawMangleName2DeclMap, std::move(astCacheInfo), *package, options,
   222→                                                 importManager, cachedInfo, fileMap, std::move(directExtends)});
   223→    if (increRes.kind == IncreKind::INCR) {
   224→        // check cached bitcode infos
   225→        const std::string& packageName = package->fullPackageName;
   226→        bool isCachedBitcodeGood = CheckCachedBitcodeInfo(packageName, options);
   227→        if (!isCachedBitcodeGood) {
   228→            increRes.kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   229→        } else {
   230→            // set deleted mangles Name for codegen
   231→            cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.insert(
   232→                increRes.deletedMangleNames.begin(), increRes.deletedMangleNames.end());
   233→        }
   234→    }
   235→    if (increRes.kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   236→        // check cached obj file
   237→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   238→            options.UpdateCachedDirName(srcPkg->fullPackageName);
   239→        }
   240→        if (!options.IsLTOEnabled() && !CheckCachedObjFile(options, increRes.cacheInfo)) {
   241→            increRes.kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   242→        }
   243→        if (options.IsLTOEnabled() && !CheckCachedBitcodeInfoForLTO(options, increRes.cacheInfo)) {
   244→            increRes.kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   245→        }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    increRes.Dump();
   249→    SaveCompilationResult(std::move(increRes));
   250→#endif
   251→    return true;
   252→}
   253→
   254→static bool HasSimpleInitialiser(const AST::VarDecl& decl)
   255→{
   256→    auto& init = decl.initializer;
   257→    if (!init) {
   258→        return false;
   259→    }
   260→    if (init->astKind == ASTKind::LIT_CONST_EXPR) {
   261→        auto kind = StaticCast<LitConstExpr>(init.get())->kind;
   262→        return kind != LitConstKind::JSTRING && kind != LitConstKind::UNIT;
   263→    }
   264→    return false;
   265→}
   266→
   267→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformSema()
   268→{
   269→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Semantic");
   270→    if (auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance(); logger.IsEnable()) {
   271→        std::string message = kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE
   272→            ? "no change, skip sema"
   273→            : (kind == IncreKind::ROLLBACK ? "full sema" : "incremental sema");
   274→        logger.LogLn(message);
   275→    }
   276→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   277→        return true;
   278→    } else if (kind == IncreKind::ROLLBACK) {
   279→        return CompilerInstance::PerformSema();
   280→    }
   281→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(typeManager);
   282→    // Load cached types. Should only exist exactly one source package.
   283→    for (auto srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   284→        srcPkg->EnableAttr(Attribute::INCRE_COMPILE);
   285→        Sema::HandleCtorForIncr(*srcPkg, mangledName2DeclMap, cachedInfo.semaInfo);
   286→        cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.merge(importManager.LoadCachedTypeForPackage(*srcPkg, mangledName2DeclMap));
   287→    }
   288→    Sema::MarkIncrementalCheckForCtor(declsToBeReCompiled);
   289→
   290→    auto visit = [](Decl& decl) {
   291→        // NOTE: Avoid some sema rules to be rechecked.
   292→        // To guarantee the member decls will be checked, the type decl cannot be marked with following attributes.
   293→        if (!decl.IsNominalDecl() && decl.astKind != ASTKind::PROP_DECL) {
   294→            decl.EnableAttr(Attribute::IS_CHECK_VISITED, Attribute::INITIALIZED, Attribute::INITIALIZATION_CHECKED,
   295→                Attribute::INCRE_COMPILE);
   296→        }
   297→        // Remove body to avoid walker walk-in.
   298→        if (auto fd = DynamicCast<FuncDecl*>(&decl); fd && fd->funcBody) {
   299→            fd->funcBody->body.reset();
   300→            return;
   301→        }
   302→        if (auto vd = DynamicCast<VarDecl*>(&decl)) {
   303→            if (!vd->initializer) {
   304→                return;
   305→            }
   306→            vd->EnableAttr(Attribute::DEFAULT);
   307→            if (HasSimpleInitialiser(*vd)) {
   308→                vd->DisableAttr(Attribute::IS_CHECK_VISITED);
   309→            }
   310→        }
   311→        // PropDecl's getter/setter will be counted separately and should not be cleared from propDecl.
   312→    };
   313→    for (auto& [_, decl] : mangledName2DeclMap) {
   314→        if (!decl->toBeCompiled && !IsInDeclWithAttribute(*decl, Attribute::GENERIC) && Ty::IsTyCorrect(decl->ty) &&
   315→            (decl->astKind != ASTKind::FUNC_DECL || !decl->TestAttr(Attribute::DEFAULT))) {
   316→        // NOTE: for now, generic definitions and default implementations should be kept for code re-generation.
   317→            visit(*decl);
   318→        }
   319→    }
   320→    return CompilerInstance::PerformSema();
   321→}
   322→
   323→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformOverflowStrategy()
   324→{
   325→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Overflow Strategy");
   326→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   327→        return true;
   328→    }
   329→    return CompilerInstance::PerformOverflowStrategy();
   330→}
   331→
   332→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformDesugarAfterSema()
   333→{
   334→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Desugar after Sema");
   335→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   336→        return true;
   337→    }
   338→    return CompilerInstance::PerformDesugarAfterSema();
   339→}
   340→
   341→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformGenericInstantiation()
   342→{
   343→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Generic Instantiation");
   344→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   345→        return true;
   346→    }
   347→    bool ret = CompilerInstance::PerformGenericInstantiation();
   348→    if (ret) {
   349→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   350→            changedTypes.merge(Sema::CollectChangedStructTypes(*srcPkg, declsToBeReCompiled));
   351→            IterateAllExportableDecls(*srcPkg, [this](auto& decl) {
   352→                // If non-export function/variable is marked as external linkage, codegen should change its linkage.
   353→                if (!decl.IsExportedDecl() && decl.linkage == Linkage::EXTERNAL && !decl.mangledName.empty()) {
   354→                    cacheMangles.newExternalDecls.emplace(decl.mangledName);
   355→                }
   356→            });
   357→        }
   358→    }
   359→    return ret;
   360→}
   361→
   362→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformMangling()
   363→{
   364→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   365→        return true;
   366→    }
   367→    bool success = DefaultCompilerInstance::PerformMangling();
   368→    if (success) {
   369→        // mangle of full exported decl is empty in cjo, we need update it after mangling.
   370→        cacheMangles.UpdateImportedInlineDeclsMangle();
   371→    }
   372→    return success;
   373→}
   374→
   375→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::UpdateCachedInfo()
   376→{
   377→    UpdateMangleNameForCachedInfo();
   378→    UpdateCHIROptEffectMap();
   379→    if (kind == IncreKind::ROLLBACK) {
   380→        cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep = std::move(chirInfo.curVirtFuncWrapDep);
   381→        cachedInfo.ccOutFuncs = std::move(chirInfo.ccOutFuncsRawMangle);
   382→        cachedInfo.varInitDepMap = std::move(chirInfo.varInitDepMap);
   383→    } else if (kind == IncreKind::INCR) {
   384→        for (auto& [raw, _] : chirInfo.delVirtFuncWrapForIncr) {
   385→            cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep.erase(raw);
   386→        }
   387→        for (auto& [raw, warp] : chirInfo.curVirtFuncWrapDep) {
   388→            cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep[raw] = warp;
   389→        }
   390→        for (auto& rm : std::as_const(rawIncrRemovedDecls)) {
   391→            cachedInfo.varInitDepMap.erase(rm);
   392→        }
   393→        for (auto& [raw, warp] : chirInfo.varInitDepMap) {
   394→            cachedInfo.varInitDepMap[raw] = warp;
   395→        }
   396→        cachedInfo.ccOutFuncs.merge(std::move(chirInfo.ccOutFuncsRawMangle));
   397→    }
   398→    // Update usage of compiler added.
   399→    for (auto pkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   400→        Sema::CollectCompilerAddedDeclUsage(*pkg, cachedInfo.semaInfo);
   401→    }
   402→}
   403→
   404→namespace Cangjie {
   405→/// implemented in IncrementalScopeAnalysis
   406→void MergeCHIROptEffectMap(
   407→    const OptEffectStrMap& newMap, OptEffectStrMap& lastCachedMap, const RawMangled2DeclMap& rawMangled2Decl);
   408→void DeleteRemovedNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(const std::list<std::string>& removedDecls, OptEffectStrMap& effectMap);
   409→void DeleteRecompiledNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(
   410→    const std::unordered_set<Ptr<AST::Decl>>& recompiledNodes, OptEffectStrMap& effectMap);
   411→}
   412→
   413→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::UpdateCHIROptEffectMap()
   414→{
   415→    DeleteRemovedNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(rawIncrRemovedDecls, cachedInfo.chirOptInfo);
   416→    DeleteRecompiledNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(declsToBeReCompiled, cachedInfo.chirOptInfo);
   417→
   418→    MergeCHIROptEffectMap(chirInfo.optEffectMap, cachedInfo.chirOptInfo, rawMangleName2DeclMap);
   419→}
   420→
   421→namespace {
   422→void UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVirtualFuncDep(CachedMangleMap& cacheMangles, std::list<std::string>& rawIncrRemovedDecls,
   423→    VirtualWrapperDepMap& virtualFuncDep, VirtualWrapperDepMap& delVirtFuncWrapForIncr)
   424→{
   425→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   426→    for (auto& delRaw : rawIncrRemovedDecls) {
   427→        if (auto it = virtualFuncDep.find(delRaw); it != virtualFuncDep.end()) {
   428→            logger.LogLn("[delVirDep][remove] raw: " + delRaw + " mg: " + it->second);
   429→            cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace(it->second);
   430→        }
   431→    }
   432→    for (auto& [delRaw, del] : delVirtFuncWrapForIncr) {
   433→        logger.LogLn("[delVirDep][change] raw: " + delRaw + " mg: " + del);
   434→        cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace(del);
   435→    }
   436→}
   437→void UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVarInitDep(CachedMangleMap& cacheMangles, std::list<std::string>& rawIncrRemovedDecls,
   438→    VarInitDepMap& varInitDepMap)
   439→{
   440→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   441→    for (auto& delRaw : std::as_const(rawIncrRemovedDecls)) {
   442→        if (auto it = varInitDepMap.find(delRaw); it != varInitDepMap.end()) {
   443→            logger.LogLn("[delVarInitDep][remove] raw: " + delRaw + " mg: " + it->second);
   444→            cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace(it->second);
   445→        }
   446→    }
   447→}
   448→} // namespace
   449→
   450→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCHIRCompilation()
   451→{
   452→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "CHIR");
   453→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   454→        return true;
   455→    }
   456→    auto ret = CompilerInstance::PerformCHIRCompilation();
   457→    for (auto ty : chirInfo.ccTys) {
   458→        changedTypes.insert(ty);
   459→    }
   460→    if (kind == IncreKind::INCR) {
   461→        UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVirtualFuncDep(cacheMangles, rawIncrRemovedDecls, cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep,
   462→            chirInfo.delVirtFuncWrapForIncr);
   463→        UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVarInitDep(cacheMangles, rawIncrRemovedDecls, cachedInfo.varInitDepMap);
   464→    }
   465→    return ret;
   466→}
   467→
   468→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease()
   469→{
   470→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Release AST");
   471→
   472→    // Always extract CodeGen metadata before potential release.
   473→    PrepareCodeGenInfo();
   474→
   475→    // For NO_CHANGE / EMPTY_PKG, no AST was built — nothing to release.
   476→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   477→        return true;
   478→    }
   479→
   480→    // Save results before AST is freed (ADR-009, F-02).
   481→    // PerformResultsSaving needs srcPkgs for ExportASTSignature and SaveCjo.
   482→    if (!resultsSaved) {
   483→        if (!PerformResultsSaving()) {
   484→            return false;  // Propagate save failure to abort compilation.
   485→        }
   486→        resultsSaved = true;
   487→    }
   488→
   489→    // Write incremental compilation cache before AST is freed (ADR-009).
   490→    if (ShouldWriteCacheFile() && !cacheWritten) {
   491→        UpdateCachedInfo();
   492→        WriteCachedInfo();
   493→        cacheWritten = true;
   494→    }
   495→
   496→    // Allow skipping AST release for debugging (e.g., ASan leak analysis).
   497→    if (invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST) {
   498→        return true;
   499→    }
   500→
   501→    // Clean incremental-compilation-specific AST pointers.
   502→    changedTypes.clear();
   503→    declsToBeReCompiled.clear();
   504→    cacheMangles.Clear();
   505→
   506→    // Delegate to base class for the 5-phase cleanup.
   507→    ReleaseASTMemory();
   508→    return true;
   509→}
   510→
   511→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::LoadCachedCodegenResult() const
   512→{
   513→    for (auto fileName : cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName) {
   514→        auto cachePath = invocation.globalOptions.GenerateCachedPathNameForCodeGen(fileName, ".bc");
   515→        TempFileInfo bcFileInfo = TempFileInfo{fileName, cachePath, "", true};
   516→        invocation.globalOptions.frontendOutputFiles.emplace_back(bcFileInfo);
   517→    }
   518→}
   519→
   520→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCodeGen()
   521→{
   522→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "CodeGen");
   523→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   524→        // Use codeGenPkgInfos if AST is released, otherwise use srcPkgs.
   525→        if (IsASTReleased()) {
   526→            for (auto& info : codeGenPkgInfos) {
   527→                LoadCachedCodegenResult();
   528→                invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(info.fullPackageName);
   529→            }
   530→        } else {
   531→            for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   532→                LoadCachedCodegenResult();
   533→                invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(srcPkg->fullPackageName);
   534→            }
   535→        }
   536→        return true;
   537→    }
   538→    // Before CodeGen, the dependency relationship of a package contains only some packages.
   539→    // So this function rearranges the dependencies of all packages.
   540→    RearrangeImportedPackageDependence();
   541→    bool ret = true;
   542→    if (IsASTReleased()) {
   543→        for (auto& info : codeGenPkgInfos) {
   544→            ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(info.fullPackageName, info.isEmpty, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   545→        }
   546→    } else {
   547→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   548→            ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(*srcPkg, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   549→        }
   550→    }
   551→    return ret;
   552→}
   553→
   554→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCjoSaving()
   555→{
   556→    if (auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance(); logger.IsEnable()) {
   557→        std::string message;
   558→        if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   559→            message = "no change, skip cjo saving";
   560→        } else if (kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   561→            message = "empty pkg, skip cjo saving";
   562→        } else if (invocation.globalOptions.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR) {
   563→            message = " chir output mode, skip cjo saving";
   564→        } else {
   565→            message = "incremental cjo saving";
   566→        }
   567→        logger.LogLn(message);
   568→    }
   569→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   570→        return true;
   571→    }
   572→
   573→    return DefaultCompilerInstance::PerformCjoSaving();
   574→}
   575→
   576→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformResultsSaving()
   577→{
   578→    if (resultsSaved) {
   579→        return true;
   580→    }
   581→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Save results");
   582→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   583→        return true;
   584→    }
   585→    bool ret = true;
   586→    for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   587→        if (invocation.globalOptions.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR) {
   588→            ret = ret && SaveCjo(*srcPkg);
   589→        }
   590→        if (ret && !srcPkg->IsEmpty()) {
   591→            // Write astData for incremental compilation in cache path.
   592→            std::string cachedCjo =
   593→                invocation.globalOptions.GenerateCachedPathName(srcPkg->fullPackageName, SERIALIZED_FILE_EXTENSION);
   594→            ret = ret && FileUtil::WriteBufferToASTFile(cachedCjo, importManager.ExportASTSignature(*srcPkg));
   595→        }
   596→    }
   597→    return ret;
   598→}
```

    43→
    44→enum class DepType { DIRECT, INDIRECT, BOTH };
    45→
    46→/**
    47→ * ImportManager is used to manage all imported packages. It can do these things:
    48→ * 1. Load a saved package to a @see PackageDecl node using deserialization method.
    49→ * 2. Export external decls in current package AST using serialization method.
    50→ * 3. Manage all imported packages.
    51→ * 4. Merge ASTs from source files into one Package AST and generate file-realImports Map based on source file asts.
    52→ * 5. Provide methods for decl lookup in sema.
    53→ */
    54→class ImportManager {
    55→public:
    56→    explicit ImportManager(DiagnosticEngine& d, TypeManager& typeManager, const GlobalOptions& opts)
    57→        : diag(d), opts(opts), typeManager(typeManager)
    58→    {
    59→        cjoManager = MakeOwned<CjoManager>(CjoManager::Config{diag, typeManager, opts, importSrcCode});
    60→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(cjoManager);
    61→        dependencyGraph = MakeOwned<DependencyGraph>(*cjoManager);
    62→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(dependencyGraph);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    ~ImportManager();

```
     1→// Copyright (c) Huawei Technologies Co., Ltd. 2025. All rights reserved.
     2→// This source file is part of the Cangjie project, licensed under Apache-2.0
     3→// with Runtime Library Exception.
     4→//
     5→// See https://cangjie-lang.cn/pages/LICENSE for license information.
     6→
     7→/**
     8→ * @file
     9→ *
    10→ * This file implements the CjoManager related classes.
    11→ */
    12→
    13→#include "cangjie/Modules/CjoManager.h"
    14→
    15→#include <queue>
    16→
    17→#include "CjoManagerImpl.h"
    18→#include "cangjie/AST/ASTCasting.h"
    19→#include "cangjie/AST/Utils.h"
    20→#include "cangjie/AST/Walker.h"
    21→#include "cangjie/Modules/ASTSerialization.h"
    22→#include "cangjie/Modules/ModulesUtils.h"
    23→
    24→using namespace Cangjie;
    25→using namespace AST;
    26→
    27→namespace Cangjie {
    28→namespace {
    29→void AddDeclToMap(Decl& decl, std::map<std::string, OrderedDeclSet>& declMap)
    30→{
    31→    if (decl.astKind == ASTKind::EXTEND_DECL) {
    32→        return; // ExtendDecl cannot be referenced by name.
    33→    }
    34→    if (auto vpd = DynamicCast<VarWithPatternDecl*>(&decl); vpd) {
    35→        // A VarWithPatternDecl is viewed as a collection of VarDecls.
    36→        Walker walker(vpd->irrefutablePattern.get(), [&declMap](Ptr<Node> node) {
    37→            if (auto vd = DynamicCast<VarDecl>(node)) {
    38→                declMap[vd->identifier].emplace(vd);
    39→            }
    40→            return VisitAction::WALK_CHILDREN;
    41→        });
    42→        walker.Walk();
    43→    } else if (auto funcDecl = DynamicCast<FuncDecl*>(&decl);
    44→        funcDecl == nullptr || (!funcDecl->TestAttr(Attribute::MAIN_ENTRY) && funcDecl->identifier != MAIN_INVOKE)) {
    45→        // Main function won't be imported.
    46→        declMap[decl.identifier].emplace(&decl);
    47→    }
    48→}
    49→
    50→bool CanInline(const GlobalOptions& opts)
    51→{
    52→    return opts.chirLLVM && opts.optimizationLevel > GlobalOptions::OptimizationLevel::O1 && !opts.enableCompileTest &&
    53→        !opts.enableHotReload;
    54→}
    55→} // namespace
    56→
    57→CjoManager::CjoManager(const CjoManager::Config& config) : impl{new CjoManagerImpl{config}}
    58→{
    59→}
    60→
    61→CjoManager::~CjoManager()
    62→{
    63→    DeleteASTLoaders();
    64→    delete impl;
    65→}
    66→
    67→void CjoManager::DeleteASTLoaders() const noexcept
    68→{
    69→    for (auto& p : impl->GetPackageNameMap()) {
    70→        delete p.second->loader.get();
    71→        p.second->loader = nullptr;
    72→    }
    73→}
    74→
    75→CjoManagerImpl::CjoManagerImpl(const CjoManager::Config& config)
    76→    : diag(config.diag),
    77→      typeManager(config.typeManager),
    78→      globalOptions(config.globalOptions),
    79→      importSrcCode(config.importSrcCode),
    80→      canInline(CanInline(config.globalOptions))
    81→{
    82→}
    83→
    84→Ptr<CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo> CjoManagerImpl::GetPackageInfo(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
    85→{
    86→    auto iter = packageNameMap.find(fullPackageName);
    87→    if (iter != packageNameMap.cend()) {
    88→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(iter->second);
    89→        return iter->second.get();
    90→    }
    91→    return nullptr;
    92→}
    93→
    94→bool CjoManager::IsOnlyUsedByMacro(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
    95→{
    96→    auto info = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
    97→    return info ? info->onlyUsedByMacro : false;
    98→}
    99→
   100→void CjoManager::SetOnlyUsedByMacro(const std::string& fullPackageName, bool onlyUsedByMacro) const
   101→{
   102→    auto info = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
   103→    if (info != nullptr) {
   104→        info->onlyUsedByMacro = onlyUsedByMacro;
   105→    }
   106→}
   107→
   108→bool CjoManager::IsMacroRelatedPackageName(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   109→{
   110→    auto info = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
   111→    return info != nullptr ? info->onlyUsedByMacro : false;
   112→}
   113→
   114→void CjoManager::UpdateSearchPath(const std::string& cangjieModules) const
   115→{

   117→}

   125→{

   128→
   129→void CjoManager::SetPackageCjoCache(
   130→    const std::string& fullPackageName, const std::vector<uint8_t>& cjoData, CjoChangeState changeState) const
   131→{

   133→}
   134→

   136→{
   137→    impl->ClearCjoCache();
   138→}
   139→
   140→void CjoManager::ClearVisitedPkgs() const
   141→{
   142→    impl->ClearVisitedPkgs();

   154→

   164→
   165→Ptr<std::unordered_map<std::string, Ptr<AST::Decl>>> CjoManager::GetExportIdDeclMap(
   166→    const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   167→{

   169→}
   170→
   171→std::vector<OwnedPtr<ASTLoader>>& CjoManager::GetCommonPartCjos(std::string packageName) const
   172→{
   173→    return impl->GetCommonPartCjos(packageName, *this);
   174→}
   175→
   176→Ptr<PackageDecl> CjoManager::GetPackageDecl(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   177→{
   178→    auto info = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
   179→    if (info == nullptr) {
   180→        return nullptr;
   181→    }
   182→    return info->pkgDecl.get();
   183→}
   184→
   185→Ptr<Package> CjoManager::GetPackage(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   186→{
   187→    auto info = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
   188→    if (info == nullptr) {
   189→        return nullptr;
   190→    }
   191→    return info->pkg.get();
   192→}
   193→
   194→std::string CjoManager::GetPackageDepInfo(const std::string& cjoPath) const
   195→{
   196→    auto loader = impl->ReadCjo("", cjoPath, *this);
   197→    if (loader == nullptr) {
   198→        return "";
   199→    }
   200→    return loader->LoadPackageDepInfo();
   201→}
   202→
   203→Ptr<std::unordered_map<std::string, Ptr<AST::Decl>>> CjoManagerImpl::GetExportIdDeclMap(
   204→    const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   205→{
   206→    auto iter = packageNameMap.find(fullPackageName);
   207→    if (iter != packageNameMap.cend()) {
   208→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(iter->second);
   209→        return &iter->second->exportIDDeclMap;
   210→    }
   211→    return nullptr;
   212→}
   213→
   214→const std::map<std::string, OrderedDeclSet>& CjoManager::GetPackageMembers(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   215→{
   216→    const static std::map<std::string, OrderedDeclSet> EMPTY_MAP;
   217→    auto iter = impl->GetPackageNameMap().find(fullPackageName);
   218→    if (iter != impl->GetPackageNameMap().cend()) {
   219→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(iter->second);
   220→        return iter->second->declMap;
   221→    }
   222→    return EMPTY_MAP;
   223→}
   224→
   225→const OrderedDeclSet& CjoManager::GetPackageMembersByName(
   226→    const std::string& fullPackageName, const std::string& name) const
   227→{
   228→    const static OrderedDeclSet EMPTY_DECLS;
   229→    auto& declMap = GetPackageMembers(fullPackageName);
   230→    auto iter = declMap.find(name);
   231→    if (iter != declMap.cend()) {
   232→        return iter->second;
   233→    }
   234→    return EMPTY_DECLS;
   235→}
   236→
   237→Ptr<Decl> CjoManager::GetImplicitPackageMembersByName(const std::string& fullPackageName, const std::string& name) const
   238→{
   239→    auto info = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
   240→    if (!info) {
   241→        return nullptr;
   242→    }
   243→    auto found = info->implicitDeclMap.find(name);
   244→    return found == info->implicitDeclMap.end() ? nullptr : found->second;
   245→}
   246→
   247→bool CjoManager::LoadPackageHeader(const std::string& fullPackageName, const std::string& cjoPath) const
   248→{
   249→    auto iter = impl->GetPackageNameMap().find(fullPackageName);
   250→    if (iter != impl->GetPackageNameMap().cend()) {
   251→        return true;
   252→    }
   253→    auto loader = impl->ReadCjo(fullPackageName, cjoPath, *this);
   254→    if (loader == nullptr) {
   255→        return false;
   256→    }
   257→    auto pkg = loader->LoadPackageDependencies();
   258→    if (pkg == nullptr) {
   259→        return false;
   260→    }
   261→    auto pkgInfo = MakeOwned<CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo>(CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo(
   262→        {.loader = loader.release(), .pkg = pkg.get(), .pkgDecl = MakeOwned<PackageDecl>(*pkg)}));
   263→    impl->AddImportedPackages(pkg);
   264→    impl->GetPackageNameMap().emplace(fullPackageName, std::move(pkgInfo));
   265→    return true;
   266→}
   267→
   268→bool CjoManagerImpl::IsReExportBy(const std::string& srcPackage, const std::string& reExportPackage) const
   269→{
   270→    auto info = GetPackageInfo(srcPackage);
   271→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(info);
   272→    for (auto& file : info->pkg->files) {
   273→        for (auto& importSpec : file->imports) {
   274→            if (!importSpec->IsReExport()) {
   275→                continue;
   276→            }
   277→            auto found = importedPackageNameMap.find(importSpec.get());
   278→            if (found != importedPackageNameMap.end() && found->second.first == reExportPackage) {
   279→                return true;
   280→            }
   281→        }
   282→    }
   283→    return false;
   284→}
   285→
   286→bool CjoManager::NeedCollectDependency(const std::string& curName, bool isCurMacro, const std::string& depName) const
   287→{
   288→    if (depName == curName || impl->AlreadyLoaded(depName)) {
   289→        return false;
   290→    }
   291→
   292→    // If current is macro package, only load decls for dependent macro package,
   293→    // otherwise, load decls for all dependent package (macro package was filtered before).
   294→    // NOTE: non-macro package's will never be used through macro package.
   295→    if (auto depPd = GetPackageDecl(depName); depPd) {
   296→        bool isDepMacro = depPd->srcPackage->isMacroPackage;
   297→        if (!isCurMacro || isDepMacro || depName == AST_PACKAGE_NAME || impl->IsReExportBy(curName, depName)) {
   298→            return true;
   299→        }
   300→    }
   301→
   302→    return false;
   303→}
   304→
   305→bool CjoManager::LoadFilesOfCommonPart(Ptr<Package> pkg)
   306→{
   307→    if (!impl->GetGlobalOptions().IsCompilingCJMPSpecific() && impl->GetGlobalOptions().commonPartCjos.empty()) {
   308→        return true;
   309→    }
   310→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(pkg);
   311→    // Remove existing isCommon files from pkg before loading new common part for lsp incremental compilation.
   312→    Utils::EraseIf(pkg->files, [](const auto& file) { return file->TestAttr(Attribute::FROM_COMMON_PART); });
   313→    for (Ptr<ASTLoader> commonLoader : GetCommonPartCjos(pkg->fullPackageName)) {
   314→        if (!commonLoader->PreloadCommonPartOfPackage(*pkg)) {
   315→            return false;
   316→        }
   317→    }
   318→    return true;
   319→}
   320→
   321→void CjoManager::LoadPackageDeclsOnDemand(const std::vector<Ptr<Package>>& packages, bool fromLsp) const
   322→{
   323→    // Add all directly imported package's loader.
   324→    std::queue<Ptr<CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo>> q;
   325→    for (auto pkg : packages) {
   326→        if (fromLsp) {
   327→            q.push(impl->GetPackageInfo(pkg->fullPackageName));
   328→        }
   329→        for (auto& file : pkg->files) {
   330→            for (auto& import : file->imports) {
   331→                auto pkgName = GetPackageNameByImport(*import);
   332→                if (!pkgName.empty()) {
   333→                    q.push(impl->GetPackageInfo(pkgName));
   334→                }
   335→            }
   336→        }
   337→    }
   338→
   339→    std::vector<Ptr<ASTLoader>> loaders;
   340→    loaders.reserve(q.size());
   341→    // Load common part cjo
   342→    for (auto pkg : packages) {
   343→        if (impl->GetGlobalOptions().IsCompilingCJMPSpecific() || !impl->GetGlobalOptions().commonPartCjos.empty()) {
   344→            std::string expectedPackageName = pkg->fullPackageName;
   345→            for (Ptr<ASTLoader> commonLoader : GetCommonPartCjos(expectedPackageName)) {
   346→                commonLoader->LoadPackageDecls();
   347→                loaders.emplace_back(commonLoader);
   348→            }
   349→        }
   350→    }
   351→
   352→    while (!q.empty()) {
   353→        auto cur = q.front();
   354→        q.pop();
   355→        if (cur == nullptr || cur->loader == nullptr) {
   356→            continue; // If any error happens during loading 'cjo', the loader will be null.
   357→        }
   358→        const auto& pkgName = cur->loader->GetImportedPackageName();
   359→        if (auto [_, success] = impl->AddLoadedPackages(pkgName); !success) {
   360→            continue;
   361→        }
   362→        loaders.emplace_back(cur->loader);
   363→        cur->loader->LoadPackageDecls();
   364→        bool isCurMacro = cur->pkg->isMacroPackage;
   365→        const auto& deps = cur->loader->GetDependentPackageNames();
   366→        for (const auto& pkg : deps) {
   367→            if (NeedCollectDependency(pkgName, isCurMacro, pkg)) {
   368→                q.push(impl->GetPackageInfo(pkg));
   369→            }
   370→        }
   371→    }
   372→
   373→    for (auto loader : loaders) {
   374→        loader->LoadRefs();
   375→    }
   376→
   377→    // Node's ty may reference TypeAliasTy from imported package, need to substitute them to real type.
   378→    // It must be done after all type references are loaded.
   379→    impl->SubstituteImportedTypeAliasTy(packages);
   380→}
   381→
   382→void CjoManager::LoadAllDeclsAndRefs() const
   383→{
   384→    // 'packageNameMap' also contains source package, we only need to load for imported package.
   385→    for (auto& p : impl->GetPackageNameMap()) {
   386→        auto& pkgInfo = p.second;
   387→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(pkgInfo);
   388→        if (pkgInfo->loader) {
   389→            pkgInfo->loader->LoadPackageDecls();
   390→        }
   391→    }
   392→    for (auto& p : impl->GetPackageNameMap()) {
   393→        if (p.second->loader) {
   394→            p.second->loader->LoadRefs();
   395→        }
   396→    }
   397→}
   398→
   399→void CjoManagerImpl::SubstituteImportedTypeAliasTy(const std::vector<Ptr<Package>>& srcPackages)
   400→{
   401→    auto replaceAliasUseTy = [this](Ptr<Node> node) {
   402→        if (node->astKind == ASTKind::TYPE_ALIAS_DECL) {
   403→            return VisitAction::WALK_CHILDREN;
   404→        }
   405→        if (node->IsDecl() || Is<FuncBody>(node)) {
   406→            node->ty = typeManager.SubstituteTypeAliasInTy(*node->ty);
   407→        } else if (auto type = DynamicCast<Type>(node); type && !Ty::IsInitialTy(type->aliasTy)) {
   408→            type->ty = typeManager.SubstituteTypeAliasInTy(*type->ty);
   409→        }
   410→        return VisitAction::WALK_CHILDREN;
   411→    };
   412→    for (auto& pkgName2PkgInfo : GetPackageNameMap()) {
   413→        // For cjlint tool could have more than one src-package.
   414→        bool isSrcPackage = Utils::In(srcPackages,
   415→            [&pkgName2PkgInfo](Ptr<Package> pkg) { return pkg->fullPackageName == pkgName2PkgInfo.first; });
   416→        if (isSrcPackage && globalOptions.commonPartCjos.size() == 0) {
   417→            continue;
   418→        }
   419→        auto& pkgInfo = pkgName2PkgInfo.second;
   420→        for (auto& file : pkgInfo->pkg->files) {
   421→            // For compile platform part, need only substitute type alias in common part files.
   422→            if (isSrcPackage && !file->TestAttr(Attribute::FROM_COMMON_PART)) {
   423→                continue;
   424→            }
   425→            Walker(file.get(), replaceAliasUseTy).Walk();
   426→        }
   427→    }
   428→}
   429→
   430→std::vector<OwnedPtr<ASTLoader>>& CjoManagerImpl::GetCommonPartCjos(
   431→    std::string packageName, const CjoManager& cjoManager)
   432→{
   433→    if (commonPartLoaders.empty()) {
   434→        if (globalOptions.commonPartCjos.empty()) {
   435→            diag.DiagnoseRefactor(DiagKindRefactor::module_common_part_path_is_required, DEFAULT_POSITION);
   436→        }
   437→        for (auto commonPartCjo : globalOptions.commonPartCjos) {
   438→            commonPartLoaders.emplace_back(ReadCjo(packageName, commonPartCjo, cjoManager));
   439→        }
   440→    }
   441→
   442→    return commonPartLoaders;
   443→}
   444→
   445→OwnedPtr<ASTLoader> CjoManagerImpl::ReadCjo(
   446→    const std::string& fullPackageName, const std::string& cjoPath, const CjoManager& cjoManager, bool printErr) const
   447→{
   448→    std::vector<uint8_t> buffer;
   449→    if (auto found = cjoFileCacheMap.find(fullPackageName); found != cjoFileCacheMap.end()) {
   450→        buffer = found->second.data;
   451→    } else {
   452→        std::string failedReason;
   453→        FileUtil::ReadBinaryFileToBuffer(cjoPath, buffer, failedReason);
   454→        if (printErr && !failedReason.empty()) {
   455→            diag.DiagnoseRefactor(
   456→                DiagKindRefactor::module_read_file_to_buffer_failed, DEFAULT_POSITION, cjoPath, failedReason);
   457→            return nullptr;
   458→        }
   459→    }
   460→    auto loader = MakeOwned<ASTLoader>(std::move(buffer), fullPackageName, typeManager, cjoManager, globalOptions);
   461→    loader->SetImportSourceCode(importSrcCode);
   462→    return loader;
   463→}
   464→
   465→std::unordered_set<std::string> CjoManager::LoadCachedPackage(const AST::Package& pkg, const std::string& cjoPath,
   466→    const std::map<std::string, Ptr<AST::Decl>>& mangledName2DeclMap) const
   467→{
   468→    auto loader = impl->ReadCjo(pkg.fullPackageName, cjoPath, *this, false);
   469→    if (loader == nullptr) {
   470→        return {};
   471→    }
   472→    return loader->LoadCachedTypeForPackage(pkg, mangledName2DeclMap);
   473→}
   474→
   475→void CjoManager::AddSourcePackage(AST::Package& pkg) const
   476→{
   477→    auto pkgInfo = MakeOwned<CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo>(
   478→        CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo({.pkg = &pkg, .pkgDecl = MakeOwned<PackageDecl>(pkg)}));
   479→    impl->GetPackageNameMap().emplace(pkg.fullPackageName, std::move(pkgInfo));
   480→}
   481→
   482→void CjoManager::AddImportedPackageFromASTNode(OwnedPtr<AST::Package>&& pkg) const
   483→{
   484→    auto pkgInfo = MakeOwned<CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo>(
   485→        CjoManagerImpl::PackageInfo({.pkg = pkg.get(), .pkgDecl = MakeOwned<PackageDecl>(*pkg)}));
   486→    impl->GetPackageNameMap().emplace(pkg->fullPackageName, std::move(pkgInfo));
   487→    pkg->EnableAttr(Attribute::TOOL_ADD);
   488→    impl->AddImportedPackages(pkg);
   489→}
   490→
   491→void CjoManagerImpl::AddImportsToMap(
   492→    const ImportSpec& import, const std::string& importedPackage, std::map<std::string, OrderedDeclSet>& declMap) const
   493→{
   494→    auto pkgInfo = GetPackageInfo(importedPackage);
   495→    if (!pkgInfo) {
   496→        return; // Failed to load current package.
   497→    }
   498→    auto importLevel = GetAccessLevel(import);
   499→    if (import.content.kind == ImportKind::IMPORT_ALL) {
   500→        for (auto& [name, decls] : pkgInfo->declMap) {
   501→            auto& targetMap = declMap[name];
   502→            Modules::AddImportedDeclToMap(decls, targetMap, importLevel);
   503→        }
   504→        return;
   505→    }
   506→    auto& decls = pkgInfo->declMap[import.content.identifier];
   507→    if (import.content.kind == ImportKind::IMPORT_SINGLE) {
   508→        auto& targetMap = declMap[import.content.identifier];
   509→        Modules::AddImportedDeclToMap(decls, targetMap, importLevel);
   510→    } else if (import.content.kind == ImportKind::IMPORT_ALIAS) {
   511→        auto& targetMap = declMap[import.content.aliasName];
   512→        Modules::AddImportedDeclToMap(decls, targetMap, importLevel);
   513→    }
   514→}
   515→
   516→void CjoManager::AddPackageDeclMap(const std::string& fullPackageName, const std::string& importedPackage)
   517→{
   518→    auto pkgInfo = impl->GetPackageInfo(fullPackageName);
   519→    // Failed to load current package or already collect the decls.
   520→    if (!pkgInfo || impl->IsVisitedPackage(fullPackageName)) {
   521→        return;
   522→    }
   523→    impl->AddVisitedPackage(fullPackageName);
   524→    auto relation = importedPackage.empty() ? Modules::PackageRelation::CHILD
   525→                                            : Modules::GetPackageRelation(importedPackage, fullPackageName);
   526→    for (auto& file : pkgInfo->pkg->files) {
   527→        // For imported package, 'file->decls' will only contains public decls.
   528→        for (auto& decl : file->decls) {
   529→            if (decl->astKind == ASTKind::MACRO_EXPAND_DECL) {
   530→                continue; // Macro expand decl cannot be reference.
   531→            }
   532→            AddDeclToMap(*decl, pkgInfo->declMap);
   533→        }
   534→        for (auto& decl : file->exportedInternalDecls) {
   535→            if (decl->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPLICIT_USED)) {
   536→                pkgInfo->implicitDeclMap.emplace(decl->identifier, decl.get());
   537→            }
   538→        }
   539→    }
   540→    for (auto& file : pkgInfo->pkg->files) {
   541→        for (auto& import : file->imports) {
   542→            if (import->IsImportMulti()) {
   543→                continue;
   544→            }
   545→            auto pkgName = GetPackageNameByImport(*import);
   546→            if (pkgName.empty()) {
   547→                continue;
   548→            }
   549→            AddPackageDeclMap(pkgName, fullPackageName);
   550→            if (import->IsReExport() && Modules::IsVisible(*import, relation)) {
   551→                impl->AddImportsToMap(*import, pkgName, pkgInfo->declMap);
   552→            }
   553→        }
   554→    }
   555→}
   556→
   557→std::string CjoManager::GetPackageCjoPath(const std::string& fullPackageName) const
   558→{
   559→    if (auto found = impl->GetCjoFileCacheMap().find(fullPackageName); found != impl->GetCjoFileCacheMap().end()) {
   560→        return fullPackageName; // Set dummy path for cached cjo data.
   561→    }
   562→    std::string cjoPath = "";
   563→    if (impl->GetCjoPathFromFindCache(fullPackageName, cjoPath)) {
   564→        return cjoPath;
   565→    }
   566→    cjoPath = FileUtil::FindSerializationFile(fullPackageName, SERIALIZED_FILE_EXTENSION, GetSearchPath());
   567→    impl->CacheCjoPathForFind(fullPackageName, cjoPath);
   568→    return cjoPath;
   569→}
   570→
   571→std::pair<std::string, std::string> CjoManager::GetPackageCjo(const AST::ImportSpec& importSpec) const
   572→{
   573→    std::string cjoPath;
   574→    std::string cjoName;
   575→    for (auto it : GetPossibleCjoNames(importSpec)) {
   576→        cjoName = it;
   577→        if (auto found = impl->GetCjoFileCacheMap().find(FileUtil::ToPackageName(cjoName));
   578→            found != impl->GetCjoFileCacheMap().end()) {
   579→            cjoPath = cjoName; // Set dummy path for cached cjo data.
   580→        } else {
   581→            cjoPath = FileUtil::FindSerializationFile(
   582→                FileUtil::ToPackageName(cjoName), SERIALIZED_FILE_EXTENSION, GetSearchPath());
   583→        }
   584→        if (!cjoPath.empty()) {
   585→            break;
   586→        }
   587→    }
   588→    CJC_ASSERT(!cjoName.empty());
   589→    auto cjoPackageName = FileUtil::ToPackageName(cjoName);
   590→    // Store importSpec with packageName.
   591→    std::string possibleName = importSpec.content.GetImportedPackageName();
   592→    impl->AddImportedPackageName(&importSpec,
   593→        std::make_pair(
   594→            cjoPackageName, cjoPackageName == possibleName && importSpec.content.kind != ImportKind::IMPORT_ALL));
   595→    return {cjoPackageName, cjoPath};
   596→}
   597→
   598→std::vector<std::string> CjoManager::GetPossibleCjoNames(const ImportSpec& import) const
   599→{
   600→    // Multi-imports are desugared after parser which should not be used for get package name.
   601→    CJC_ASSERT(import.content.kind != ImportKind::IMPORT_MULTI);
   602→    if (auto it = GetPackageNameByImport(import); !it.empty()) {
   603→        return {FileUtil::ToCjoFileName(it)};
   604→    }
   605→    std::vector<std::string> possibleNames;
   606→    for (auto& name : import.content.GetPossiblePackageNames()) {
   607→        possibleNames.emplace_back(FileUtil::ToCjoFileName(name));
   608→    }
   609→    return possibleNames;
   610→}
   611→
   612→std::string CjoManager::GetPackageNameByImport(const AST::ImportSpec& importSpec) const
   613→{
   614→    return impl->GetPackageNameByImport(importSpec);
   615→}
   616→
   617→bool CjoManager::IsImportPackage(const AST::ImportSpec& importSpec) const
   618→{
   619→    return impl->IsImportPackage(importSpec);
   620→}
   621→
   622→std::vector<Ptr<AST::PackageDecl>> CjoManager::GetAllPackageDecls(bool includeMacroPkg) const
   623→{
   624→    std::vector<Ptr<AST::PackageDecl>> ret;
   625→    for (auto& p : impl->GetPackageNameMap()) {
   626→        auto& pkgInfo = p.second;
   627→        CJC_ASSERT(pkgInfo && pkgInfo->pkgDecl);
   628→        // Temporarily contains source package to keep same implementation as before.
   629→        if (!pkgInfo->pkg->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPORTED) || includeMacroPkg ||
   630→            (!pkgInfo->onlyUsedByMacro && !pkgInfo->pkg->isMacroPackage)) {
   631→            ret.emplace_back(pkgInfo->pkgDecl.get());
   632→        }
   633→    }
   634→    return ret;
   635→}
   636→
   637→void CjoManager::RemovePackage(const std::string& fullPkgName, const Ptr<Package> package) const
   638→{
   639→    impl->RemoveImportedPackages(package);
   640→    if (auto found = impl->GetPackageNameMap().find(fullPkgName); found != impl->GetPackageNameMap().end()) {
   641→        delete found->second->loader.get();
   642→        found->second->loader = nullptr;
   643→        impl->GetPackageNameMap().erase(fullPkgName);
   644→    }
   645→}
   646→
   647→void CjoManager::ClearImportedPackages() const
   648→{
   649→    // Release ownership of imported AST packages to reclaim memory.
   650→    impl->GetImportedPackages().clear();
   651→    // Clear all AST pointer fields in PackageInfo to eliminate dangling references.
   652→    // After importedPackages.clear(), the AST::Package objects are destroyed, so
   653→    // pkg, pkgDecl, exportIDDeclMap, declMap, implicitDeclMap all become dangling.
   654→    for (auto& [name, info] : impl->GetPackageNameMap()) {
   655→        info->pkg = nullptr;
   656→        info->pkgDecl.reset();
   657→        info->exportIDDeclMap.clear();
   658→        info->declMap.clear();
   659→        info->implicitDeclMap.clear();
   660→    }
   661→}
   662→
   663→void CjoManagerImpl::ClearForReBuildIndex()
   664→{
   665→    // Delete all AST loaders first
   666→    for (auto& p : packageNameMap) {
   667→        delete p.second->loader.get();
   668→        p.second->loader = nullptr;
   669→    }
   670→    // Clear all package-related maps and caches
   671→    packageNameMap.clear();
   672→    importedPackageNameMap.clear();
   673→    visitedPkgs.clear();
   674→    loadedPackages.clear();
   675→    importedPackages.clear();
   676→    // Reset BuildIndex flag
   677→    hasBuildIndex = false;
   678→    // Don't clear cjoFileCacheMap and cjoPathCache, because they are used for rebuild index.
   679→}
   680→} // namespace Cangjie
   681→
```

</details>

     7→/**
     8→ * @file ASTReleaseFunctionalTest.cpp
     9→ *
    10→ * Comprehensive functional tests for the AST memory release feature.
    11→ *
    12→ * Test coverage:
    13→ *   1. PerformASTRelease pipeline stage behavior
    14→ *   2. ReleaseASTMemory 5-phase cleanup correctness
    15→ *   3. PrepareCodeGenInfo metadata extraction
    16→ *   4. CodeGen dual-path (with/without AST)
    17→ *   5. --no-release-ast debug flag
    18→ *   6. Idempotency and guard flags (astReleased, resultsSaved, cacheWritten)
    19→ *   7. Regression tests for BUG-01/02/03 and VULN-01
    20→ *   8. Manager cleanup (ImportManager, PackageManager, CjoManager)
    21→ *   9. Destructor safety after partial/full AST release
    22→ *  10. IncrementalCompilerInstance-specific paths
    23→ */

    37→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    38→// Helper: Create a minimal CompilerInstance for testing
    39→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    40→
    41→namespace {
    42→
    43→struct TestCIFixture {
    44→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
    45→    CompilerInvocation invocation;
    46→    std::unique_ptr<CompilerInstance> ci;
    47→
    48→    TestCIFixture()
    49→    {
    50→        ci = std::make_unique<CompilerInstance>(invocation, diag);
    51→    }
    52→};
    53→} // anonymous namespace
    54→
    55→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    56→// Section 1: State Flag Initialization and Accessors
    57→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    58→
    59→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, InitialStateAllFlagsAreFalse)
    60→{
    61→    TestCIFixture f;
    62→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsASTReleased());
    63→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
    64→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsCacheWritten());
    65→    EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->GetCodeGenPkgInfos().empty());
    66→}
    67→
    68→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, SetResultsSavedToggle)
    69→{
    70→    TestCIFixture f;
    71→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
    72→    f.ci->SetResultsSaved(true);
    73→    EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
    74→    f.ci->SetResultsSaved(false);
    75→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
    76→}
    77→
    78→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    79→// Section 2: noReleaseAST Debug Flag
    80→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    81→
    82→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, NoReleaseASTDefaultsFalse)
    83→{
    84→    GlobalOptions opts;
    85→    EXPECT_FALSE(opts.noReleaseAST);
    86→}
    87→
    88→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, NoReleaseASTCanBeEnabled)
    89→{
    90→    GlobalOptions opts;
    91→    opts.noReleaseAST = true;
    92→    EXPECT_TRUE(opts.noReleaseAST);
    93→}
    94→
    95→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, NoReleaseASTPreservesASTState)
    96→{
    97→    // When noReleaseAST is true, PerformASTRelease should NOT set astReleased.
    98→    TestCIFixture f;
    99→    f.invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST = true;
   100→    auto ci = std::make_unique<CompilerInstance>(f.invocation, f.diag);
   101→    // After PerformASTRelease with noReleaseAST=true, AST should NOT be released.
   102→    // We can't call PerformASTRelease directly without full pipeline, but we verify
   103→    // the flag is correctly propagated.
   104→    EXPECT_TRUE(ci->invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST);
   105→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci->IsASTReleased());
   106→}
   107→
   108→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   109→// Section 3: PackageCodeGenInfo Metadata Extraction
   110→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   111→
   112→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageCodeGenInfoDefaultValues)
   113→{
   114→    CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   115→    EXPECT_TRUE(info.fullPackageName.empty());
   116→    EXPECT_FALSE(info.isEmpty);
   117→}
   118→
   119→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageCodeGenInfoStoresValues)
   120→{

   122→    info.fullPackageName = "std.core";
   123→    info.isEmpty = false;
   124→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName, "std.core");
   125→    EXPECT_FALSE(info.isEmpty);

   127→
   128→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageCodeGenInfoEmptyPackage)
   129→{

   131→    info.fullPackageName = "empty.pkg";
   132→    info.isEmpty = true;
   133→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName, "empty.pkg");
   134→    EXPECT_TRUE(info.isEmpty);
   135→}
   136→
   137→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageCodeGenInfoMoveSemantics)
   138→{
   139→    CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   140→    info.fullPackageName = "test.package.with.long.name";
   141→    info.isEmpty = false;
   142→
   143→    CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo moved = std::move(info);
   144→    EXPECT_EQ(moved.fullPackageName, "test.package.with.long.name");
   145→    EXPECT_FALSE(moved.isEmpty);
   146→}
   147→
   148→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, CodeGenPkgInfosEmptyByDefault)
   149→{
   150→    TestCIFixture f;
   151→    EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->GetCodeGenPkgInfos().empty());
   152→}
   153→
   154→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   155→// Section 4: AST2CHIRNodeMap Clear Tests

   162→    nodeMap.Clear();

   173→}

   189→    EXPECT_EQ(map.newExternalDecls.size(), 1u);

   194→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.importedInlineDecls.empty());
   195→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.newExternalDecls.empty());

   216→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.incrRemovedDecls.count("old_decl") == 0);
   217→}
