   311→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   312→// Section 8: CompileStage Enum Ordering
   313→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   314→
   315→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, ReleaseASTStageIsAfterCHIR)
   316→{
   317→    // RELEASE_AST must come after CHIR in the pipeline.
   318→    EXPECT_GT(static_cast<int>(CompileStage::RELEASE_AST),
   319→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CHIR));
   320→}
   321→
   322→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, ReleaseASTStageIsBeforeCodeGen)
   323→{
   324→    // RELEASE_AST must come before CODEGEN in the pipeline.
   325→    EXPECT_LT(static_cast<int>(CompileStage::RELEASE_AST),
   326→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CODEGEN));
   327→}
   328→
   329→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, ReleaseASTStageIsBeforeSaveResults)
   330→{
   331→    // RELEASE_AST must come before SAVE_RESULTS.
   332→    EXPECT_LT(static_cast<int>(CompileStage::RELEASE_AST),
   333→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS));
   334→}
   335→
   336→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PipelineStageOrderIsCorrect)
   337→{
   338→    // Verify the full pipeline ordering around RELEASE_AST.
   339→    int chir = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CHIR);
   340→    int releaseAst = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::RELEASE_AST);
   341→    int codegen = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CODEGEN);
   342→    int saveResults = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS);
   343→
   344→    EXPECT_EQ(releaseAst, chir + 1) << "RELEASE_AST must immediately follow CHIR";
   345→    EXPECT_EQ(codegen, releaseAst + 1) << "CODEGEN must immediately follow RELEASE_AST";
   346→    EXPECT_GT(saveResults, codegen) << "SAVE_RESULTS must come after CODEGEN";
   347→}
   348→
   349→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, CompileStageNumberIsLast)
   350→{
   351→    // COMPILE_STAGE_NUMBER must be the last enum value.
   352→    EXPECT_GT(static_cast<int>(CompileStage::COMPILE_STAGE_NUMBER),
   353→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS));
   354→}
   355→
   356→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   357→// Section 9: Regression Test - BUG-01 (CJO Loss Prevention)
   358→//
   359→// BUG-01: DefaultCompilerInstance in CHIR output mode did not
   360→// call PerformResultsSaving() before ReleaseASTMemory(), causing
   361→// srcPkgs to be empty when SaveCjo ran, silently losing CJO files.
   362→//
   363→// Fix: PerformASTRelease() now calls PerformResultsSaving() before
   364→// ReleaseASTMemory(), guarded by resultsSaved flag.
   365→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   366→
   367→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG01_ResultsSavedGuardPreventsDoubleExecution)
   368→{
   369→    // Verify that the resultsSaved guard prevents double execution.
   370→    TestCIFixture f;
   371→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   372→
   373→    // Simulate first save.
   374→    f.ci->SetResultsSaved(true);
   375→    EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   376→
   377→    // The guard should prevent PerformResultsSaving from running again
   378→    // inside PerformASTRelease. We verify the flag is correctly set.
   379→    // (Full pipeline test would verify CJO file generation.)
   380→}
   381→
   382→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG01_ResultsSavedFlagInitiallyFalse)
   383→{
   384→    // Ensure resultsSaved starts as false so PerformResultsSaving runs
   385→    // at least once during PerformASTRelease.
   386→    TestCIFixture f;
   387→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   388→}
   389→
   390→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   391→// Section 10: Regression Test - BUG-02 (Return Value Check)
   392→//
   393→// BUG-02: PerformResultsSaving() return value was ignored in both
   394→// CompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease() and
   395→// IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease().
   396→//
   397→// Fix: Both now check the return value and propagate failure.
   398→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   399→
   400→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG02_ResultsSavedFlagNotSetOnFailure)
   401→{
   402→    // If PerformResultsSaving fails, resultsSaved should remain false
   403→    // so the destructor can still clean up properly.
   404→    TestCIFixture f;
   405→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   406→    // On failure path, resultsSaved stays false, AST stays intact for cleanup.
   407→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsASTReleased());
   408→}
   409→
   410→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   411→// Section 11: Regression Test - BUG-03 (ASTWriter Leak)
   412→//
   413→// BUG-03: ImportManager::ClearASTReferences() called
   414→// astWriters.clear() instead of DeleteASTWriters(), leaking
   415→// new-allocated ASTWriter* objects.
   416→//
   417→// Fix: Replaced astWriters.clear() with DeleteASTWriters().
   418→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   419→
   420→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG03_ClearASTReferencesDoesNotLeak)
   421→{
   422→    // Verify ClearASTReferences can be called without crash.
   423→    // The actual leak detection requires ASan, but we verify the
   424→    // code path executes correctly.
   425→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   426→    TypeManager typeManager;
   427→    GlobalOptions opts;
   428→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   429→
   430→    // Call ClearASTReferences which should use DeleteASTWriters()
   431→    // instead of astWriters.clear().
   432→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   433→}
   434→
   435→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   436→// Section 12: Regression Test - VULN-01 (Dangling Pointers)

   439→// fields in PackageInfo (pkgDecl, exportIDDeclMap, declMap,
   440→// implicitDeclMap), leaving dangling pointers after AST release.

   443→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════

   448→    // and doesn't leave dangling state.

   451→    GlobalOptions opts;
   452→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   453→
   454→    // First clear.

   456→    // Second clear should be safe (no dangling pointers).
   457→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   458→}
   459→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════

   464→{

   468→    // Destructor runs when f goes out of scope — should not crash.
   469→}

   482→
   483→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, MultipleCompilerInstancesIndependent)
   484→{
   485→    // Multiple CompilerInstances should have independent state.
   486→    DiagnosticEngine diag1, diag2;
   487→    CompilerInvocation inv1, inv2;

   489→    CompilerInstance ci2(inv2, diag2);
   490→

   493→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci2.IsResultsSaved());
   494→
   495→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci1.IsASTReleased());
   496→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci2.IsASTReleased());

   511→{

   514→    auto pkg3 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg3");
   515→

   541→    std::string longName(1024, 'a');
   542→    for (size_t i = 0; i < longName.size(); i += 10) {
   543→        longName[i] = '.';
   544→    }

   546→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName.size(), 1024u);

   553→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName, "仓颉.编译器.测试");
   554→}
   555→
   556→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageManagerClearWithDependencyCycles)
   557→{
   558→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   559→    TypeManager typeManager;
   560→    GlobalOptions opts;
   561→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   562→    PackageManager pm(importManager);
   563→
   564→    // Create circular dependency: pkg1 -> pkg2 -> pkg1
   565→    auto pkg1 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   566→    auto pkg2 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg2");
   567→    pkg1->deps.insert(pkg2.get());
   568→    pkg2->deps.insert(pkg1.get());
   569→
   570→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg1"] = std::move(pkg1);
   571→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg2"] = std::move(pkg2);
   572→
   573→    // ClearASTReferences should handle circular deps safely.
   574→    pm.ClearASTReferences();
   575→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageInfoMap.empty());
   576→}
   577→
   578→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, CachedMangleMapLargeDataSet)
   579→{
   580→    CachedMangleMap map;
   581→    // Insert many entries to test scalability.
   582→    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; ++i) {
   583→        map.incrRemovedDecls.emplace("decl_" + std::to_string(i));
   584→        map.importedInlineDecls.emplace("inline_" + std::to_string(i));
   585→        map.newExternalDecls.emplace("ext_" + std::to_string(i));
   586→    }
   587→    EXPECT_EQ(map.incrRemovedDecls.size(), 1000u);
   588→    EXPECT_EQ(map.importedInlineDecls.size(), 1000u);
   589→    EXPECT_EQ(map.newExternalDecls.size(), 1000u);
   590→
   591→    map.Clear();
   592→
   593→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
   594→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.importedInlineDecls.empty());
   595→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.newExternalDecls.empty());
   596→}
   597→
   598→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   599→// Section 16: Determinism Tests
   600→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   601→
   602→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, StateTransitionsAreDeterministic)
   603→{
   604→    // Same sequence of operations should produce same state.
   605→    for (int trial = 0; trial < 3; ++trial) {
   606→        TestCIFixture f;
   607→        EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsASTReleased());
   608→        EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   609→        EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsCacheWritten());
   610→        f.ci->SetResultsSaved(true);
   611→        EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   612→    }
   613→}
   614→
   615→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageCodeGenInfoVectorOrdering)
   616→{
   617→    // Verify that CodeGenPkgInfos preserves insertion order.
   618→    std::vector<CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo> infos;
   619→    for (int i = 0; i < 5; ++i) {
   620→        CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   621→        info.fullPackageName = "pkg" + std::to_string(i);
   622→        info.isEmpty = (i % 2 == 0);
   623→        infos.push_back(std::move(info));
   624→    }
   625→    EXPECT_EQ(infos.size(), 5u);
   626→    for (int i = 0; i < 5; ++i) {
   627→        EXPECT_EQ(infos[i].fullPackageName, "pkg" + std::to_string(i));
   628→        EXPECT_EQ(infos[i].isEmpty, (i % 2 == 0));
   629→    }
   630→}
   631→
   632→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   633→// Section 17: Cross-Component Integration Tests
   634→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   635→
   636→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, AllManagersClearInSequence)
   637→{
   638→    // Simulate the Phase 3 cleanup sequence: managers cleared in order.
   639→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   640→    TypeManager typeManager;
   641→    GlobalOptions opts;
   642→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   643→    PackageManager pm(importManager);
   644→
   645→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg1"] = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   646→    pm.packageToOtherSccMap["pkg1"] = {"dep1"};
   647→
   648→    // Phase 3f: ImportManager clear
   649→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   650→
   651→    // Phase 3g: PackageManager clear
   652→    pm.ClearASTReferences();
   653→
   654→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageInfoMap.empty());
   655→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageToOtherSccMap.empty());
   656→}
   657→
   658→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, CachedMangleMapAndPackageManagerClearTogether)
   659→{
   660→    // Simulate IncrementalCompilerInstance cleanup sequence.
   661→    CachedMangleMap cacheMangles;
   662→    cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace("removed_1");
   663→    cacheMangles.importedInlineDecls.emplace("inline_1");
   664→
   665→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   666→    TypeManager typeManager;
   667→    GlobalOptions opts;
   668→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   669→    PackageManager pm(importManager);
   670→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg1"] = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   671→
   672→    // Incremental-specific cleanup
   673→    cacheMangles.Clear();
   674→    EXPECT_TRUE(cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
   675→
   676→    // Then base class cleanup
   677→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   678→    pm.ClearASTReferences();
   679→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageInfoMap.empty());
   680→}
   681→
```

</details>

<details><summary>返回结果 (211 行)</summary>

```
     1→// Copyright (c) Huawei Technologies Co., Ltd. 2025. All rights reserved.
     2→// This source file is part of the Cangjie project, licensed under Apache-2.0
     3→// with Runtime Library Exception.
     4→//
     5→// See https://cangjie-lang.cn/pages/LICENSE for license information.
     6→
     7→#include "gtest/gtest.h"
     8→#include "cangjie/AST/Node.h"
     9→#include "cangjie/CHIR/CHIR.h"
    10→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/AST2CHIRNodeMap.h"
    11→#include "cangjie/CHIR/IR/Type/CHIRType.h"
    12→#include "cangjie/Frontend/CompilerInstance.h"
    13→#include "cangjie/IncrementalCompilation/CachedMangleMap.h"
    14→#include "cangjie/Modules/PackageManager.h"

    23→TEST(AST2CHIRNodeMapTest, ClearEmptiesCache)
    24→{
    25→    CHIR::AST2CHIRNodeMap<CHIR::CustomTypeDef> nodeMap;
    26→    EXPECT_TRUE(nodeMap.GetALL().empty());
    27→
    28→    // Clear on empty map should be safe.
    29→    nodeMap.Clear();
    30→    EXPECT_TRUE(nodeMap.GetALL().empty());
    31→}
    32→
    33→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    34→// CachedMangleMap::Clear tests
    35→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
    36→
    37→TEST(CachedMangleMapTest, ClearRemovesAllData)
    38→{
    39→    CachedMangleMap map;
    40→    map.incrRemovedDecls.emplace("test_decl_1");
    41→    map.importedInlineDecls.emplace("inline_decl_1");
    42→    map.newExternalDecls.emplace("external_decl_1");
    43→
    44→    EXPECT_FALSE(map.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
    45→    EXPECT_FALSE(map.importedInlineDecls.empty());
    46→    EXPECT_FALSE(map.newExternalDecls.empty());
    47→
    48→    map.Clear();
    49→
    50→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
    51→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.importedInlineDecls.empty());
    52→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.newExternalDecls.empty());
    53→}
    54→
    55→TEST(CachedMangleMapTest, ClearIsIdempotent)
    56→{
    57→    CachedMangleMap map;
    58→    map.incrRemovedDecls.emplace("decl_1");
    59→
    60→    map.Clear();
    61→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
    62→
    63→    // Second clear should be safe.
    64→    map.Clear();
    65→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
    66→}

   324→    void CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable();
   325→
   326→    void CollectStaticInitFuncInfo();
   327→    void CollectFuncsAndVars();
   328→    void CollectLocalConstFuncAndVars(const AST::Package& pkg);
   329→    std::pair<InitOrder, bool> SortGlobalVarDecl(const AST::Package& pkg);
   330→
   331→    void SetGenericDecls() const;
   332→    void SetExtendInfo();
   333→    void UpdateExtendParent();
   334→
   335→    Translator CreateTranslator();
   336→    /* Micro refactoring for CJMP. */
   337→    void TranslateFuncParams(const AST::FuncDecl& funcDecl, Func& func) const;
   338→    void TranslateVecDecl(const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls, Translator& trans) const;
   339→
   340→    /* Add methods for CJMP. */
   341→    // Try to deserialize common part for CJMP.
   342→    bool TryToDeserializeCHIR();
   343→    // Check whether the decl is deserialized for CJMP.
   344→    bool MaybeDeserialized(const AST::Decl& decl) const;
   345→    // Try to get deserialized node from package including CustomTypeDef (excluding Extend), Func, GlobalVar,
   346→    // ImportedValue.
   347→    template<typename T>
   348→    T* TryGetDeserialized(const AST::Decl& decl)
   349→    {
   350→        if (!MaybeDeserialized(decl)) {
   351→            return nullptr;
   352→        }
   353→        std::string key = GLOBAL_VALUE_PREFIX + decl.mangledName;
   354→        if (decl.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::FOREIGN) && decl.IsFunc()) {
   355→            key = decl.rawMangleName;
   356→        }
   357→        T* res = nullptr;
   358→        if constexpr (std::is_base_of_v<CustomTypeDef, T>) {
   359→            auto it = deserializedDefs.find(key);
   360→            res = it == deserializedDefs.end() ? nullptr : static_cast<T*>(it->second);
   361→        } else {
   362→            // get value
   363→            auto it = deserializedVals.find(key);
   364→            res = it == deserializedVals.end() ? nullptr : dynamic_cast<T*>(it->second);
   365→        }
   366→        if (res && !decl.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::SPECIFIC)) {
   367→            deserializedDecls.insert(&decl);
   368→        }
   369→        return res;
   370→    }
   371→    // build symbol table for deserialized decls from common part.
   372→    void BuildDeserializedTable();
   373→
   374→    // Reset specific func for CJMP.
   375→    void ResetSpecificFunc(const AST::FuncDecl& funcDecl, Func& func);
   376→    // Check whether the decl need be translated for CJMP.
   377→    inline bool NeedTranslate(const AST::Decl& decl) const
   378→    {
   379→        return deserializedDecls.find(&decl) == deserializedDecls.end();
   380→    }
   381→    void ProcessCommonAndSpecificExtends();
   382→    void ProcessClassStructVarInits(Translator& trans);
   383→    const GlobalOptions& opts;
   384→    const GenericInstantiationManager* gim;
   385→    ImportManager& importManager;
   386→    SourceManager& sourceManager;
   387→    TypeManager& types;
   388→    DiagAdapter& diag;
   389→    CompilationCache& cachedInfo;
   390→    IncreKind kind;
   391→    VirtualWrapperDepMap curVirtFuncWrapDep;
   392→    VirtualWrapperDepMap delVirtFuncWrapForIncr;
   393→    // cache global func decl, global var decl
   394→    AST2CHIRNodeMap<Value> globalCache;
   395→
   396→    CHIRBuilder& builder;
   397→    CHIRType& chirType;
   398→
   399→    std::vector<Ptr<AST::Node>> allTopLevelNodes;
   400→    /** @brief all files that after sorting in this package */
   401→    std::vector<AST::File*> pkgFiles;
   402→    std::unordered_map<std::string, FuncBase*> implicitFuncs;
   403→    std::vector<FuncBase*> initFuncsForConstVar;
   404→    std::vector<Func*> initFuncsForAnnoFactory;

   416→    std::unordered_set<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> implicitDecls{};
   417→    // including imported global var and static var.
   418→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> importedGlobalAndStaticVars{};
   419→    // including imported global func and member func.
   420→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> importedGlobalAndMemberFuncs{};
   421→    // including imported nominal decl: ClassDecl、InterfaceDecl、StructDecl、EnumDecl.
   422→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> importedNominalDecls{};
   423→

   425→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> importedGenericInstantiatedNominalDecls{};
   426→
   427→    // ======================== Current Pkg Top-Level Decl Part ======================== //
   428→    // including global VarDecl、global VarWithPatternDecl、static member VarDecl.
   429→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> globalAndStaticVars{};
   430→    /// during computeAnnotations, translate only the annoFactoryFuncs of these decls.
   431→    /// These are decls that are not preserved when selecting const subpkg but have @!CustomAnnotations's.
   432→    /// \See ComputeAnnotations.cpp
   433→    std::vector<const AST::Decl*> annoOnlyDecls{};
   434→    // including global FuncDecl、instantiated global FuncDecl、 MemberDecl(instance/static/open/abstract/instantiated).
   435→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> globalAndMemberFuncs{};
   436→    // including ClassDecl、InterfaceDecl、StructDecl、ExtendDecl、EnumDecl.
   437→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> nominalDecls{};
   438→
   439→    // Definition in other language, thus no body
   440→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> foreignFuncs{};
   441→

   445→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> genericNominalDecls{};
   446→

     1→// Copyright (c) Huawei Technologies Co., Ltd. 2025. All rights reserved.
     2→// This source file is part of the Cangjie project, licensed under Apache-2.0
     3→// with Runtime Library Exception.
     4→//
     5→// See https://cangjie-lang.cn/pages/LICENSE for license information.
     6→
     7→/**
     8→ * @file
     9→ *
    10→ * This file declares the symbol table of CHIR.
    11→ */
    12→
    13→#ifndef CANGJIE_CHIR_SYMBOLTABLE_H
    14→#define CANGJIE_CHIR_SYMBOLTABLE_H
    15→
    16→#include "cangjie/AST/Match.h"
    17→#include "cangjie/AST/Node.h"
    18→#include "cangjie/CHIR/IR/Value/Value.h"
    19→#include "cangjie/Mangle/CHIRMangler.h"
    20→#include "cangjie/Sema/TypeManager.h"
    21→
    22→namespace Cangjie::CHIR {
    23→template <typename T> class AST2CHIRNodeMap {
    24→public:
    25→    AST2CHIRNodeMap()
    26→    {
    27→    }
    28→    ~AST2CHIRNodeMap() = default;
    29→    bool Has(const Cangjie::AST::Node& node) const
    30→    {
    31→        return cache.find(&node) != cache.end();
    32→    }
    33→
    34→    void Set(const Cangjie::AST::Node& node, T& chirNode)
    35→    {
    36→        CJC_ASSERT(cache.emplace(&node, &chirNode).second);
    37→    }
    38→
    39→    T* Get(const Cangjie::AST::Node& node) const
    40→    {
    41→        auto chirNode = cache.at(&node);
    42→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(chirNode);
    43→        return chirNode;
    44→    }
    45→
    46→    T* TryGet(const Cangjie::AST::Node& node) const
    47→    {
    48→        auto it = cache.find(&node);
    49→        if (it != cache.end()) {
    50→            return it->second;
    51→        }
    52→        return nullptr;
    53→    }
    54→
    55→    const std::unordered_map<const Cangjie::AST::Node*, T*>& GetALL() const
    56→    {
    57→        return cache;
    58→    }
    59→
    60→    void Erase(const Cangjie::AST::Node& node)
    61→    {
    62→        (void)cache.erase(&node);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    void Clear()
    66→    {
    67→        cache.clear();
    68→    }
    69→
    70→private:
    71→    std::unordered_map<const Cangjie::AST::Node*, T*> cache;
    72→};
    73→} // namespace Cangjie::CHIR
    74→#endif
```

    27→ * PackageInfo stores information about the current package, including to packageName, package dir path, source files
    28→ * and dependencies.
    29→ */
    30→struct PackageInfo {

    40→};
    41→
    42→/**
    43→ * PackageManager is used to do module compilation by resolving package dependencies and generating build commands.
    44→ */
    45→class PackageManager {
    46→public:
    47→    explicit PackageManager(ImportManager& importManager) : importManager(importManager)
    48→    {
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    /**
    52→     * Resolve package dependencies using topological sort method. It should be noted that circular dependencies are
    53→     * allowed.
    54→     * @param pkgs packages whose dependencies need to be resolved.
    55→     * @param withCodeGen it is true when call this function in CodeGen staged.
    56→     */
    57→    bool ResolveDependence(std::vector<Ptr<AST::Package>>& pkgs);
    58→
    59→    /**
    60→     * Return buildOrders for read private member.
    61→     */

    63→    {
    64→        return orderedPackageInfos;
    65→    }
    66→
    67→    /**
    68→     * If a package relies on packages which are from other SCC (Strongly Connected Component), it should be recorded.
    69→     */
    70→    std::unordered_map<std::string, std::set<std::string>> packageToOtherSccMap;
    71→    std::unordered_map<std::string, std::unique_ptr<PackageInfo>> packageInfoMap;
    72→
    73→    /**
    74→     * Clear AST-derived dependency data after CHIR lowering.
    75→     * The dependency info has already been resolved and is no longer needed.
    76→     */
    77→    void ClearASTReferences()
    78→    {
    79→        packageToOtherSccMap.clear();
    80→        packageInfoMap.clear();
    81→        orderedPackageInfos.clear();
    82→    }
    83→
    84→private:
    85→    ImportManager& importManager;
    86→    std::vector<std::vector<PackageInfo*>> orderedPackageInfos;
    87→    struct TarjanContext {
    88→        std::unordered_map<PackageInfo*, size_t> indices;  /**< The discovered order of vertices in a DFS. */
    89→        std::unordered_map<PackageInfo*, size_t> lowlinks; /**< The smallest index reachable from the vertex. */
    90→        std::unordered_map<PackageInfo*, bool> onStack;    /**< Indicate whether the vertex is on stack. */
    91→    };

    34→using namespace Cangjie;

    38→namespace {
    39→void AddImplicitImportAll(File& file, const std::string& fullPackageName)
    40→{
    41→    // Check whether the prefix paths are already cached.
    42→    static FullPackageNameToPrefixPaths fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths;
    43→    std::vector<std::string> curPrefixPaths{};
    44→    if (fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths.find(fullPackageName) != fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths.end()) {
    45→        curPrefixPaths = fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths.at(fullPackageName);
    46→    } else {
    47→        curPrefixPaths = Utils::SplitQualifiedName(fullPackageName);
    48→        fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths.insert({fullPackageName, curPrefixPaths});
    49→    }
    50→    // Check whether the import is already added.
    51→    for (auto it = file.imports.rbegin(); it != file.imports.rend(); ++it) {
    52→        auto& import = *it;
    53→        if (!import->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPLICIT_ADD)) {
    54→            continue;
    55→        }
    56→        if (import->content.kind != ImportKind::IMPORT_ALL) {
    57→            continue;
    58→        }
    59→        if (import->content.prefixPaths == fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths.at(fullPackageName)) {
    60→            return; // The import is already added not add again.
    61→        }
    62→    }
    63→    // Add the import if not added.
    64→    file.imports.emplace_back(CreateImportSpec(fullPackageName, "*", "", fullPackageNameToPrefixPaths));
    65→}
    66→
    67→void AddImplicitImports(Package& pkg, const GlobalOptions& opts)
    68→{
    69→    for (auto& file : pkg.files) {
    70→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(file);
    71→        if (opts.implicitPrelude) {
    72→            AddImplicitImportAll(*file, CORE_PACKAGE_NAME);
    73→        }
    74→        if (opts.enableCompileTest) {
    75→            AddImplicitImportAll(*file, "std.unittest");
    76→            AddImplicitImportAll(*file, "std.unittest.testmacro");
    77→        }
    78→        if (opts.compileTestsOnly && ImportManager::IsTestPackage(pkg.fullPackageName)) {
    79→            AddImplicitImportAll(*file, ImportManager::GetMainPartPkgNameForTestPkg(pkg.fullPackageName));
    80→        }
    81→    }
    82→}
    83→
    84→struct DependencyInfoItem {
    85→    std::string package;
    86→    std::string orPackage;
    87→    bool isStd{false};
    88→    std::set<Ptr<ImportSpec>, CmpNodeByPos> imports;
    89→};
    90→
    91→std::string Jsonfy(bool b)
    92→{
    93→    return b ? "true" : "false";

    97→{
    98→    CJC_ASSERT(level != AccessLevel::PRIVATE);
    99→    return level == AccessLevel::PUBLIC ? "public" : level == AccessLevel::PROTECTED ? "protected" : "internal";

<details><summary>返回结果 (300 行)</summary>

```
     1→# 仓颉编译器 AST 内存释放方案
     2→
     3→---
     4→
     5→## 一、需求背景
     6→
     7→### 1.1 问题
     8→
     9→仓颉编译器在 AST 阶段结束后，AST 数据结构仍驻留内存直到编译器实例析构。对于大型项目，AST 占用的内存可达数百 MB，而后续的 CHIR lowering 和 CodeGen 阶段不再需要 AST。需要在 CHIR lowering 完成后主动释放 AST 内存，降低编译峰值内存。
    10→
    11→### 1.2 核心前提（已验证）
    12→
    13→**CHIR IR 节点不持有 AST 指针**：
    14→- `CHIR::Package`、`CHIR::Func`、`CHIR::Block`、`CHIR::Value` 等 IR 节点使用独立的 `DebugLocation`（文件名 + 行号），不引用 AST 节点
    15→- `GenPackageModules()`（`EmitPackageIR.cpp:587`）签名接收 `CHIRData&`，不依赖 `AST::Package`
    16→- CodeGen 的类型信息完全来自 CHIR 类型系统（`CHIR::Type`），与 AST 类型系统（`AST::Ty`）独立
    17→
    18→### 1.3 编译流水线
    19→
    20→```
    21→PARSE → CONDITION_COMPILE → IMPORT_PACKAGE → MACRO_EXPAND → AST_DIFF →
    22→SEMA → MANGLING → SAVE_CJO → CHIR → [RELEASE_AST] → CODEGEN → SAVE_RESULTS
    23→                                       ↑ 新增阶段
    24→```
    25→
    26→`CompileStage` 枚举（`CompilerInstance.h:45-65`）驱动 `Compile()` 主循环（`CompilerInstance.cpp:175-213`），每个阶段对应一个 `Perform*()` 虚方法。
    27→
    28→---
    29→
    30→## 二、方案总览
    31→
    32→方案由两个互补部分组成：
    33→
    34→| 方案 | 释放时机 | 释放粒度 | 内存收益 | 改动量 |
    35→|------|---------|---------|---------|--------|
    36→| **函数体粒度释放** | CHIR lowering Step 4 中逐步释放 | `FuncBody::body`、`VarDeclAbstract::initializer` | 60-80% AST | ~60 行 |
    37→| **完整清理** | CHIR 完成后独立阶段一次性释放 | 整棵 AST + 管理器 + imported packages | 90-95% AST | ~320 行 |
    38→| **组合（推荐）** | Step 4 中 + CHIR 后 | 全部 | 95%+ AST | ~380 行 |
    39→
    40→内存曲线对比：
    41→
    42→```
    43→当前：AST 存活到编译器析构
    44→ 内存 ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    45→      │   AST (全量)                                  │
    46→      └──────────────────────────────────────────────┘
    47→
    48→组合方案：边翻译边释放 + CHIR 后完整清理
    49→ 内存 ┌──────────┐
    50→      │ AST 全量  │╲
    51→      │           │  ╲  ← 函数体粒度释放（Step 4 中）
    52→      │           │    ╲
    53→      │           │ 骨架 ╲──┐
    54→      │           │         │ ← 完整清理（RELEASE_AST 阶段）
    55→      └───────────┘         └──────────────────────►
    56→      Step1-3    Step4    RELEASE_AST           CodeGen
    57→```
    58→
    59→---
    60→
    61→## 三、函数体粒度释放
    62→
    63→### 3.1 原理
    64→
    65→AST 声明节点（`FuncDecl`、`VarDecl`）在整个 lowering 过程中被 `globalCache`、`AST2CHIRCheck`、`CompilationCache` 反复引用，必须保留。但函数体内部的代码块和变量初始化表达式在翻译完成后不再被访问：
    66→
    67→```
    68→FuncDecl (声明节点 — 必须保留)
    69→├── identifier, mangledName, ty, attrs  ← 签名信息，被 globalCache/AST2CHIRCheck 引用
    70→├── funcBody: OwnedPtr<FuncBody>
    71→│   ├── paramLists  ← 被 GlobalDeclAnalysis 引用（GlobalDeclAnalysis.cpp:46-48）
    72→│   ├── retType     ← 签名信息
    73→│   └── body: OwnedPtr<Block>  ← 实际代码块，翻译后可释放 ✅
    74→│       ├── statements
    75→│       ├── expressions
    76→│       └── nested blocks
    77→
    78→VarDeclAbstract (声明节点 — 必须保留)
    79→├── identifier, mangledName, ty, attrs  ← 签名信息
    80→├── type: OwnedPtr<Type>  ← 类型信息，保留
    81→└── initializer: OwnedPtr<Expr>  ← 初始化表达式，翻译后可释放 ✅
    82→```
    83→
    84→**安全边界**：仅释放 `funcBody->body`（`OwnedPtr<Block>`），不释放 `funcBody` 本身。`funcBody->paramLists`、`funcBody->retType` 等签名级成员不受影响。不得将释放粒度扩大到整个 `funcBody`（`TranslateNominalDecls` 内部的 genericFuncMap 构建依赖 `paramLists`，见 `ASTPackage2CHIR.cpp:1308-1312`）。
    85→
    86→### 3.2 安全性验证
    87→
    88→`ToCHIRPackage()` 的 5 步流程中，各步骤对 `funcBody->body` 和 `initializer` 的访问情况：
    89→
    90→| 步骤 | 操作 | 读取 body | 读取 initializer |
    91→|------|------|-----------|-----------------|
    92→| Step 1: CollectTopLevelDecls | 收集声明指针 | ❌ | ❌ |
    93→| Step 2: SortGlobalVarDecl | 依赖分析 | ❌（仅读 paramLists） | ✅ 读取 |
    94→| Step 3: CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable | 创建签名 | ❌ | ❌ |
    95→| Step 4a: TranslateNominalDecls | 翻译类型方法体 | ✅ 读取并翻译 | — |
    96→| Step 4a 内部: genericFuncMap 构建 | 泛型参数验证 | ❌（仅读 paramLists） | — |
    97→| Step 4b: TranslateInitOfGlobalVars | 翻译全局变量初始化 | — | ✅ 读取并翻译 |
    98→| Step 4c: TranslateTopLevelDecls | 翻译函数体 | ✅ 读取并翻译 | — |
    99→| Step 5: AST2CHIRCheck | 验证 | ❌ 仅读 ty/identifier/mangledName | ❌ 仅读 ty |
   100→
   101→关键验证结果：
   102→
   103→1. `AST2CHIRCheck`（`AST2CHIRChecker.cpp:481-522`）：`CheckFunc` 仅访问 `decl.outerDecl`、`decl.ty`、`decl.TestAttr()`；`CheckVar` 仅访问 `decl.ty`。不读取函数体和初始化表达式。
   104→
   105→2. `GlobalDeclAnalysis`（`GlobalDeclAnalysis.cpp:20-53`）：`CollectDepInCallExpr` 访问 `funcBody->paramLists[0]->params[i]->desugarDecl`，但不访问 `funcBody->body`。
   106→
   107→3. 并行翻译（`ParallelUtil::RunAST2CHIRInParallel`）：每个函数的 body 只被一个线程读取，释放不存在竞争。
   108→
   109→4. `globalCache` 引用其他函数时只查找 CHIR 签名，不读取其他函数的 AST body。
   110→
   111→5. Lowering 阶段不执行内联展开（`@inline` 在 CodeGen 阶段处理），并行翻译中不存在函数体交叉引用。
   112→
   113→### 3.3 释放策略
   114→
   115→| 翻译子步骤 | 释放方式 | 理由 |
   116→|-----------|---------|------|
   117→| TranslateNominalDecls | 返回后**批量释放**方法体 | 内部逻辑复杂（泛型实例化、extends），侵入性高 |
   118→| TranslateInitOfGlobalVars | 返回后**批量释放** initializer | 委托给 GlobalVarInitializer，侵入性高 |
   119→| TranslateTopLevelDecls（串行） | 循环中**逐个释放** | 循环结构简单，峰值内存收益最大 |
   120→| TranslateTopLevelDecls（并行） | 返回后**批量释放** | 避免修改 ParallelUtil 通用接口 |
   121→| annoFactoryFuncs | 循环中**逐个释放** | 串行循环，结构简单 |
   122→
   123→### 3.4 实现代码
   124→
   125→#### 辅助方法声明
   126→
   127→```cpp
   128→// AST2CHIR.h — 新增 private 方法
   129→private:
   130→    void ReleaseFuncBody(const AST::Decl& decl);
   131→    void ReleaseVarInitializer(AST::VarDeclAbstract& decl);
   132→    void ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(const AST::Package& pkg);
   133→    void ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(const InitOrder& initOrder);
   134→    void ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies();
   135→```
   136→
   137→#### 辅助方法实现
   138→
   139→```cpp
   140→// AST2CHIR.cpp
   141→
   142→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseFuncBody(const AST::Decl& decl)
   143→{
   144→    if (auto* funcDecl = DynamicCast<const AST::FuncDecl*>(&decl)) {
   145→        if (funcDecl->funcBody && funcDecl->funcBody->body) {
   146→            // OwnedPtr::get() 是 const 方法，返回 Ptr<T>
   147→            // 通过 Ptr<FuncBody> 访问 body 得到 OwnedPtr<Block>&（非 const），reset() 合法
   148→            funcDecl->funcBody->body.reset();
   149→        }
   150→    }
   151→}
   152→
   153→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseVarInitializer(AST::VarDeclAbstract& decl)
   154→{
   155→    if (decl.initializer) {
   156→        decl.initializer.reset();
   157→    }
   158→}
   159→
   160→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(const AST::Package& pkg)
   161→{
   162→    // 只遍历当前包的 nominal 类型，跳过 imported 类型
   163→    auto releaseMethodBodies = [this](const auto& declList) {
   164→        for (auto& decl : declList) {
   165→            if (!NeedTranslate(*decl)) { continue; }
   166→            // ClassDecl、InterfaceDecl 继承 ClassLikeDecl
   167→            if (auto* classLike = DynamicCast<const AST::ClassLikeDecl*>(decl.get())) {
   168→                for (auto& member : classLike->members) {
   169→                    ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   170→                }
   171→            }
   172→            // StructDecl 不继承 ClassLikeDecl，独立处理
   173→            if (auto* structDecl = DynamicCast<const AST::StructDecl*>(decl.get())) {
   174→                for (auto& member : structDecl->members) {
   175→                    ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   176→                }
   177→            }
   178→            // EnumDecl 不继承 ClassLikeDecl，独立处理
   179→            if (auto* enumDecl = DynamicCast<const AST::EnumDecl*>(decl.get())) {
   180→                for (auto& member : enumDecl->members) {
   181→                    ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   182→                }
   183→            }
   184→        }
   185→    };
   186→    releaseMethodBodies(nominalDecls);
   187→    releaseMethodBodies(genericNominalDecls);
   188→}
   189→
   190→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(const InitOrder& initOrder)
   191→{
   192→    for (auto& [decl, deps] : initOrder) {
   193→        if (auto* varDecl = DynamicCast<AST::VarDeclAbstract*>(
   194→                const_cast<AST::Decl*>(decl))) {
   195→            ReleaseVarInitializer(*varDecl);
   196→        }
   197→    }
   198→}
   199→
   200→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies()
   201→{
   202→    for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   203→        if (NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   204→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   205→        }
   206→    }
   207→    for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   208→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   209→    }
   210→}
   211→```
   212→
   213→#### TranslateAllDecls 修改
   214→
   215→```cpp
   216→// AST2CHIR.cpp — TranslateAllDecls 修改
   217→void AST2CHIR::TranslateAllDecls(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   218→{
   219→    // step 1: translate nominal decls
   220→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateNominalDecls");
   221→    TranslateNominalDecls(pkg);
   222→    ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(pkg);  // 批量释放 nominal 方法体
   223→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateNominalDecls");
   224→
   225→    // step 2: translate initialization of global var
   226→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateInitOfGlobalVars");
   227→    TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(pkg, initOrder);
   228→    ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(initOrder);  // 批量释放 initializer
   229→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateInitOfGlobalVars");
   230→
   231→    // step 3: translate body of all funcs
   232→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   233→    if (opts.GetJobs() > 1) {
   234→        TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel();
   235→        ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies();  // 并行完成后批量释放
   236→    } else {
   237→        for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   238→            if (!NeedTranslate(*decl)) { continue; }
   239→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   240→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   241→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   242→            if (decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GLOBAL)) {
   243→                trans.CollectValueAnnotation(*decl);
   244→            }
   245→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);  // 逐个释放
   246→        }
   247→        for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   248→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   249→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   250→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   251→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);  // 逐个释放
   252→        }
   253→    }
   254→    // annoFactoryFuncs
   255→    for (auto decl : annoFactoryFuncs) {
   256→        auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   257→        trans.SetTopLevel(*decl.first);
   258→        trans.TranslateAnnoFactoryFuncBody(*decl.first, *decl.second);
   259→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl.first);  // 逐个释放
   260→    }
   261→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   262→
   263→    // step 4: set CompileTimeValue for lambda — 不受影响，操作 CHIR IR
   264→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   265→    for (auto func : package->GetGlobalFuncs()) {
   266→        if (func->TestAttr(Attribute::CONST)) {
   267→            SetCompileTimeValueFlagRecursivly(*func);
   268→        }
   269→    }
   270→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   271→}
   272→```
   273→
   274→### 3.5 接口稳定性
   275→
   276→- 不修改任何现有公开接口
   277→- `ReleaseFuncBody` 等方法均为 `AST2CHIR` 的 private 方法
   278→- `TranslateAllDecls` 的签名和语义不变
   279→- `OwnedPtr::reset()` 将指针置 null 并 delete 旧对象，后续任何误访问会立即暴露为 null 解引用
   280→
   281→---
   282→
   283→## 四、CHIR 完成后完整清理

   295→    RELEASE_AST,    // 新增：AST 内存释放

   300→
   301→#### Compile() 主循环扩展
   302→
   303→```cpp
   304→// CompilerInstance.cpp — Compile() 中添加 case
   305→case CompileStage::RELEASE_AST:
   306→    ret = PerformASTRelease();
   307→    break;

   309→
   310→#### PerformASTRelease 虚方法
   311→
   312→```cpp
   313→// CompilerInstance.h — 新增
   314→protected:
   315→    bool astReleased = false;
   316→    void ReleaseASTMemory();
   317→
   318→public:
   319→    bool IsASTReleased() const { return astReleased; }
   320→    virtual bool PerformASTRelease();
   321→```
   322→
   323→```cpp
   324→// CompilerInstance.cpp
   325→bool CompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease()
   326→{
   327→    // 无论是否释放 AST，都提取 CodeGen 元信息（统一单路径）
   328→    if (codeGenPkgInfos.empty()) {
   329→        PrepareCodeGenInfo();
   330→    }
   331→    if (!packageDependenceResolved) {
   332→        MaterializePackageDependence();
   333→    }
   334→
   335→    if (invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST) {
   336→        return true;
   337→    }
   338→
   339→    ReleaseASTMemory();
   340→    return true;
   341→}
   342→```
   343→
   344→### 4.2 PackageCodeGenInfo — CodeGen 脱离 srcPkgs 依赖
   345→
   346→AST 释放后 `srcPkgs` 为空，`GetSourcePackages()` 返回空列表，CodeGen 循环体不执行。解决方案：在 AST 释放前提取 CodeGen 所需的最小元信息，CodeGen 统一走单路径。
   347→
   348→```cpp
   349→// CompilerInstance.h — 新增
   350→struct PackageCodeGenInfo {
   351→    std::string fullPackageName;
   352→    bool isEmpty;
   353→};
   354→
   355→class CompilerInstance {
   356→    // ...
   357→    std::vector<PackageCodeGenInfo> codeGenPkgInfos;
   358→    bool packageDependenceResolved = false;
   359→};
   360→```
   361→
   362→```cpp
   363→// CompilerInstance.cpp
   364→void CompilerInstance::PrepareCodeGenInfo()
   365→{
   366→    codeGenPkgInfos.clear();
   367→    for (auto& srcPkg : srcPkgs) {
   368→        codeGenPkgInfos.push_back({srcPkg->fullPackageName, srcPkg->IsEmpty()});
   369→    }
   370→}
   371→```
   372→
   373→#### CodeGen 统一单路径
   374→
   375→不保留旧路径，始终通过 `PackageCodeGenInfo` 驱动。即使 AST 未释放（`--no-release-ast`），也在 `RELEASE_AST` 阶段提取 `PackageCodeGenInfo`（但不释放 AST）。
   376→
   377→```cpp
   378→// DefaultCompilerInstance.cpp — 统一后的 PerformCodeGen
   379→bool DefaultCIImpl::PerformCodeGen()
   380→{
   381→    MaterializePackageDependenceIfNeeded();
   382→    bool ret = true;
   383→    for (auto& info : ci.codeGenPkgInfos) {
   384→        ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(info, false);
   385→    }
   386→    return ret;
   387→}
   388→
   389→bool DefaultCIImpl::CodegenOnePackage(
   390→    const PackageCodeGenInfo& pkgInfo, bool enableIncrement)
   391→{
   392→    if (pkgInfo.isEmpty) { return true; }
   393→    if (ci.invocation.globalOptions.disableCodeGen) { return true; }
   394→
   395→    auto backend = ci.invocation.globalOptions.backend;
   396→    switch (backend) {
   397→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   398→        case Triple::BackendType::CJNATIVE: {
   399→            if (!EmitLLVMSimilarBytecode(pkgInfo.fullPackageName, enableIncrement)) {
   400→                return false;
   401→            }
   402→            break;
   403→        }
   404→#endif
   405→        // ... 其他 backend
   406→    }
   407→    return true;
   408→}
   409→
   410→bool DefaultCIImpl::EmitLLVMSimilarBytecode(
   411→    const std::string& fullPackageName, bool enableIncrement)
   412→{
   413→    CHIR::CHIRBuilder builder(ci.chirData.GetCHIRContext());
   414→    // GenPackageModules 不依赖 AST::Package
   415→    llvmModules = CodeGen::GenPackageModules(
   416→        builder, ci.chirData, ci.invocation.globalOptions, ci, enableIncrement);
   417→
   418→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("CodeGen", "Save bc file");
   419→    ci.invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(fullPackageName);
   420→    if (llvmModules.size() == 1) {
   421→        auto filePath = GenerateBCFilePathAndUpdateToInvocation(
   422→            TempFileKind::T_BC, fullPackageName);
   423→        if (filePath.empty()) { return false; }
   424→        CodeGen::SavePackageModule(*llvmModules[0], filePath);
   425→    } else {
   426→        // 多模块并行保存，使用 fullPackageName 字符串
   427→        // ...
   428→    }
   429→    if (ci.invocation.globalOptions.enIncrementalCompilation) {
   430→        auto fileName = GenerateFileName(fullPackageName, "");
   431→        ci.cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName = std::vector<std::string>{fileName};
   432→    }
   433→    return true;
   434→}
   435→```
   436→
   437→#### 包依赖关系物化
   438→
   439→```cpp
   440→// CompilerInstance.cpp
   441→void CompilerInstance::MaterializePackageDependence()
   442→{
   443→    std::vector<Ptr<AST::Package>> allImportedPackages;
   444→    for (auto pd : importManager.GetAllImportedPackages(true)) {
   445→        if (pd && pd->srcPackage) {
   446→            allImportedPackages.push_back(pd->srcPackage);
   447→        }
   448→    }
   449→    packageManager->ResolveDependence(allImportedPackages);
   450→    packageDependenceResolved = true;
   451→}
   452→
   453→// DefaultCompilerInstance.cpp
   454→void DefaultCIImpl::MaterializePackageDependenceIfNeeded()
   455→{
   456→    if (ci.packageDependenceResolved) {
   457→        return;  // 已在 AST 释放前完成
   458→    }
   459→    // fallback：--no-release-ast 模式下首次调用
   460→    ci.MaterializePackageDependence();
   461→}
   462→```
   463→
   464→### 4.3 ReleaseASTMemory — 完整 5 阶段清理
   465→
   466→```cpp
   467→// CompilerInstance.cpp
   468→void CompilerInstance::ReleaseASTMemory()
   469→{
   470→    if (astReleased) { return; }
   471→
   472→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   473→    // Phase 0: 前置操作（必须在 AST 释放前完成）
   474→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   475→
   476→    // 0a. 提取 CodeGen 所需的最小元信息
   477→    if (codeGenPkgInfos.empty()) {
   478→        PrepareCodeGenInfo();
   479→    }
   480→
   481→    // 0b. 物化包依赖关系
   482→    if (!packageDependenceResolved) {
   483→        MaterializePackageDependence();
   484→    }
   485→
   486→    // 0c. 物化 CompilationCache 中的 AST 引用
   487→    //     必须在 CHIR 阶段完成后执行（GlobalDeclAnalysis.cpp:490 重写 varAndFuncDep）
   488→    MaterializeCachedASTReferences();
   489→
   490→    // 0d. 增量编译缓存写入
   491→    //     WriteCachedInfo 原本在 FrontendTool.cpp:216 的 ExecuteCompile() 返回后调用，
   492→    //     但它解引用 srcPkgs[0]、order 中的 AST 指针、varAndFuncDep 和 semaInfo.usages。
   493→    //     必须在 AST 释放前完成。
   494→    if (ShouldWriteCacheFile() && !cacheWritten) {
   495→        WriteCachedInfoBeforeRelease();
   496→        cacheWritten = true;
   497→    }
   498→
   499→    // 0e. 增量编译结果保存
```

</details>

    31→CMAKE_OUTPUT_DIR = os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output")
    32→OUTPUT_BIN_DIR = os.path.join(CMAKE_OUTPUT_DIR, "bin")
    33→LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BUILD_DIR, "logs")

    35→
    36→IS_WINDOWS = platform.system() == "Windows"
    37→IS_MACOS = platform.system() == "Darwin"
    38→IS_ARM = platform.uname().processor in ["aarch64", "arm", "arm64"]
    39→CJ_OS_NAME = platform.system().lower()
    40→CJ_ARCH_NAME = platform.machine().replace("AMD64", "x86_64").lower() # normalize AMD64 in Windows to x86_64
    41→CAN_RUN_CJNATIVE = (platform.system(), platform.machine()) in [
    42→    ("Linux", "x86_64"),

    51→# Wait for the version of aarch64 libcore to be ready.
    52→DELTA_JOBS = 2
    53→MAKE_JOBS = multiprocessing.cpu_count() + DELTA_JOBS

    73→def resolve_path(path):
    74→    if os.path.isabs(path):
    75→        return path
    76→    return os.path.abspath(path)
    77→
    78→def log_output(output, checker=None, args=[]):
    79→    """log command output"""
    80→    while True:
    81→        line = output.stdout.readline()
    82→        if not line:
    83→            output.communicate()
    84→            returncode = output.returncode
    85→            if returncode != 0:
    86→                LOG.error("build error: %d!\n", returncode)
    87→                sys.exit(1)
    88→            break
    89→        try:
    90→            LOG.info(line.decode("ascii", "ignore").rstrip())
    91→        except UnicodeEncodeError:
    92→            LOG.info(line.decode("utf-8", "ignore").rstrip())
    93→
    94→def generate_version_tail(target):
    95→    """generate version string for cjc compiler"""
    96→
    97→    res = "{}".format("cjnative")
    98→    res = " (" + res + ")"
    99→
   100→    arch_name = platform.machine().replace("AMD64", "x86_64").replace("arm64", "aarch64").lower()
   101→    vendor_name = "apple" if IS_MACOS else "unknown"
   102→    os_name = None
   103→    if IS_WINDOWS:
   104→        os_name = "windows-gnu"
   105→    elif IS_MACOS:
   106→        os_name = "darwin"
   107→    else:
   108→        os_name = "linux-gnu"
   109→    res += "\\nTarget: {}".format(target) if target else "\\nTarget: {0}-{1}-{2}".format(arch_name, vendor_name, os_name)
   110→    return str(res)
   111→
   112→def generate_cmake_defs(args):
   113→    """convert args to cmake defs"""
   114→
   115→    def bool_to_opt(value):
   116→        return "ON" if value else "OFF"
   117→
   118→    if args.target:
   119→        if args.target == "aarch64-linux-ohos":
   120→            toolchain_file = "ohos_aarch64_clang_toolchain.cmake"
   121→        elif args.target == "arm-linux-ohos":
   122→            toolchain_file = "ohos_arm_clang_toolchain.cmake"
   123→        elif args.target == "x86_64-linux-ohos":
   124→            toolchain_file = "ohos_x86_64_clang_toolchain.cmake"
   125→        elif args.target == "x86_64-w64-mingw32":
   126→            toolchain_file = "mingw_x86_64_toolchain.cmake"
   127→        elif args.target == "arm64-apple-ios11-simulator":
   128→            toolchain_file = "ios_simulator_arm64_toolchain.cmake"
   129→        elif args.target == "x86_64-apple-ios11-simulator":
   130→            toolchain_file = "ios_simulator_x86_64_toolchain.cmake"
   131→        elif args.target == "arm64-apple-ios11":
   132→            toolchain_file = "ios_arm64_toolchain.cmake"
   133→        elif "aarch64-linux-android" in args.target:
   134→            toolchain_file = "android_aarch64_toolchain.cmake"
   135→        elif "x86_64-linux-android" in args.target:
   136→            toolchain_file = "android_x86_64_toolchain.cmake"
   137→    else:
   138→        args.target = None
   139→        if IS_WINDOWS:
   140→            toolchain_file = "mingw_x86_64_toolchain.cmake"
   141→        elif IS_MACOS:
   142→            toolchain_file = "darwin_aarch64_toolchain.cmake" if IS_ARM else "darwin_x86_64_toolchain.cmake"
   143→        elif IS_ARM:
   144→            toolchain_file = "linux_aarch64_toolchain.cmake"
   145→        else:
   146→            toolchain_file = "linux_x86_64_toolchain.cmake"
   147→
   148→    install_prefix = CMAKE_OUTPUT_DIR + ("-{}".format(args.target) if (args.target and args.product == "cjc") else "")
   149→
   150→    result = [
   151→        "-DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=" + args.build_type.value,
   152→        "-DCMAKE_ENABLE_ASSERT=" + bool_to_opt(args.enable_assert),
   153→        "-DCMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX=" + install_prefix,
   154→        "-DCMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE=" + os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "cmake/" + toolchain_file),
   155→        "-DCMAKE_PREFIX_PATH=" + (args.target_toolchain + "/../x86_64-w64-mingw32" if args.target_toolchain else ""),
   156→        "-DCANGJIE_BUILD_TESTS=" + bool_to_opt((not args.no_tests) and (args.product == "all" or args.product == "libs")),
   157→        "-DCANGJIE_BUILD_CJC=" + bool_to_opt(args.product in ['all', 'cjc']),
   158→        "-DCANGJIE_BUILD_STD_SUPPORT=" + bool_to_opt(args.product in ['all', 'libs']),
   159→        "-DCANGJIE_BUILD_CJDB=" + bool_to_opt(args.build_cjdb),
   160→        "-DCANGJIE_INSTALL_CJDB_SCRIPT=" + bool_to_opt(args.install_cjdb_script),
   161→        "-DCANGJIE_ENABLE_HWASAN=" + bool_to_opt(args.hwasan),
   162→        "-DCANGJIE_VERSION=" + generate_version_tail(args.target),
   163→        "-DBUILD_GCC_TOOLCHAIN=" + (args.gcc_toolchain if args.gcc_toolchain and args.target is None else ""),
   164→        "-DCANGJIE_TARGET_LIB=" + (";".join(args.target_lib) if args.target_lib else ""),
   165→        "-DCANGJIE_TARGET_TOOLCHAIN=" + (args.target_toolchain if args.target_toolchain else ""),
   166→        "-DCANGJIE_INCLUDE=" + (";".join(args.include) if args.include else ""),
   167→        "-DCANGJIE_TARGET_SYSROOT=" + (args.target_sysroot if args.target_sysroot else ""),
   168→        "-DCANGJIE_LINK_JOB_POOL=" + (str(args.link_jobs) if args.link_jobs != 0 else ""),
   169→        "-DCANGJIE_DISABLE_STACK_GROW_FEATURE=" + bool_to_opt(args.disable_stack_grow_feature),
   170→        "-DCANGJIE_USE_OH_LLVM_REPO=" + bool_to_opt(args.use_oh_llvm_repo),
   171→        "-DCANGJIE_ENABLE_SANITIZE_OPTION=" + bool_to_opt(args.enable_sanitize_option)]
   172→
   173→    if args.version:
   174→        result.append("-DCJ_SDK_VERSION=" + args.version)
   175→
   176→    if args.target and "aarch64-linux-android" in args.target:
   177→        android_api_level = re.match(r'aarch64-linux-android(\d{2})?', args.target).group(1)
   178→        result.append("-DCMAKE_ANDROID_NDK=" + (args.android_ndk if args.android_ndk else ""))
   179→        result.append("-DCMAKE_ANDROID_API=" + (android_api_level if android_api_level else ""))
   180→
   181→    if args.sanitizer_support:
   182→        result.append("-DCANGJIE_SANITIZER_SUPPORT=" + args.sanitizer_support)
   183→    return result
   184→
   185→def download_and_patch_tinytoml():
   186→    """Set up the tinytoml third-party library"""
   187→    TINYTOML_DIR = os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "third_party", "tinytoml")
   188→    PATCH_FILE = os.path.join(TINYTOML_DIR, "fixFloatEqualError.patch")
   189→    TAR_PATH = os.path.join(TINYTOML_DIR, "tinytoml-0.4.tar.gz")
   190→    TINYTOMLTAR_PATH = os.path.join(TINYTOML_DIR, "tinytoml-0.4")
   191→
   192→    LOG.info("Setting up tinytoml...")
   193→
   194→    # Create Parent Directory
   195→    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(TINYTOML_DIR), exist_ok=True)
   196→
   197→    try:
   198→
   199→        if not os.path.exists(TAR_PATH):
   200→            # Fetch tinytoml from the remote repostory
   201→            subprocess.run(
   202→                ["git", "clone", "https://gitcode.com/src-openeuler/tinytoml.git",
   203→                 TINYTOML_DIR],
   204→                 check=True
   205→            )
   206→            # Switch to the specified tag
   207→            subprocess.run(
   208→                ["git", "checkout", "openEuler-24.03-LTS-SP1"],
   209→                cwd=TINYTOML_DIR,
   210→                check=True
   211→            )
   212→
   213→        # Extract the package
   214→        LOG.info("Extracting tinytoml package...")
   215→        with tarfile.open(TAR_PATH) as tar:
   216→            tar.extractall(path=TINYTOML_DIR)
   217→
   218→        # Apply Patch
   219→        patch_file_exists = os.path.exists(PATCH_FILE)
   220→        target_dir_exists = os.path.exists(TINYTOMLTAR_PATH) and os.path.isdir(TINYTOMLTAR_PATH)
   221→        if patch_file_exists and target_dir_exists:
   222→            LOG.info("Applying tinytoml patch...")
   223→            subprocess.run(
   224→                f"patch -p0 -l -f < {PATCH_FILE}",
   225→                cwd=TINYTOMLTAR_PATH,
   226→                shell=True,
   227→                check=True
   228→            )
   229→        else:
   230→            LOG.warning(f"Patch file not found: {PATCH_FILE}")
   231→
   232→        TOML_H_SRC = os.path.join(TINYTOMLTAR_PATH, "include", "toml", "toml.h")
   233→        TOML_H_DST = os.path.join(TINYTOML_DIR, "toml.h")
   234→
   235→        if os.path.exists(TOML_H_SRC):
   236→            LOG.info(f"Copying toml.h from {TOML_H_SRC} to {TOML_H_DST}")
   237→            shutil.copy2(TOML_H_SRC, TOML_H_DST)
   238→
   239→    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
   240→        LOG.error(f"Failed to setup tinytoml: {str(e)}")
   241→        # Clean Files
   242→        if os.path.exists(TINYTOML_DIR):
   243→            shutil.rmtree(TINYTOML_DIR)
   244→        raise
   245→
   246→def build(args):
   247→    # The target also affects the prefix concatenation of the compiler executable file; it is specific.
   248→    if args.target:
   249→        args.target = TARGET_DICTIONARY[args.target]
   250→
   251→    if args.gcc_toolchain and args.target and args.product != "cjc":
   252→        LOG.warning("There is no intermediate or product targeting the host platform in this build, so --gcc-toolchain won't take effect")
   253→
   254→    # Add the tinytoml third-party library for acquisition and customize code application.
   255→    tinytoml_target = os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "third_party", "tinytoml", "toml.h")
   256→    if not os.path.exists(tinytoml_target):
   257→        download_and_patch_tinytoml()
   258→
   259→    check_compiler(args)
   260→
   261→    """build cangjie compiler"""
   262→    LOG.info("begin build...")
   263→
   264→    set_cjnative_backend_env(args)
   265→
   266→    if args.product is None:
   267→        args.product = "all" if args.target is None else "libs"
   268→
   269→    if args.target == "aarch64-linux-ohos" or args.target == "x86_64-linux-ohos":
   270→        # Frontend supports cross compilation in a general way by asking path to required tools
   271→        # and libraries. However, Runtime supports cross compilation in a speific way, which asks
   272→        # for the root path of OHOS toolchain. Since we asked for a path to tools, the root path of
   273→        # OHOS toolchain is relative to the tool path we get. Tool path normally looks like
   274→        # ${OHOS_ROOT}/prebuilts/clang/ohos/linux-x86_64/llvm/bin/. Six /.. can bring us to the root.
   275→        os.environ["OHOS_ROOT"] = os.path.join(args.target_toolchain, "../../../../../..")
   276→
   277→    if args.android_ndk:
   278→        os.environ["ANDROID_NDK_ROOT"] = args.android_ndk
   279→
   280→    if IS_WINDOWS:
   281→        # For Windows, try Ninja first, otherwise use Make instead.
   282→        ninja_valid = True
   283→        try:
   284→            output = subprocess.Popen(["ninja", "--version"], stdout=DEVNULL, stderr=DEVNULL)
   285→            output.communicate()
   286→            ninja_valid = output.returncode == 0
   287→        except:
   288→            ninja_valid = False
   289→
   290→        if ninja_valid:
   291→            generator = "Ninja"
   292→            build_cmd = ["ninja"]
   293→            if args.jobs > 0:
   294→                build_cmd.extend(["-j", str(args.jobs)])
   295→        else:
   296→            generator = "MinGW Makefiles"
   297→            build_cmd = ["mingw32-make", "-j" + str(MAKE_JOBS)]
   298→    else:
   299→        # For Linux, just use Ninja.
   300→        generator = "Ninja"
   301→        build_cmd = ["ninja"]
   302→        if args.jobs > 0:
   303→            build_cmd.extend(["-j", str(args.jobs)])
   304→
   305→    cmake_command = ["cmake", HOME_DIR, "-G", generator] + generate_cmake_defs(args)
   306→
   307→    if args.print_cmd:
   308→        print(' '.join(cmake_command))
   309→        exit(0)
   310→
   311→    if args.target == "x86_64-w64-mingw32":
   312→        package_mingw_dependencies(args)
   313→
   314→    if not os.path.exists(BUILD_DIR):
   315→        os.makedirs(BUILD_DIR)
   316→
   317→    if args.sanitizer_support:
   318→        cmake_build_dir = os.path.join(BUILD_DIR, "build-libs-{}".format(args.sanitizer_support))
   319→        if args.target:
   320→            cmake_build_dir += "-{}".format(args.target)
   321→    else:
   322→        cmake_build_dir = os.path.join(BUILD_DIR, "build-{}-{}".format(args.product, args.target)) if args.target else CMAKE_BUILD_DIR
   323→
   324→    if not os.path.exists(os.path.join(cmake_build_dir, "build.ninja")):
   325→        os.makedirs(cmake_build_dir, exist_ok=True)
   326→        output = subprocess.Popen(cmake_command, cwd=cmake_build_dir, stdout=PIPE)
   327→        log_output(output)
   328→
   329→    output = subprocess.Popen(build_cmd, cwd=cmake_build_dir, stdout=PIPE)
   330→    log_output(output)
   331→
   332→    if output.returncode != 0:
   333→        LOG.fatal("build failed")
   334→
   335→    LOG.info("end build")
   336→
   337→def set_cangjie_env(args):
   338→    os.environ["HOME_DIR"] = HOME_DIR
   339→    os.environ[LD_LIBRARY_PATH] = PATH_ENV_SEPERATOR.join([
   340→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output/lib"),
   341→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output/runtime/lib/{os}_{arch}_cjnative".format(os=CJ_OS_NAME, arch=CJ_ARCH_NAME)),
   342→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output/tools/lib"),
   343→        os.environ.get(LD_LIBRARY_PATH, "")
   344→    ])
   345→    LOG.info("set cangjie env: %s=%s", LD_LIBRARY_PATH, os.environ[LD_LIBRARY_PATH])
   346→
   347→def set_cjnative_backend_env(args):
   348→    os.environ[LD_LIBRARY_PATH] = PATH_ENV_SEPERATOR.join([
   349→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, CMAKE_OUTPUT_DIR, "lib"),
   350→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, CMAKE_OUTPUT_DIR, "lib/{os}_{arch}_cjnative".format(os=CJ_OS_NAME, arch=CJ_ARCH_NAME)),
   351→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "build/build/lib"),
   352→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "build/build/lib/{os}_{arch}_cjnative".format(os=CJ_OS_NAME, arch=CJ_ARCH_NAME)),
   353→        os.environ.get(LD_LIBRARY_PATH, "")
   354→    ] + (args.target_lib if hasattr(args, 'target_lib') else []))
   355→    LOG.info("set cjnative backend env: %s=%s", LD_LIBRARY_PATH, os.environ[LD_LIBRARY_PATH])
   356→
   357→    os.environ[LIBRARY_PATH] = PATH_ENV_SEPERATOR.join([
   358→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "build/build/lib"),
   359→        os.environ.get(LIBRARY_PATH, "")
   360→    ] + (args.target_lib if hasattr(args, 'target_lib') else []))
   361→    LOG.info("set cjnative backend env: %s=%s", LIBRARY_PATH, os.environ[LIBRARY_PATH])
   362→
   363→    os.environ["PATH"] = PATH_ENV_SEPERATOR.join([
   364→        os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output/tools/bin"),
   365→        os.environ.get("PATH", "")])
   366→
   367→    if IS_MACOS:
   368→        os.environ["ZERO_AR_DATE"] = "1"
   369→
   370→def test(args):
   371→    """test"""
   372→    LOG.info("begin test...")
   373→    if platform.system() == "Linux" or platform.system() == "Darwin":
   374→        set_cangjie_env(args)
   375→    unit_test(args)
   376→    LOG.info("end test...\n")
   377→
   378→def unit_test(args):
   379→    """unit test"""
   380→    LOG.info("begin unit test...\n")
   381→    output = subprocess.Popen(
   382→        ["ctest", "--output-on-failure"], cwd=CMAKE_BUILD_DIR, stdout=PIPE
   383→    )
   384→    log_output(output)
   385→    LOG.info("end unit test...\n")
   386→
   387→def install(args):
   388→    """install targets"""
   389→    if args.host:
   390→        args.host = TARGET_DICTIONARY[args.host]
   391→
   392→    LOG.info("begin install targets...")
   393→    targets = []
   394→
   395→    # - If "build.py install" is invoked without "--host",
   396→    #   the native build directories and all cross-compiled libs
   397→    #   will be installed to the "output" directory.
   398→    # - If "build.py install" is invoked with "--host <triple>",
   399→    #   the build-cjc-<triple> directories and all cross-compiled libs
   400→    #   will be installed to a seperated "output-<target>" directory.
   401→
   402→    # Searching for cjc's build directory.
   403→    if not args.host:
   404→        if os.path.exists(CMAKE_BUILD_DIR):
   405→            targets.append(("native", CMAKE_BUILD_DIR))
   406→    else:
   407→        suffix = "cjc-{}".format(args.host)
   408→        cross_build_path = os.path.join(BUILD_DIR, "build-{}".format(suffix))
   409→        if os.path.exists(cross_build_path):
   410→            targets.append((suffix, cross_build_path))
   411→
   412→    # Searching for all libs' build directories.
   413→    for directory in os.listdir(BUILD_DIR):
   414→        build_prefix = "build-libs-"
   415→        if directory.startswith(build_prefix):
   416→            targets.append(("libs-{}".format(directory[len(build_prefix):]), os.path.join(BUILD_DIR, directory)))
   417→
   418→    if len(targets) == 0:
   419→        LOG.fatal("Nothing is built yet.")
   420→        sys.exit(1)
   421→
   422→    # install for all build directories in the list
   423→    for target in targets:
   424→        LOG.info("installing {} build...".format(target[0]))
   425→        cmake_cmd = ["cmake", "--install", "."]
   426→        if args.prefix:
   427→            cmake_cmd += ["--prefix", os.path.abspath(args.prefix)]
   428→        elif args.host:
   429→            cmake_cmd += ["--prefix", os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output-{}".format(args.host))]
   430→
   431→        output = subprocess.Popen(cmake_cmd, cwd=target[1], stdout=PIPE)
   432→        log_output(output)
   433→        if output.returncode != 0:
   434→            LOG.fatal("install {} build failed".format(target[0]))
   435→            sys.exit(1)
   436→
   437→    if args.host == "x86_64-w64-mingw32":
   438→        mingw_bin_path = os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output-x86_64-w64-mingw32/third_party/mingw/bin")
   439→        if os.path.exists(mingw_bin_path):
   440→            for bin in os.listdir(mingw_bin_path):
   441→                bin_path = os.path.join(mingw_bin_path, bin)
   442→                if os.path.isfile(bin_path) and not bin.endswith(".exe") and bin != "libssp-0.dll":
   443→                    os.remove(bin_path)
   444→    LOG.info("end install targets...")
   445→
   446→def redo_with_write(redo_func, path, err):
   447→    # Is the error an access error?
   448→    if not os.access(path, os.W_OK):
   449→        os.chmod(path, stat.S_IWUSR)
   450→        redo_func(path)
   451→    else:
   452→        raise
   453→
   454→def clean(args):
   455→    """clean build outputs and logs"""
   456→
   457→    LOG.info("begin clean...\n")
   458→    # In order to successfully delete all files in the build directory,
   459→    # the file handlers (especially for cangjie.log) that this script holds must be closed first.
   460→    handlerToBeRemoved = []
   461→    for handler in LOG.handlers:
   462→        if isinstance(handler, logging.FileHandler):
   463→            handler.close()
   464→            handlerToBeRemoved.append(handler)
   465→    for handler in handlerToBeRemoved:
   466→        LOG.removeHandler(handler)
   467→    output_dirs = []
   468→
   469→    # Remove entire build directory by default
   470→    output_dirs.append("build")
   471→    output_dirs.append("output")
   472→    # Files in `cjnative_backend` directory may be used while installing if native build is built
   473→    # from binary. It can only be removed when `build.py clean` is being applied to all build targets.
   474→    output_dirs.append("third_party/binary/llvm_backend")
   475→
   476→    # Collecting all cross-compiled cjcs' build directories.
   477→    cross_output_suffix = []
   478→    for directory in os.listdir(BUILD_DIR):
   479→        build_prefix = "build-cjc-"
   480→        if directory.startswith(build_prefix):
   481→            cross_output_suffix.append(directory[len(build_prefix):])
   482→    # Removing all cross-compiled output package.
   483→    for suffix in cross_output_suffix:
   484→        cross_output_path = os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "output-{}".format(suffix))
   485→        if os.path.isdir(cross_output_path):
   486→            output_dirs.append(cross_output_path)
   487→
   488→    for file_path in output_dirs:
   489→        abs_file_path = os.path.join(HOME_DIR, file_path)
   490→        if os.path.isdir(abs_file_path):
   491→            # If some build files are read-only and not allowed to be deleted (especially in Windows),
   492→            # Try to deal with the error by giving write permissions and deleting them again.
   493→            shutil.rmtree(abs_file_path, ignore_errors=False, onerror=redo_with_write)
   494→        if os.path.isfile(abs_file_path):
   495→            os.remove(abs_file_path)
   496→    LOG.info("end clean\n")
   497→
   498→def package_mingw_dependencies(args):
   499→    if os.path.exists(os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "third_party/binary/windows-x86_64-mingw.tar.gz")):
   500→        return
   501→    LOG.info("Packaging mingw dependencies...")
   502→    def copy_files_to(from_path, filename_list, to_directory):
   503→        if not os.path.exists(to_directory):
   504→            os.makedirs(to_directory, exist_ok=True)
   505→        for filename in filename_list:
   506→            filepath = os.path.join(from_path, filename)
   507→            if os.path.exists(filepath):
   508→                shutil.copy(filepath, to_directory + "/")
   509→            else:
   510→                LOG.info("%s not found, skipped packaging the file...", filepath)
   511→
   512→    search_path = args.target_toolchain if args.target_toolchain else None
   513→    mingw_path = str(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(shutil.which("x86_64-w64-mingw32-gcc", path=search_path)))))
   514→    mingw_package_path = str(os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "third_party/binary/mingw"))
   515→    dll_dependencies = ["bin/libc++.dll", "bin/libunwind.dll", "bin/libwinpthread-1.dll"]
   516→    copy_files_to(os.path.join(mingw_path, "x86_64-w64-mingw32"), dll_dependencies, os.path.join(mingw_package_path, "dll"))
   517→    lib_dependencies = ["crt2.o", "dllcrt2.o", "libadvapi32.a", "libkernel32.a", "libm.a", "libmingw32.a",
   518→                            "libmingwex.a", "libmoldname.a", "libmsvcrt.a", "libpthread.a", "libshell32.a", "libuser32.a",
   519→                            "libc++.a", "libdbghelp.a", "libshlwapi.a", "libunwind.a",
   520→                            "libws2_32.a", "libcrypt32.a", "crtbegin.o", "crtend.o", "CRT_glob.o"]
   521→    copy_files_to(os.path.join(mingw_path, "x86_64-w64-mingw32/lib"), lib_dependencies, os.path.join(mingw_package_path, "lib"))
   522→
   523→    subprocess.run(["tar", "-C", "mingw", "-zcf", "windows-x86_64-mingw.tar.gz", "dll", "lib"],
   524→        cwd=os.path.join(HOME_DIR, "third_party/binary"))
   525→    
   526→def init_log(name):
   527→    """init log config"""
   528→    if not os.path.exists(LOG_DIR):
   529→        os.makedirs(LOG_DIR)
   530→
   531→    log = logging.getLogger(name)
   532→    log.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
   533→    formatter = logging.Formatter(
   534→        "[%(asctime)s] [%(module)s] [%(levelname)s] %(message)s",
   535→        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
   536→    )
   537→    streamhandler = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
   538→    streamhandler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
   539→    streamhandler.setFormatter(formatter)
   540→    log.addHandler(streamhandler)
   541→    filehandler = TimedRotatingFileHandler(
   542→        LOG_FILE, when="W6", interval=1, backupCount=60
   543→    )
   544→    filehandler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
   545→    filehandler.setFormatter(formatter)
   546→    log.addHandler(filehandler)
   547→    return log
   548→
   549→class BuildType(Enum):
   550→    """CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE options"""
   551→
   552→    debug = "Debug"
   553→    release = "Release"
   554→    relwithdebinfo = "RelWithDebInfo"
   555→
   556→    def __str__(self):
   557→        return self.name
   558→
   559→    def __repr__(self):
   560→        return str(self)
   561→
   562→    @staticmethod
   563→    def argparse(s):
   564→        try:
   565→            return BuildType[s]
   566→        except KeyError:
   567→            return s.build_type
   568→
   569→def main():
   570→    """build entry"""
   571→    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="build cangjie project")
   572→    subparsers = parser.add_subparsers(help="sub command help")
   573→
   574→    parser_clean = subparsers.add_parser("clean", help="clean build", add_help=False)
   575→    parser_clean.set_defaults(func=clean)
   576→
   577→    parser_build = subparsers.add_parser("build", help=" build cangjie")
   578→    parser_build.add_argument(
   579→        "-t", "--build-type", type=BuildType.argparse, dest="build_type", choices=list(BuildType), required=True,
   580→        help="select target build type"
   581→    )
   582→    parser_build.add_argument(
   583→        "--print-cmd", action="store_true", help="print the command to cmake without running"
   584→    )
   585→    parser_build.add_argument(
   586→        "-j", "--jobs", dest="jobs", type=int, default=0, help="run N jobs in parallel (0 means default)"
   587→    )
   588→    parser_build.add_argument(
   589→        "--link-jobs", dest="link_jobs", type=int, default=0, help="max N link jobs in parallel (0 means default)"
   590→    )
   591→    parser_build.add_argument(
   592→        "--enable-assert", action="store_true", help="build with assert and self-checking, only effective in release mode"
   593→    )
   594→    parser_build.add_argument(
   595→        "--no-tests", action="store_true", help="build without unittests"
   596→    )
   597→    # cjnative BE supports stack grow feature and cjc enables stack grow feature by default. However, the feature is
   598→    # supported at a cost of code-size and performance. In code-size and performance sensitive scenario, the feature
   599→    # can be disabled by specifying the following build option.
   600→    parser_build.add_argument(
   601→        "--disable-stack-grow-feature", action="store_true", help="disable default stack grow feature for cjnative BE"
   602→    )
   603→    parser_build.add_argument(
   604→        "--hwasan", action="store_true",
   605→        help="build with hardware asan, only available when the target is ohos-aarch64 or ohos-x86_64"
   606→    )
   607→    parser_build.add_argument(
   608→        "--gcc-toolchain", dest="gcc_toolchain", help="Specify toolchain for cjc, stdlib & BE build"
   609→    )
   610→    parser_build.add_argument(
   611→        "--target", dest="target", type=str, choices=TARGET_DICTIONARY.keys(),
   612→        help="build a second stdlib for the target triple specified"
   613→    )
   614→    parser_build.add_argument(
   615→        "-L", "--target-lib", dest="target_lib", type=str, action='append', default=[],
   616→        help="link libraries under this path for all products"
   617→    )
   618→    parser_build.add_argument(
   619→        "--target-toolchain", dest="target_toolchain", type=str,
   620→        help="use the tools under the given path to cross-compile stdlib"
   621→    )
   622→    parser_build.add_argument(
   623→        "-I", "--include", dest="include", type=str, action='append', default=[],
   624→        help="search header files in given paths"
   625→    )
   626→    parser_build.add_argument(
   627→        "--target-sysroot", dest="target_sysroot", type=str,
   628→        help="pass this argument to C/CXX compiler as --sysroot"
   629→    )
   630→    parser_build.add_argument(
   631→        "--android-ndk", dest="android_ndk", type=str,
   632→        help="Specify the path to the android NDK"
   633→    )
   634→    product_types=['all', 'cjc', 'libs']
   635→    parser_build.add_argument(
   636→        "--product", dest="product", choices=product_types,
   637→        help="specify which part of Cangjie to build"
   638→    )
   639→    parser_build.add_argument(
   640→        "--build-cjdb", action="store_true",
   641→        help="build cjc with cjdb"
   642→    )
   643→    parser_build.add_argument(
   644→            "--install-cjdb-script", action="store_true",
   645→            help="install cjdb with python script"
   646→    )
   647→    parser_build.add_argument(
   648→        "--use-oh-llvm-repo", action="store_true",
   649→        help="use OpenHarmony llvm repo with Cangjie llvm patch instead of cangjie llvm repo for building"
   650→    )
   651→    parser_build.add_argument(
   652→        "--cjlib-sanitizer-support",
   653→        type=str,
   654→        choices=["asan", "tsan", "hwasan"],
   655→        dest="sanitizer_support",
   656→        help="Enable cangjie sanitizer support for cangjie libraries."
   657→    )
   658→    parser_build.add_argument(
   659→        "--enable-sanitize-option", action="store_true",
   660→        help="enable --sanitize option for cjc"
   661→    )
   662→    parser_build.add_argument(
   663→        "-v", "--version",
   664→        dest="version",
   665→        default="0.0.1",
   666→        help="Version string, e.g., 0.0.1"
   667→    )
   668→    parser_build.set_defaults(func=build)
   669→
   670→    parser_install = subparsers.add_parser("install", help="install targets")
   671→    parser_install.add_argument(
   672→        "--host", dest="host", type=str, choices=TARGET_DICTIONARY.keys(),
   673→        help="Generate installation package for the host. When --prefix is specified, this option will not take effect"
   674→    )
   675→    parser_install.add_argument(
   676→        "--prefix", dest="prefix", help="target install prefix"
   677→    )
   678→    parser_install.set_defaults(func=install)
   679→
   680→    parser_test = subparsers.add_parser("test", help="run unittests", add_help=False)
   681→    parser_test.set_defaults(func=test)
   682→
   683→    args = parser.parse_args()
   684→    args.func(args)
   685→
   686→def check_compiler(args):
   687→    # If user didn't specify --target-toolchain, we search for an available compiler in $PATH.
   688→    # If user did specify --target-toolchain, we search in user given path ONLY. By doing so
   689→    # user could see a 'compiler not found' error if the given path is incorrect.
   690→    toolchain_path = args.target_toolchain if args.target_toolchain else None
   691→    if toolchain_path and (not os.path.exists(toolchain_path)):
   692→        LOG.error("the given toolchain path does not exist, {}".format(toolchain_path))
   693→    # The gcc with the MinGW triple prefix is used for Windows native compiling.
   694→    if IS_WINDOWS and args.target is None:
   695→        c_compiler = shutil.which("x86_64-w64-mingw32-gcc.exe", path=toolchain_path)
   696→        cxx_compiler = shutil.which("x86_64-w64-mingw32-g++.exe", path=toolchain_path)
   697→    else: # On other platform, clang is always the first choice.
   698→        c_compiler = shutil.which("clang", path=toolchain_path)
   699→        cxx_compiler = shutil.which("clang++", path=toolchain_path)
   700→    # If clang is not available and we are cross compiling, we check for gcc cross compiler.
   701→    if (c_compiler == None or cxx_compiler == None) and args.target:
   702→        c_compiler = shutil.which(args.target + "-gcc", path=toolchain_path)
   703→        cxx_compiler = shutil.which(args.target + "-g++", path=toolchain_path)
   704→    # If none of above is available, we search for generic gcc compiler.
   705→
   706→    if c_compiler == None or cxx_compiler == None:
   707→        c_compiler = shutil.which("gcc", path=toolchain_path)
   708→        cxx_compiler = shutil.which("g++", path=toolchain_path)
   709→
   710→    if c_compiler == None or cxx_compiler == None:
   711→        if toolchain_path:
   712→            LOG.error("cannot find available compiler in the given toolchain path")
   713→        else:
   714→            LOG.error("cannot find available compiler in $PATH")
   715→        LOG.error("clang/clang++ or gcc/g++ is required to build cangjie compiler")
   716→
   717→    # If cross-compiling cjc, a native compiler is also needed by cross-building LLVM,
   718→    # because it needs some native tools like llvm-tblgen to generate codes.
   719→    # In this case, CMake will use the value in $CC as the native compiler.
   720→    if args.target and args.product == "cjc" and not c_compiler.endswith("clang"):
   721→        os.environ["CC"] = shutil.which("clang") + (" --gcc-toolchain={}".format(args.gcc_toolchain) if args.gcc_toolchain else "")
   722→        os.environ["CXX"] = shutil.which("clang++") + (" --gcc-toolchain={}".format(args.gcc_toolchain) if args.gcc_toolchain else "")
   723→    else:
   724→        os.environ["CC"] = c_compiler
   725→        os.environ["CXX"] = cxx_compiler
   726→
   727→if __name__ == "__main__":
   728→    LOG = init_log("root")
   729→    os.environ["LANG"] = "C.UTF-8"
   730→
   731→    main()
   732→
```

     1→// Copyright (c) Huawei Technologies Co., Ltd. 2025. All rights reserved.

     7→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/AST2CHIR.h"
     8→
     9→#include "cangjie/AST/Match.h"
    10→#include "cangjie/AST/Utils.h"
    11→#include "cangjie/Basic/Match.h"
    12→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/AST2CHIRChecker.h"
    13→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/CollectLocalConstDecl/CollectLocalConstDecl.h"
    14→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/GlobalDeclAnalysis.h"
