    16→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/TranslateASTNode/Translator.h"

    23→
    24→namespace Cangjie::CHIR {
    25→bool AST2CHIR::HasFailed() const
    26→{
    27→    return this->failure;
    28→}
    29→
    30→void AST2CHIR::RegisterAllSources()
    31→{
    32→    auto& sources = sourceManager.GetSources();
    33→    for (auto idToSource : sources) {
    34→        auto& source = idToSource.second;
    35→        auto filePath = source.path;
    36→        auto absPath = FileUtil::GetAbsPath(source.path);
    37→        if (absPath.has_value()) {
    38→            filePath = absPath.value();
    39→        } else {
    40→            filePath = FileUtil::Normalize(filePath);
    41→        }
    42→        builder.GetChirContext().RegisterSourceFileName(source.fileID, filePath);
    43→    }
    44→}
    45→
    46→void AST2CHIR::CollectStaticInitFuncInfo()
    47→{
    48→    auto collectStaticInitFuncInfo = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& funcs) {
    49→        for (auto& func : funcs) {
    50→            if (!IsStaticInitializer(*func)) {
    51→                continue;
    52→            }
    53→            // Get all the static member variables which are inited by this `static.init` func
    54→            std::vector<Ptr<const AST::VarDecl>> staticVars;
    55→            Ptr<const AST::VarDecl> staticInitVar = nullptr;
    56→            auto parentDecl = StaticCast<const AST::InheritableDecl*>(func->outerDecl);
    57→            for (auto memberVar : GetStaticMemberVars(*parentDecl)) {
    58→                // Skip the generated class_static_init variable
    59→                if (memberVar->identifier == STATIC_INIT_VAR) {
    60→                    staticInitVar = memberVar;
    61→                    continue;
    62→                }
    63→                // Skip the variable which has default init value
    64→                if (memberVar->initializer != nullptr) {
    65→                    continue;
    66→                }
    67→                staticVars.emplace_back(memberVar);
    68→                varsInitedByStaticInitFunc.emplace(memberVar);
    69→            }
    70→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(func->outerDecl);
    71→            staticInitFuncInfoMap.emplace(
    72→                func->outerDecl, StaticInitInfo(StaticCast<AST::FuncDecl*>(func), staticInitVar, staticVars));
    73→        }
    74→    };
    75→    collectStaticInitFuncInfo(globalAndMemberFuncs);
    76→}
    77→
    78→void AST2CHIR::CollectFuncsAndVars()
    79→{
    80→    auto collectVars = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& candidateVars) {
    81→        for (auto& var : candidateVars) {
    82→            // Skip the static variables which are inited by the `static init func`
    83→            if (var->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::STATIC) && var->identifier != STATIC_INIT_VAR) {
    84→                bool fromCommon = var->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::FROM_COMMON_PART);
    85→                bool initedInStaticInit = varsInitedByStaticInitFunc.find(var) != varsInitedByStaticInitFunc.end();
    86→                if (!fromCommon && initedInStaticInit) {
    87→                    continue;
    88→                }
    89→            }
    90→            funcsAndVars.AddElement(var);
    91→            fileAndVarMap[var->curFile].emplace_back(var);
    92→        }
    93→    };
    94→    collectVars(globalAndStaticVars);
    95→
    96→    auto collectFuncs = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& candidateFuncs) {
    97→        for (auto& func : candidateFuncs) {
    98→            if (func->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::MAIN_ENTRY) || func->identifier == MAIN_INVOKE) {
    99→                continue;
   100→            }
   101→            funcsAndVars.AddElement(func);
   102→        }
   103→    };
   104→    collectFuncs(globalAndMemberFuncs);
   105→}
   106→
   107→void AST2CHIR::CollectLocalConstFuncAndVars(const AST::Package& pkg)
   108→{
   109→    CollectLocalConstDecl collector;
   110→    collector.Collect(globalAndStaticVars, true);
   111→    collector.Collect(globalAndMemberFuncs, true);
   112→
   113→    /*  some const decl in member var can't be collected by visiting `init` func
   114→        class CA {
   115→            var b = { => const a = 1 }
   116→        }
   117→        member var `b` has default value, its default value doesn't show in CA.init func
   118→    */
   119→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> instanceMemberVars;
   120→    for (auto& decl : nominalDecls) {
   121→        for (auto member : decl->GetMemberDeclPtrs()) {
   122→            if (member->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL && !member->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::STATIC)) {
   123→                instanceMemberVars.emplace_back(member);
   124→            }
   125→        }
   126→    }
   127→    collector.Collect(instanceMemberVars, true);
   128→
   129→    /*  some local func decl can't be collected by visiting its outer decl
   130→        func foo() {
   131→            const func goo<T>() {}
   132→            goo<Int32>()
   133→        }
   134→        we can only collect goo's generic declare by visiting func foo, goo's instantiated declare can't be seen
   135→        goo's instantiated declare can only be seen in `pkg.genericInstantiatedDecls`
   136→    */
   137→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> instLocalconstFuncs;
   138→    for (auto& decl : pkg.genericInstantiatedDecls) {
   139→        // we only collect local const func decl
   140→        if (decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL && decl->IsConst() &&
   141→            IsLocalFunc(*StaticCast<AST::FuncDecl*>(decl.get()))) {
   142→            instLocalconstFuncs.emplace_back(StaticCast<AST::FuncDecl*>(decl.get()));
   143→        }
   144→    }
   145→    collector.Collect(instLocalconstFuncs, false);
   146→
   147→    for (const auto decl : collector.GetLocalConstFuncDecls()) {
   148→        localConstFuncs.AddElement(decl);
   149→    }
   150→    for (const auto decl : collector.GetLocalConstVarDecls()) {
   151→        localConstVars.AddElement(decl);
   152→    }
   153→}
   154→
   155→std::pair<InitOrder, bool> AST2CHIR::SortGlobalVarDecl(const AST::Package& pkg)
   156→{
   157→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "SortGlobalVarDecl");
   158→
   159→    CollectStaticInitFuncInfo();
   160→    CollectFuncsAndVars();
   161→    CollectLocalConstFuncAndVars(pkg);
   162→
   163→    ElementList<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> nodesWithDeps;
   164→    for (auto element : funcsAndVars.stableOrderValue) {
   165→        // We will skip those non-recompiled decls in incremental compilation cause they will have no body to be
   166→        // analyze, but the desugar generated `$init` should be kept specially cause it has body
   167→        if (kind == IncreKind::INCR && !element->toBeCompiled && element->identifier != STATIC_INIT_VAR) {
   168→            continue;
   169→        }
   170→        nodesWithDeps.AddElement(element);
   171→    }
   172→
   173→    auto analysis = GlobalDeclAnalysis(
   174→        diag, gim, kind, funcsAndVars, localConstVars, staticInitFuncInfoMap, outputCHIR, mergingSpecific);
   175→    auto initOrder = analysis.Run(nodesWithDeps, fileAndVarMap, cachedInfo);
   176→
   177→    // Speically, now we want to flattern the local const VarWithPattern decl which will be useful in translation later.
   178→    // Also we need to set these local const vars with `Recompile` flag for the sake of incremental compilation.
   179→    ElementList<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> flatternedLocalConstVars;
   180→    for (auto& element : localConstVars.stableOrderValue) {
   181→        if (element->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL) {
   182→            (const_cast<AST::Decl*>(element.get()))->toBeCompiled = true;
   183→            flatternedLocalConstVars.AddElement(element);
   184→        } else if (auto varWithPattern = DynamicCast<const AST::VarWithPatternDecl*>(element)) {
   185→            (const_cast<AST::VarWithPatternDecl*>(varWithPattern))->toBeCompiled = true;
   186→            auto allPatterns = FlattenVarWithPatternDecl(*varWithPattern);
   187→            for (auto pattern : allPatterns) {
   188→                if (pattern->astKind != AST::ASTKind::VAR_PATTERN) {
   189→                    continue;
   190→                }
   191→                auto varPattern = StaticCast<AST::VarPattern*>(pattern);
   192→                varPattern->varDecl->toBeCompiled = true;
   193→                flatternedLocalConstVars.AddElement(varPattern->varDecl);
   194→            }
   195→        }
   196→    }
   197→    localConstVars = std::move(flatternedLocalConstVars);
   198→
   199→    // If we find circular dependency, return false
   200→    bool result = diag.GetErrorCount() == 0;
   201→    return std::make_pair(initOrder, result);
   202→}
   203→
   204→void AST2CHIR::CreateGlobalVarSignature(const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls, bool isLocalConst)
   205→{
   206→    for (auto& decl : decls) {
   207→        CJC_ASSERT(decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL || decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_WITH_PATTERN_DECL);
   208→        if (decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL) {
   209→            CreateAndCacheGlobalVar(*StaticCast<const AST::VarDecl*>(decl), isLocalConst);
   210→        } else if (decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_WITH_PATTERN_DECL) {
   211→            FlatternPattern(*(StaticCast<const AST::VarWithPatternDecl*>(decl)->irrefutablePattern), isLocalConst);
   212→        }
   213→    }
   214→}
   215→
   216→void AST2CHIR::FlatternPattern(const AST::Pattern& pattern, bool isLocalConst)
   217→{
   218→    switch (pattern.astKind) {
   219→        case AST::ASTKind::VAR_PATTERN: {
   220→            auto varPattern = StaticCast<const AST::VarPattern*>(&pattern);
   221→            auto varDecl = varPattern->varDecl.get();
   222→            CreateAndCacheGlobalVar(*varDecl, isLocalConst);
   223→            break;
   224→        }
   225→        case AST::ASTKind::TUPLE_PATTERN: {
   226→            auto tuplePattern = StaticCast<const AST::TuplePattern*>(&pattern);
   227→            for (auto& subPattern : tuplePattern->patterns) {
   228→                FlatternPattern(*subPattern, isLocalConst);
   229→            }
   230→            break;
   231→        }
   232→        case AST::ASTKind::ENUM_PATTERN: {
   233→            auto enumPattern = StaticCast<const AST::EnumPattern*>(&pattern);
   234→            for (auto& subPattern : enumPattern->patterns) {
   235→                FlatternPattern(*subPattern, isLocalConst);
   236→            }
   237→            break;
   238→        }
   239→        case AST::ASTKind::WILDCARD_PATTERN: {
   240→            break;
   241→        }
   242→        default: {
   243→            Errorln("decl with unsupported pattern");
   244→            CJC_ABORT();
   245→        }
   246→    }
   247→}
   248→
   249→void AST2CHIR::SetInitFuncForStaticVar()
   250→{
   251→    for (auto& skipedStaticVar : varsInitedByStaticInitFunc) {
   252→        // If common var with specific one, need to skip
   253→        auto skipedStaticVarVal = globalCache.TryGet(*skipedStaticVar);
   254→        if (skipedStaticVarVal == nullptr || skipedStaticVar->specificImplementation) {
   255→            continue;
   256→        }
   257→        CJC_ASSERT(skipedStaticVar->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL);
   258→        // Also set the init func here
   259→        if (auto skipedStaticVarInCHIR = DynamicCast<GlobalVar*>(skipedStaticVarVal)) {
   260→            auto staticInitFuncInAST = staticInitFuncInfoMap.at(skipedStaticVar->outerDecl).staticInitFunc;
   261→            auto staticInitFuncInCHIR = DynamicCast<Func*>(globalCache.Get(*staticInitFuncInAST));
   262→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(staticInitFuncInCHIR);
   263→            skipedStaticVarInCHIR->SetInitFunc(*staticInitFuncInCHIR);
   264→        }
   265→    }
   266→}
   267→
   268→Translator AST2CHIR::CreateTranslator()
   269→{
   270→    return Translator{builder, chirType, opts, gim, globalCache, localConstVars, localConstFuncs, kind,
   271→        deserializedVals, annoFactoryFuncs, maybeUnreachable, isComputingAnnos, initFuncsForAnnoFactory, types};
   272→}
   273→
   274→void AST2CHIR::TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   275→{
   276→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateInitOfGlobalVars");
   277→    auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   278→    GlobalVarInitializer initializer(trans, importManager, initFuncsForConstVar, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   279→    initializer.Run(pkg, initOrder);
   280→    SetInitFuncForStaticVar();
   281→}
   282→
   283→void AST2CHIR::CollectTopLevelDecls(AST::Package& pkg)
   284→{
   285→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "CollectTopLevelDecls");
   286→    // For some special functions, they are explicitly imported even they are NOT explicitly used.
   287→    // Collect implicit imported/used decl, the decl list is made by
   288→    // `REG_IMPLICIT_IMPORTED_NON_GENERIC_FUNC` and `REG_IMPLICIT_IMPORTED_GENERIC_FUNC`,there are two cases:
   289→    //   1. if `pkg` is not std.core, we collect implicit imported decls, especially those generic decl in std.core, but
   290→    //   instantiated decls in other imported package.
   291→    //   2. if `pkg` is std.core (aka we are compiling std.core), we collect implicit used decls by down stream package.
   292→    CollectImplicitFuncs();
   293→
   294→    // Collect Imported Pkg Top-Level Decl Part
   295→    CollectImportedDecls(pkg);
   296→
   297→    // Collect Current Pkg Top-Level Decl & Generic Top-Level Decl Part
   298→    CollectDeclsInCurPkg(pkg);
   299→}
   300→
   301→void AST2CHIR::CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable()
   302→{
   303→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable");
   304→    // translate all custom type decl, and cache them to global symbol table
   305→    // only create a shell of `CustomTypeDef`, including its ptr and attribute, not fill its method, vtable and so on
   306→    CacheCustomTypeDefToGlobalSymbolTable();
   307→    // translate all custom type's type, and set type to `CustomTypeDef`
   308→    TranslateAllCustomTypeTy();
   309→    // create all top-level func decl's shell and var decls, cache them to global symbol table.
   310→    CacheTopLevelDeclToGlobalSymbolTable();
   311→
   312→    SetGenericDecls();
   313→}
   314→
   315→void AST2CHIR::SetGenericDecls() const
   316→{
   317→    if (!gim) {
   318→        return;
   319→    }
   320→    auto genericToInsMap = gim->GetAllGenericToInsDecls();
   321→    for (auto& mapIt : genericToInsMap) {
   322→        if (mapIt.first->astKind == AST::ASTKind::EXTEND_DECL) {
   323→            continue;
   324→        }
   325→        if (mapIt.first->IsNominalDecl()) {
   326→            auto chirGeneric = chirType.TryGetGlobalNominalCache(*mapIt.first);
   327→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(chirGeneric);
   328→            for (auto insDecl : mapIt.second) {
   329→                auto chirIns = chirType.TryGetGlobalNominalCache(*insDecl);
   330→                // instantiated decl may be imported but not used in current package, so it's not translated by CHIR
   331→                if (chirIns == nullptr) {
   332→                    continue;
   333→                }
   334→                chirIns->SetGenericDecl(*chirGeneric);
   335→            }
   336→        } else if (mapIt.first->astKind == AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL) {
   337→            auto chirGeneric = globalCache.TryGet(*mapIt.first);
   338→            // intrinsic
   339→            if (chirGeneric == nullptr) {
   340→                continue;
   341→            }
   342→            for (auto insDecl : mapIt.second) {
   343→                auto chirIns = globalCache.TryGet(*insDecl);
   344→                // shouldn't be nullptr
   345→                if (chirIns == nullptr) {
   346→                    continue;
   347→                }
   348→                VirtualCast<FuncBase*>(chirIns)->SetGenericDecl(*VirtualCast<FuncBase*>(chirGeneric));
   349→            }
   350→        }
   351→    }
   352→}
   353→
   354→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseFuncBody(const AST::Decl& decl)
   355→{
   356→    if (decl.astKind != AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL) {
   357→        return;
   358→    }
   359→    // const_cast is safe: we own the AST tree and are past the translation point for this decl.
   360→    auto& funcDecl = const_cast<AST::FuncDecl&>(static_cast<const AST::FuncDecl&>(decl));
   361→    if (funcDecl.funcBody != nullptr && funcDecl.funcBody->body != nullptr) {
   362→        funcDecl.funcBody->body.reset();
   363→    }
   364→}
   365→
   366→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseVarInitializer(AST::VarDeclAbstract& decl)
   367→{
   368→    if (decl.initializer != nullptr) {
   369→        decl.initializer.reset();
   370→    }
   371→}
   372→
   373→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(const AST::Package& /* pkg */)
   374→{
   375→    // Release method bodies from nominal decls (class/interface/struct/enum) after batch translation.
   376→    // Uses GetMemberDecls() which is the canonical way to access members across all nominal types.
   377→    auto releaseMethodBodies = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls) {
   378→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   379→            auto& memberDecls = decl->GetMemberDecls();
   380→            for (auto& member : memberDecls) {
   381→                ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   382→            }
   383→        }
   384→    };
   385→    releaseMethodBodies(nominalDecls);
   386→    releaseMethodBodies(genericNominalDecls);
   387→}
   388→
   389→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(const InitOrder& initOrder)
   390→{
   391→    for (auto& [file, decls] : initOrder) {
   392→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   393→            if (auto* varDecl = DynamicCast<AST::VarDeclAbstract*>(const_cast<AST::Decl*>(decl.get()))) {
   394→                ReleaseVarInitializer(*varDecl);
   395→            }
   396→        }
   397→    }
   398→}
   399→
   400→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies()
   401→{
   402→    for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   403→        if (NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   404→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   405→        }
   406→    }
   407→    for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   408→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   409→    }
   410→}
   411→
   412→void AST2CHIR::TranslateAllDecls(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   413→{
   414→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "TranslateAllDecls");
   415→    // step 1: translate nominal decls first (signatures only — method bodies are translated in step 3)
   416→    TranslateNominalDecls(pkg);
   417→    // NOTE: Do NOT call ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies() here.
   418→    // TranslateNominalDecls only translates signatures (types, params, attributes).
   419→    // Method bodies are translated in step 3 via globalAndMemberFuncs, and released there
   420→    // by ReleaseFuncBody (serial) or ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies (parallel).
   421→    // Releasing here would null funcBody->body before step 3 translates it,
   422→    // causing null pointer dereference in HasDelegatedThisCall / TranslateNestedFunc.
   423→
   424→    // step 2: translate initialization of global var
   425→    TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(pkg, initOrder);
   426→    ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(initOrder);
   427→
   428→    // do this after init of gv to ensure gvinit of CustomAnnotations go after real gv's
   429→    // this is always safe because such gvinit's are generated by CHIR and cannot be referenced in source
   430→    for (auto decl : annoOnlyDecls) {
   431→        CreateAnnoOnlyDeclSig(*decl);
   432→    }
   433→
   434→    // step 3: translate body of all funcs, the process can be run in parallel according to the compilation option
   435→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   436→    if (opts.GetJobs() > 1) {
   437→        TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel();
   438→        ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies();
   439→    } else {
   440→        for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   441→            if (!NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   442→                continue;
   443→            }
   444→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   445→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   446→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   447→            if (decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GLOBAL)) {
   448→                trans.CollectValueAnnotation(*decl);
   449→            }
   450→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   451→        }
   452→        for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   453→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   454→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   455→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   456→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   457→        }
   458→    }
   459→    // the parallel helper does not accept this type, use serialised translation
   460→    for (auto decl : annoFactoryFuncs) {
   461→        auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   462→        trans.SetTopLevel(*decl.first);
   463→        trans.TranslateAnnoFactoryFuncBody(*decl.first, *decl.second);
   464→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl.first);
   465→    }
   466→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   467→
   468→    // step 4: set `CompileTimeValue` for lambda — operates on CHIR IR, unaffected by AST release
   469→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   470→    for (auto func : package->GetGlobalFuncs()) {
   471→        if (func->TestAttr(Attribute::CONST)) {
   472→            SetCompileTimeValueFlagRecursivly(*func);
   473→        }
   474→    }
   475→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   476→}
   477→
   478→void AST2CHIR::TranslateInParallel(const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls)
   479→{
   480→    Utils::ParallelUtil allDeclsParallel(builder, opts.GetJobs());
   481→    allDeclsParallel.RunAST2CHIRInParallel(decls, chirType, opts, gim, globalCache, localConstVars, localConstFuncs,
   482→        kind, deserializedVals, Translator::TranslateASTNode, maybeUnreachable, isComputingAnnos,
   483→        initFuncsForAnnoFactory, types, annoFactoryFuncs);
   484→}
   485→
   486→void AST2CHIR::TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel()
   487→{
   488→    // collect all top-level funcs into a vector.
   489→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> allDecls;
   490→    auto needTrans = [this](Ptr<const AST::Decl> decl) { return NeedTranslate(*decl); };
   491→    // Filter out decls that do not require translation.
   492→    std::copy_if(globalAndMemberFuncs.begin(), globalAndMemberFuncs.end(),
   493→        std::back_inserter(allDecls), needTrans);
   494→    TranslateInParallel(allDecls);
   495→
   496→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> localFuncsGeneric; // generic decls
   497→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> localFuncsOther; // instantiated or non-generic decls
   498→    for (auto func : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   499→        if (func->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GENERIC)) {
   500→            localFuncsGeneric.push_back(func);
   501→        } else {
   502→            localFuncsOther.push_back(func);
   503→        }
   504→    }
   505→    TranslateInParallel(localFuncsGeneric);
   506→    TranslateInParallel(localFuncsOther);
   507→}
   508→
   509→void AST2CHIR::AST2CHIRCheck()
   510→{
   511→    if (!opts.chirWFC) {
   512→        return;
   513→    }
   514→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "AST2CHIRCheck");
   515→    // check customDefTypes
   516→    auto customDefMap = chirType.GetAllTypeDef();
   517→    for (auto& it : customDefMap) {
   518→        const AST::Node& astNode = *it.first;
   519→        const CHIR::CustomTypeDef& chirNode = *it.second;
   520→        if (astNode.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GENERIC, AST::Attribute::IMPORTED)) {
   521→            continue;
   522→        }
   523→        if (astNode.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::IMPORTED) && chirNode.TestAttr(Attribute::DESERIALIZED)) {
   524→            continue;
   525→        }
   526→        if (chirNode.TestAttr(Attribute::SKIP_ANALYSIS)) {
   527→            continue;
   528→        }
   529→        auto ret = AST2CHIRCheckCustomTypeDef(astNode, chirNode, globalCache);
   530→        if (!ret) {
   531→            this->failure = true;
   532→            it.second->Dump();
   533→        }
   534→    }
   535→    // check globalFunc and globalVar
   536→    for (auto& it : globalCache.GetALL()) {
   537→        if (it.second->TestAttr(Attribute::SKIP_ANALYSIS)) {
   538→            continue;
   539→        }
   540→        auto ret = AST2CHIRCheckValue(*it.first, *it.second);
   541→        if (!ret) {
   542→            this->failure = true;
   543→            it.second->Dump();
   544→        }
   545→    }
   546→}
   547→
   548→/// Return true if chir was deserialized
   549→bool AST2CHIR::TryToDeserializeCHIR()
   550→{
   551→    auto& chirFiles = opts.inputChirFiles;
   552→    CJC_ASSERT(chirFiles.size() != 0);
   553→    ToCHIR::Phase phase;
   554→    bool success = true;
   555→    for (auto chirFile : chirFiles) {
   556→        success &= CHIRDeserializer::Deserialize(chirFile, builder, phase, true);
   557→        mergingSpecific = true;
   558→    }
   559→    return success;
   560→}
   561→
   562→static Package::AccessLevel BuildPackageAccessLevel(const AST::AccessLevel& level)
   563→{
   564→    static std::unordered_map<AST::AccessLevel, Package::AccessLevel> accessLevelMap = {
   565→        {AST::AccessLevel::INTERNAL, Package::AccessLevel::INTERNAL},
   566→        {AST::AccessLevel::PROTECTED, Package::AccessLevel::PROTECTED},
   567→        {AST::AccessLevel::PUBLIC, Package::AccessLevel::PUBLIC},
   568→    };
   569→
   570→    auto it = accessLevelMap.find(level);
   571→    CJC_ASSERT(it != accessLevelMap.end());
   572→    return it->second;
   573→}
   574→
   575→bool AST2CHIR::ToCHIRPackage(AST::Package& node)
   576→{
   577→    // It can be not null in case of part of the package was deserialized from .chir
   578→    bool needDesCHIR = opts.inputChirFiles.size() != 0;
   579→    if (!needDesCHIR) {
   580→        package = builder.CreatePackage(node.fullPackageName);
   581→        outputCHIR = opts.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR;
   582→    } else if (TryToDeserializeCHIR()) {
   583→        package = builder.GetCurPackage();
   584→        BuildDeserializedTable();
   585→    } else {
   586→        return false;
   587→    }
   588→    // Translating common alongside with merging specific is not supported
   589→    CJC_ASSERT(!(outputCHIR && mergingSpecific));
   590→    package->SetPackageAccessLevel(BuildPackageAccessLevel(node.accessible));
   591→    RegisterAllSources();
   592→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(package);
   593→    dependencyPkg = importManager.GetAllDependentPackageNames(node.fullPackageName);
   594→
   595→    // step 1: collect all top-level decls
   596→    CollectTopLevelDecls(node);
   597→
   598→    // step 2: sort and do circular dependency checking
   599→    auto [initOrder, result] = SortGlobalVarDecl(node);
   600→    if (!result) {
   601→        return false;
   602→    }
   603→
   604→    // step 3: create signature of nominal decls and top-level func decls
   605→    CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable();
   606→
   607→    // step 4: translate all colleted decls
   608→    TranslateAllDecls(node, initOrder);
   609→
   610→    // step 5: ast2chir check
   611→    AST2CHIRCheck();
   612→
   613→    return !HasFailed();
   614→}
   615→} // namespace Cangjie::CHIR
   616→
```

     6→
     7→/**
     8→ * @file
     9→ *
    10→ * This file implements the IncrementalCompilerInstance.
    11→ */
    12→
    13→#include "cangjie/FrontendTool/IncrementalCompilerInstance.h"
    14→#include <sstream>
    15→
    16→#include "cangjie/AST/Utils.h"
    17→#include "cangjie/Basic/StringConvertor.h"
    18→#include "cangjie/Basic/Version.h"
    19→#include "cangjie/Driver/TempFileManager.h"

    39→using namespace Cangjie;
    40→using namespace AST;
    41→
    42→IncrementalCompilerInstance::~IncrementalCompilerInstance()
    43→{
    44→}
    45→
    46→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::InitCompilerInstance()
    47→{
    48→    return CompilerInstance::InitCompilerInstance();
    49→}
    50→
    51→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::SaveCompilationResult(Cangjie::IncreResult&& result)
    52→{
    53→    kind = result.kind;
    54→    rawMangleName2DeclMap = result.mangle2decl;
    55→    switch (kind) {
    56→        case IncreKind::ROLLBACK:
    57→            declsToBeReCompiled.clear();
    58→            [[fallthrough]];
    59→        case IncreKind::INCR:
    60→            cachedInfo = std::move(result.cacheInfo);
    61→            CacheCompileArgs();
    62→            declsToBeReCompiled = std::move(result.declsToRecompile);
    63→            rawIncrRemovedDecls = std::move(result.deleted);
    64→            // Copy a non-const version for 'Sema' usage.
    65→            for (auto& [mangle, decl] : result.mangle2decl) {
    66→                if (!decl->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPORTED)) {
    67→                    mangledName2DeclMap.emplace(mangle, Ptr(const_cast<Decl*>(decl.get())));
    68→                }
    69→            }
    70→            for (auto changed : declsToBeReCompiled) {
    71→                if (changed->TestAttr(Attribute::IMPORTED) && (changed->IsFunc() || IsGlobalOrStaticVar(*changed))) {
    72→                    cacheMangles.EmplaceImportedInlineDeclPtr(*changed);
    73→                } else {
    74→                    Sema::CollectRemovedManglesForReCompile(*changed, cachedInfo.semaInfo,
    75→                        cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls);
    76→                }
    77→            }
    78→            for (auto removed : rawIncrRemovedDecls) {
    79→                Sema::CollectRemovedMangles(removed, cachedInfo.semaInfo, cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls);
    80→            }
    81→            // NOTE: since 'declsToBeReCompiled' and 'rawIncrRemovedDecls' have been process,
    82→            // this loop will only remove the re-boxed built-in types' related decls.
    83→            for (auto typeMangle : result.reBoxedTypes) {
    84→                Sema::CollectRemovedMangles(typeMangle, cachedInfo.semaInfo, cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls);
    85→            }
    86→            break;
    87→        case IncreKind::NO_CHANGE:
    88→            cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName = std::move(result.cacheInfo.bitcodeFilesName);
    89→            break;
    90→        case IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG:
    91→            break;
    92→        case IncreKind::INVALID:
    93→            CJC_ABORT();
    94→            break;
    95→    }
    96→}
    97→
    98→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
    99→namespace {
   100→std::optional<size_t> GetCachedSplitNum(const std::string& cachedCodeGenPath)
   101→{
   102→    std::optional<size_t> splitNum{std::nullopt};
   103→    llvm::SMDiagnostic err;
   104→    auto context = llvm::LLVMContext();
   105→#ifdef _WIN32
   106→    auto tempPath = StringConvertor::NormalizeStringToUTF8(cachedCodeGenPath);
   107→    CJC_ASSERT(tempPath.has_value() && "Incorrect file name encoding.");
   108→    auto module = llvm::parseIRFile(tempPath.value(), err, context);
   109→#else
   110→    auto module = llvm::parseIRFile(cachedCodeGenPath, err, context);
   111→#endif
   112→    if (module == nullptr) {
   113→        Errorln("Illegal cached codegen info detected during incremental compilation.");
   114→        return splitNum;
   115→    }
   116→    auto splitNumMD = module->getNamedMetadata("splitNum");
   117→    for (llvm::MDNode* mdNode : splitNumMD->operands()) {
   118→        auto numMD = llvm::cast<llvm::ConstantAsMetadata>(mdNode->getOperand(0));
   119→        splitNum = llvm::cast<llvm::ConstantInt>(numMD->getValue())->getZExtValue();
   120→    }
   121→    return splitNum;
   122→}
   123→
   124→bool CheckCachedBitcode(const std::string& packageName, size_t splitNum, const GlobalOptions& globalOp)
   125→{
   126→    if (splitNum == 0) {
   127→        return false;
   128→    }
   129→    for (size_t i = 0; i < splitNum; ++i) {
   130→        std::string cachedBcPath =
   131→            globalOp.GenerateCachedPathNameForCodeGen(std::to_string(i) + '-' + packageName, "_cache.bc");
   132→        if (!FileUtil::FileExist(cachedBcPath)) {
   133→            IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   134→                "the cached bitcode file is lost." + cachedBcPath + " index " + std::to_string(i));
   135→            return false;
   136→        }
   137→    }
   138→    return true;
   139→}
   140→
   141→bool CheckCachedBitcodeInfo(const std::string& packageName, const GlobalOptions& options)
   142→{
   143→    auto cgCachePath = options.GenerateCachedPathNameForCodeGen(packageName, ".cgCache");
   144→    if (!FileUtil::FileExist(cgCachePath)) {
   145→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   146→            "load cached codegen info failed, roll back to full compilation");
   147→        return false;
   148→    }
   149→    auto splitNum = GetCachedSplitNum(cgCachePath);
   150→    if (!splitNum.has_value()) {
   151→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn("get cached split num failed, roll back to full compilation");
   152→        return false;
   153→    }
   154→    bool bcCachedGood = CheckCachedBitcode(packageName, splitNum.value(), options);
   155→    if (!bcCachedGood) {
   156→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   157→            "load cached bitcode file failed, roll back to full compilation");
   158→        return false;
   159→    }
   160→    return true;
   161→}
   162→
   163→bool CheckCachedObjFile(const GlobalOptions& options, CompilationCache& cachedInfo)
   164→{
   165→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   166→    for (const auto& fileName : cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName) {
   167→        auto objFile = options.GetHashedObjFileName(fileName) + ".o";
   168→        if (!FileUtil::FileExist(objFile)) {
   169→            logger.LogLn("cached obj file not exist, roll back to full compilation");
   170→            return false;
   171→        }
   172→    }
   173→    return true;
   174→}
   175→
   176→bool CheckCachedBitcodeInfoForLTO(const GlobalOptions& options, CompilationCache& cachedInfo)
   177→{
   178→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   179→    for (const auto& fileName : cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName) {
   180→        auto objFile = options.GetHashedObjFileName(FileUtil::GetFileNameWithoutExtension(fileName)) + ".bc";
   181→        if (!FileUtil::FileExist(objFile)) {
   182→            logger.LogLn("load cached bitcode file for opt failed, roll back to full compilation");
   183→            return false;
   184→        }
   185→    }
   186→    return true;
   187→}
   188→
   189→} // namespace
   190→#endif
   191→
   192→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformIncrementalScopeAnalysis()
   193→{
   194→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   195→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "AST Diff");
   196→    CJC_ASSERT(srcPkgs.size() == 1);
   197→    auto& package = srcPkgs[0];
   198→
   199→    // calculate the AST cache info
   200→    bool res = CalculateASTCache();
   201→    if (!res) {
   202→        return true;
   203→    }
   204→
   205→    auto& options = invocation.globalOptions;
   206→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   207→    if (!options.pluginPaths.empty()) {
   208→        kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   209→        Warningf("`--incremental-compile` is incompatible with `--plugin` and will be ignored.\n");
   210→        return true;
   211→    }
   212→#endif
   213→
   214→    if (!declsWithDuplicatedRawMangleName.empty()) {
   215→        kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   216→        IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().LogLn(
   217→            "illegal source code leads to duplicated raw mangle name, roll back to full compilation");
   218→        return true;
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    auto increRes = IncrementalScopeAnalysis({rawMangleName2DeclMap, std::move(astCacheInfo), *package, options,
   222→                                                 importManager, cachedInfo, fileMap, std::move(directExtends)});
   223→    if (increRes.kind == IncreKind::INCR) {
   224→        // check cached bitcode infos
   225→        const std::string& packageName = package->fullPackageName;
   226→        bool isCachedBitcodeGood = CheckCachedBitcodeInfo(packageName, options);
   227→        if (!isCachedBitcodeGood) {
   228→            increRes.kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   229→        } else {
   230→            // set deleted mangles Name for codegen
   231→            cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.insert(
   232→                increRes.deletedMangleNames.begin(), increRes.deletedMangleNames.end());
   233→        }
   234→    }
   235→    if (increRes.kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   236→        // check cached obj file
   237→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   238→            options.UpdateCachedDirName(srcPkg->fullPackageName);
   239→        }
   240→        if (!options.IsLTOEnabled() && !CheckCachedObjFile(options, increRes.cacheInfo)) {
   241→            increRes.kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   242→        }
   243→        if (options.IsLTOEnabled() && !CheckCachedBitcodeInfoForLTO(options, increRes.cacheInfo)) {
   244→            increRes.kind = IncreKind::ROLLBACK;
   245→        }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    increRes.Dump();
   249→    SaveCompilationResult(std::move(increRes));
   250→#endif
   251→    return true;
   252→}
   253→
   254→static bool HasSimpleInitialiser(const AST::VarDecl& decl)
   255→{
   256→    auto& init = decl.initializer;
   257→    if (!init) {
   258→        return false;
   259→    }
   260→    if (init->astKind == ASTKind::LIT_CONST_EXPR) {
   261→        auto kind = StaticCast<LitConstExpr>(init.get())->kind;
   262→        return kind != LitConstKind::JSTRING && kind != LitConstKind::UNIT;
   263→    }
   264→    return false;
   265→}
   266→
   267→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformSema()
   268→{
   269→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Semantic");
   270→    if (auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance(); logger.IsEnable()) {
   271→        std::string message = kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE
   272→            ? "no change, skip sema"
   273→            : (kind == IncreKind::ROLLBACK ? "full sema" : "incremental sema");
   274→        logger.LogLn(message);
   275→    }
   276→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   277→        return true;
   278→    } else if (kind == IncreKind::ROLLBACK) {
   279→        return CompilerInstance::PerformSema();
   280→    }
   281→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(typeManager);
   282→    // Load cached types. Should only exist exactly one source package.
   283→    for (auto srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   284→        srcPkg->EnableAttr(Attribute::INCRE_COMPILE);
   285→        Sema::HandleCtorForIncr(*srcPkg, mangledName2DeclMap, cachedInfo.semaInfo);
   286→        cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.merge(importManager.LoadCachedTypeForPackage(*srcPkg, mangledName2DeclMap));
   287→    }
   288→    Sema::MarkIncrementalCheckForCtor(declsToBeReCompiled);
   289→
   290→    auto visit = [](Decl& decl) {
   291→        // NOTE: Avoid some sema rules to be rechecked.
   292→        // To guarantee the member decls will be checked, the type decl cannot be marked with following attributes.
   293→        if (!decl.IsNominalDecl() && decl.astKind != ASTKind::PROP_DECL) {
   294→            decl.EnableAttr(Attribute::IS_CHECK_VISITED, Attribute::INITIALIZED, Attribute::INITIALIZATION_CHECKED,
   295→                Attribute::INCRE_COMPILE);
   296→        }
   297→        // Remove body to avoid walker walk-in.
   298→        if (auto fd = DynamicCast<FuncDecl*>(&decl); fd && fd->funcBody) {
   299→            fd->funcBody->body.reset();
   300→            return;
   301→        }
   302→        if (auto vd = DynamicCast<VarDecl*>(&decl)) {
   303→            if (!vd->initializer) {
   304→                return;
   305→            }
   306→            vd->EnableAttr(Attribute::DEFAULT);
   307→            if (HasSimpleInitialiser(*vd)) {
   308→                vd->DisableAttr(Attribute::IS_CHECK_VISITED);
   309→            }
   310→        }
   311→        // PropDecl's getter/setter will be counted separately and should not be cleared from propDecl.
   312→    };
   313→    for (auto& [_, decl] : mangledName2DeclMap) {
   314→        if (!decl->toBeCompiled && !IsInDeclWithAttribute(*decl, Attribute::GENERIC) && Ty::IsTyCorrect(decl->ty) &&
   315→            (decl->astKind != ASTKind::FUNC_DECL || !decl->TestAttr(Attribute::DEFAULT))) {
   316→        // NOTE: for now, generic definitions and default implementations should be kept for code re-generation.
   317→            visit(*decl);
   318→        }
   319→    }
   320→    return CompilerInstance::PerformSema();
   321→}
   322→
   323→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformOverflowStrategy()
   324→{
   325→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Overflow Strategy");
   326→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   327→        return true;
   328→    }
   329→    return CompilerInstance::PerformOverflowStrategy();
   330→}
   331→
   332→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformDesugarAfterSema()
   333→{
   334→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Desugar after Sema");
   335→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   336→        return true;
   337→    }
   338→    return CompilerInstance::PerformDesugarAfterSema();
   339→}
   340→
   341→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformGenericInstantiation()
   342→{
   343→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Generic Instantiation");
   344→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   345→        return true;
   346→    }
   347→    bool ret = CompilerInstance::PerformGenericInstantiation();
   348→    if (ret) {
   349→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   350→            changedTypes.merge(Sema::CollectChangedStructTypes(*srcPkg, declsToBeReCompiled));
   351→            IterateAllExportableDecls(*srcPkg, [this](auto& decl) {
   352→                // If non-export function/variable is marked as external linkage, codegen should change its linkage.
   353→                if (!decl.IsExportedDecl() && decl.linkage == Linkage::EXTERNAL && !decl.mangledName.empty()) {
   354→                    cacheMangles.newExternalDecls.emplace(decl.mangledName);
   355→                }
   356→            });
   357→        }
   358→    }
   359→    return ret;
   360→}
   361→
   362→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformMangling()
   363→{
   364→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   365→        return true;
   366→    }
   367→    bool success = DefaultCompilerInstance::PerformMangling();
   368→    if (success) {
   369→        // mangle of full exported decl is empty in cjo, we need update it after mangling.
   370→        cacheMangles.UpdateImportedInlineDeclsMangle();
   371→    }
   372→    return success;
   373→}
   374→
   375→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::UpdateCachedInfo()
   376→{
   377→    UpdateMangleNameForCachedInfo();
   378→    UpdateCHIROptEffectMap();
   379→    if (kind == IncreKind::ROLLBACK) {
   380→        cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep = std::move(chirInfo.curVirtFuncWrapDep);
   381→        cachedInfo.ccOutFuncs = std::move(chirInfo.ccOutFuncsRawMangle);
   382→        cachedInfo.varInitDepMap = std::move(chirInfo.varInitDepMap);
   383→    } else if (kind == IncreKind::INCR) {
   384→        for (auto& [raw, _] : chirInfo.delVirtFuncWrapForIncr) {
   385→            cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep.erase(raw);
   386→        }
   387→        for (auto& [raw, warp] : chirInfo.curVirtFuncWrapDep) {
   388→            cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep[raw] = warp;
   389→        }
   390→        for (auto& rm : std::as_const(rawIncrRemovedDecls)) {
   391→            cachedInfo.varInitDepMap.erase(rm);
   392→        }
   393→        for (auto& [raw, warp] : chirInfo.varInitDepMap) {
   394→            cachedInfo.varInitDepMap[raw] = warp;
   395→        }
   396→        cachedInfo.ccOutFuncs.merge(std::move(chirInfo.ccOutFuncsRawMangle));
   397→    }
   398→    // Update usage of compiler added.
   399→    for (auto pkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   400→        Sema::CollectCompilerAddedDeclUsage(*pkg, cachedInfo.semaInfo);
   401→    }
   402→}
   403→
   404→namespace Cangjie {
   405→/// implemented in IncrementalScopeAnalysis
   406→void MergeCHIROptEffectMap(
   407→    const OptEffectStrMap& newMap, OptEffectStrMap& lastCachedMap, const RawMangled2DeclMap& rawMangled2Decl);
   408→void DeleteRemovedNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(const std::list<std::string>& removedDecls, OptEffectStrMap& effectMap);
   409→void DeleteRecompiledNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(
   410→    const std::unordered_set<Ptr<AST::Decl>>& recompiledNodes, OptEffectStrMap& effectMap);
   411→}
   412→
   413→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::UpdateCHIROptEffectMap()
   414→{
   415→    DeleteRemovedNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(rawIncrRemovedDecls, cachedInfo.chirOptInfo);
   416→    DeleteRecompiledNodesInCHIROptEffectMap(declsToBeReCompiled, cachedInfo.chirOptInfo);
   417→
   418→    MergeCHIROptEffectMap(chirInfo.optEffectMap, cachedInfo.chirOptInfo, rawMangleName2DeclMap);
   419→}
   420→
   421→namespace {
   422→void UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVirtualFuncDep(CachedMangleMap& cacheMangles, std::list<std::string>& rawIncrRemovedDecls,
   423→    VirtualWrapperDepMap& virtualFuncDep, VirtualWrapperDepMap& delVirtFuncWrapForIncr)
   424→{
   425→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   426→    for (auto& delRaw : rawIncrRemovedDecls) {
   427→        if (auto it = virtualFuncDep.find(delRaw); it != virtualFuncDep.end()) {
   428→            logger.LogLn("[delVirDep][remove] raw: " + delRaw + " mg: " + it->second);
   429→            cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace(it->second);
   430→        }
   431→    }
   432→    for (auto& [delRaw, del] : delVirtFuncWrapForIncr) {
   433→        logger.LogLn("[delVirDep][change] raw: " + delRaw + " mg: " + del);
   434→        cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace(del);
   435→    }
   436→}
   437→void UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVarInitDep(CachedMangleMap& cacheMangles, std::list<std::string>& rawIncrRemovedDecls,
   438→    VarInitDepMap& varInitDepMap)
   439→{
   440→    auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance();
   441→    for (auto& delRaw : std::as_const(rawIncrRemovedDecls)) {
   442→        if (auto it = varInitDepMap.find(delRaw); it != varInitDepMap.end()) {
   443→            logger.LogLn("[delVarInitDep][remove] raw: " + delRaw + " mg: " + it->second);
   444→            cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace(it->second);
   445→        }
   446→    }
   447→}
   448→} // namespace
   449→
   450→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCHIRCompilation()
   451→{
   452→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "CHIR");
   453→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   454→        return true;
   455→    }
   456→    auto ret = CompilerInstance::PerformCHIRCompilation();
   457→    for (auto ty : chirInfo.ccTys) {
   458→        changedTypes.insert(ty);
   459→    }
   460→    if (kind == IncreKind::INCR) {
   461→        UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVirtualFuncDep(cacheMangles, rawIncrRemovedDecls, cachedInfo.virtualFuncDep,
   462→            chirInfo.delVirtFuncWrapForIncr);
   463→        UpdateIncrRemovedDeclsForVarInitDep(cacheMangles, rawIncrRemovedDecls, cachedInfo.varInitDepMap);
   464→    }
   465→    return ret;
   466→}
   467→
   468→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease()
   469→{
   470→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Release AST");
   471→
   472→    // Always extract CodeGen metadata before potential release.
   473→    PrepareCodeGenInfo();
   474→
   475→    // For NO_CHANGE / EMPTY_PKG, no AST was built — nothing to release.
   476→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   477→        return true;
   478→    }
   479→
   480→    // Save results before AST is freed (ADR-009, F-02).
   481→    // PerformResultsSaving needs srcPkgs for ExportASTSignature and SaveCjo.
   482→    if (!resultsSaved) {
   483→        if (!PerformResultsSaving()) {
   484→            return false;  // Propagate save failure to abort compilation.
   485→        }
   486→        resultsSaved = true;
   487→    }
   488→
   489→    // Write incremental compilation cache before AST is freed (ADR-009).
   490→    if (ShouldWriteCacheFile() && !cacheWritten) {
   491→        UpdateCachedInfo();
   492→        WriteCachedInfo();
   493→        cacheWritten = true;
   494→    }
   495→
   496→    // Allow skipping AST release for debugging (e.g., ASan leak analysis).
   497→    if (invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST) {
   498→        return true;
   499→    }
   500→
   501→    // Clean incremental-compilation-specific AST pointers.
   502→    changedTypes.clear();
   503→    declsToBeReCompiled.clear();
   504→    cacheMangles.Clear();
   505→
   506→    // Delegate to base class for the 5-phase cleanup.
   507→    ReleaseASTMemory();
   508→    return true;
   509→}
   510→
   511→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::LoadCachedCodegenResult() const
   512→{
   513→    for (auto fileName : cachedInfo.bitcodeFilesName) {
   514→        auto cachePath = invocation.globalOptions.GenerateCachedPathNameForCodeGen(fileName, ".bc");
   515→        TempFileInfo bcFileInfo = TempFileInfo{fileName, cachePath, "", true};
   516→        invocation.globalOptions.frontendOutputFiles.emplace_back(bcFileInfo);
   517→    }
   518→}
   519→
   520→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCodeGen()
   521→{
   522→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "CodeGen");
   523→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   524→        // Use codeGenPkgInfos if AST is released, otherwise use srcPkgs.
   525→        if (IsASTReleased()) {
   526→            for (auto& info : codeGenPkgInfos) {
   527→                LoadCachedCodegenResult();
   528→                invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(info.fullPackageName);
   529→            }
   530→        } else {
   531→            for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   532→                LoadCachedCodegenResult();
   533→                invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(srcPkg->fullPackageName);
   534→            }
   535→        }
   536→        return true;
   537→    }
   538→    // Before CodeGen, the dependency relationship of a package contains only some packages.
   539→    // So this function rearranges the dependencies of all packages.
   540→    RearrangeImportedPackageDependence();
   541→    bool ret = true;
   542→    if (IsASTReleased()) {
   543→        for (auto& info : codeGenPkgInfos) {
   544→            ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(info.fullPackageName, info.isEmpty, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   545→        }
   546→    } else {
   547→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   548→            ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(*srcPkg, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   549→        }
   550→    }
   551→    return ret;
   552→}
   553→
   554→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCjoSaving()
   555→{
   556→    if (auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance(); logger.IsEnable()) {
   557→        std::string message;
   558→        if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   559→            message = "no change, skip cjo saving";
   560→        } else if (kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   561→            message = "empty pkg, skip cjo saving";
   562→        } else if (invocation.globalOptions.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR) {
   563→            message = " chir output mode, skip cjo saving";
   564→        } else {
   565→            message = "incremental cjo saving";
   566→        }
   567→        logger.LogLn(message);
   568→    }
   569→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   570→        return true;
   571→    }
   572→
   573→    return DefaultCompilerInstance::PerformCjoSaving();
   574→}
   575→
   576→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformResultsSaving()
   577→{
   578→    if (resultsSaved) {
   579→        return true;
   580→    }
   581→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Save results");
   582→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   583→        return true;
   584→    }
   585→    bool ret = true;
   586→    for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   587→        if (invocation.globalOptions.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR) {
   588→            ret = ret && SaveCjo(*srcPkg);
   589→        }
   590→        if (ret && !srcPkg->IsEmpty()) {
   591→            // Write astData for incremental compilation in cache path.
   592→            std::string cachedCjo =
   593→                invocation.globalOptions.GenerateCachedPathName(srcPkg->fullPackageName, SERIALIZED_FILE_EXTENSION);
   594→            ret = ret && FileUtil::WriteBufferToASTFile(cachedCjo, importManager.ExportASTSignature(*srcPkg));
   595→        }
   596→    }
   597→    return ret;
   598→}
```

</details>

   326→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CODEGEN));

   333→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS));
   334→}
   335→
   336→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PipelineStageOrderIsCorrect)
   337→{
   338→    // Verify the full pipeline ordering around RELEASE_AST.
   339→    int chir = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CHIR);
   340→    int releaseAst = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::RELEASE_AST);
   341→    int codegen = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::CODEGEN);
   342→    int saveResults = static_cast<int>(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS);
   343→
   344→    EXPECT_EQ(releaseAst, chir + 1) << "RELEASE_AST must immediately follow CHIR";
   345→    EXPECT_EQ(codegen, releaseAst + 1) << "CODEGEN must immediately follow RELEASE_AST";
   346→    EXPECT_GT(saveResults, codegen) << "SAVE_RESULTS must come after CODEGEN";
   347→}

   353→              static_cast<int>(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS));

   356→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   357→// Section 9: Regression Test - BUG-01 (CJO Loss Prevention)
   358→//
   359→// BUG-01: DefaultCompilerInstance in CHIR output mode did not
   360→// call PerformResultsSaving() before ReleaseASTMemory(), causing
   361→// srcPkgs to be empty when SaveCjo ran, silently losing CJO files.
   362→//
   363→// Fix: PerformASTRelease() now calls PerformResultsSaving() before
   364→// ReleaseASTMemory(), guarded by resultsSaved flag.
   365→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   366→
   367→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG01_ResultsSavedGuardPreventsDoubleExecution)
   368→{
   369→    // Verify that the resultsSaved guard prevents double execution.
   370→    TestCIFixture f;
   371→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   372→
   373→    // Simulate first save.
   374→    f.ci->SetResultsSaved(true);
   375→    EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   376→
   377→    // The guard should prevent PerformResultsSaving from running again
   378→    // inside PerformASTRelease. We verify the flag is correctly set.
   379→    // (Full pipeline test would verify CJO file generation.)
   380→}
   381→
   382→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG01_ResultsSavedFlagInitiallyFalse)
   383→{
   384→    // Ensure resultsSaved starts as false so PerformResultsSaving runs
   385→    // at least once during PerformASTRelease.
   386→    TestCIFixture f;
   387→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   388→}
   389→
   390→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   391→// Section 10: Regression Test - BUG-02 (Return Value Check)
   392→//
   393→// BUG-02: PerformResultsSaving() return value was ignored in both
   394→// CompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease() and
   395→// IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease().
   396→//
   397→// Fix: Both now check the return value and propagate failure.
   398→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   399→
   400→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG02_ResultsSavedFlagNotSetOnFailure)
   401→{
   402→    // If PerformResultsSaving fails, resultsSaved should remain false
   403→    // so the destructor can still clean up properly.
   404→    TestCIFixture f;
   405→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   406→    // On failure path, resultsSaved stays false, AST stays intact for cleanup.
   407→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsASTReleased());
   408→}
   409→
   410→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   411→// Section 11: Regression Test - BUG-03 (ASTWriter Leak)
   412→//
   413→// BUG-03: ImportManager::ClearASTReferences() called
   414→// astWriters.clear() instead of DeleteASTWriters(), leaking
   415→// new-allocated ASTWriter* objects.
   416→//
   417→// Fix: Replaced astWriters.clear() with DeleteASTWriters().
   418→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   419→
   420→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, BUG03_ClearASTReferencesDoesNotLeak)
   421→{
   422→    // Verify ClearASTReferences can be called without crash.
   423→    // The actual leak detection requires ASan, but we verify the
   424→    // code path executes correctly.
   425→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   426→    TypeManager typeManager;
   427→    GlobalOptions opts;
   428→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   429→
   430→    // Call ClearASTReferences which should use DeleteASTWriters()
   431→    // instead of astWriters.clear().
   432→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   433→}
   434→
   435→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   436→// Section 12: Regression Test - VULN-01 (Dangling Pointers)
   437→//
   438→// VULN-01: ClearImportedPackages() did not clear all AST pointer
   439→// fields in PackageInfo (pkgDecl, exportIDDeclMap, declMap,
   440→// implicitDeclMap), leaving dangling pointers after AST release.
   441→//
   442→// Fix: All 5 AST fields are now cleared in ClearImportedPackages().
   443→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   444→
   445→TEST(ASTReleaseRegression, VULN01_ImportManagerClearSafe)
   446→{
   447→    // Verify that ClearASTReferences on ImportManager is safe
   448→    // and doesn't leave dangling state.
   449→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   450→    TypeManager typeManager;
   451→    GlobalOptions opts;
   452→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   453→
   454→    // First clear.
   455→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   456→    // Second clear should be safe (no dangling pointers).
   457→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   458→}
   459→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   460→// Section 13: Destructor Safety Tests
   461→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   462→
   463→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, DestructorSafeWithoutRelease)
   464→{
   465→    // CompilerInstance destructor should be safe when AST was never released.
   466→    TestCIFixture f;
   467→    EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsASTReleased());
   468→    // Destructor runs when f goes out of scope — should not crash.
   469→}
   470→
   471→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, DestructorSafeAfterPartialSetup)
   472→{
   473→    // Destructor should be safe even with partial state.
   474→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   475→    CompilerInvocation invocation;
   476→    {
   477→        CompilerInstance ci(invocation, diag);
   478→        ci.SetResultsSaved(true);
   479→        // Destructor runs here — should not crash.
   480→    }
   481→}
   482→
   483→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, MultipleCompilerInstancesIndependent)
   484→{
   485→    // Multiple CompilerInstances should have independent state.
   486→    DiagnosticEngine diag1, diag2;
   487→    CompilerInvocation inv1, inv2;
   488→    CompilerInstance ci1(inv1, diag1);
   489→    CompilerInstance ci2(inv2, diag2);
   490→
   491→    ci1.SetResultsSaved(true);
   492→    EXPECT_TRUE(ci1.IsResultsSaved());
   493→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci2.IsResultsSaved());
   494→
   495→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci1.IsASTReleased());
   496→    EXPECT_FALSE(ci2.IsASTReleased());
   497→}

   499→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   500→// Section 14: PackageInfo Struct Tests
   501→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   502→
   503→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageInfoConstruction)
   504→{
   505→    PackageInfo info("test.package");
   506→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName, "test.package");
   507→    EXPECT_TRUE(info.deps.empty());
   508→}
   509→
   510→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageInfoDependencies)
   511→{
   512→    auto pkg1 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   513→    auto pkg2 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg2");
   514→    auto pkg3 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg3");
   515→
   516→    pkg1->deps.insert(pkg2.get());
   517→    pkg1->deps.insert(pkg3.get());
   518→
   519→    EXPECT_EQ(pkg1->deps.size(), 2u);
   520→    EXPECT_TRUE(pkg1->deps.count(pkg2.get()) > 0);
   521→    EXPECT_TRUE(pkg1->deps.count(pkg3.get()) > 0);
   522→}
   523→
   524→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   525→// Section 15: Edge Cases and Boundary Conditions
   526→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   527→
   528→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, EmptyPackageNameInCodeGenInfo)
   529→{
   530→    CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   531→    info.fullPackageName = "";
   532→    info.isEmpty = true;
   533→    EXPECT_TRUE(info.fullPackageName.empty());
   534→    EXPECT_TRUE(info.isEmpty);
   535→}
   536→
   537→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, LongPackageNameInCodeGenInfo)
   538→{
   539→    CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   540→    // Test with a very long package name (boundary condition).
   541→    std::string longName(1024, 'a');
   542→    for (size_t i = 0; i < longName.size(); i += 10) {
   543→        longName[i] = '.';
   544→    }
   545→    info.fullPackageName = longName;
   546→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName.size(), 1024u);
   547→}
   548→
   549→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, UnicodePackageNameInCodeGenInfo)
   550→{
   551→    CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   552→    info.fullPackageName = "仓颉.编译器.测试";
   553→    EXPECT_EQ(info.fullPackageName, "仓颉.编译器.测试");
   554→}
   555→
   556→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageManagerClearWithDependencyCycles)
   557→{
   558→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   559→    TypeManager typeManager;
   560→    GlobalOptions opts;
   561→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   562→    PackageManager pm(importManager);
   563→
   564→    // Create circular dependency: pkg1 -> pkg2 -> pkg1
   565→    auto pkg1 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   566→    auto pkg2 = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg2");
   567→    pkg1->deps.insert(pkg2.get());
   568→    pkg2->deps.insert(pkg1.get());
   569→
   570→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg1"] = std::move(pkg1);
   571→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg2"] = std::move(pkg2);
   572→
   573→    // ClearASTReferences should handle circular deps safely.
   574→    pm.ClearASTReferences();
   575→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageInfoMap.empty());
   576→}
   577→
   578→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, CachedMangleMapLargeDataSet)
   579→{
   580→    CachedMangleMap map;
   581→    // Insert many entries to test scalability.
   582→    for (int i = 0; i < 1000; ++i) {
   583→        map.incrRemovedDecls.emplace("decl_" + std::to_string(i));
   584→        map.importedInlineDecls.emplace("inline_" + std::to_string(i));
   585→        map.newExternalDecls.emplace("ext_" + std::to_string(i));
   586→    }
   587→    EXPECT_EQ(map.incrRemovedDecls.size(), 1000u);
   588→    EXPECT_EQ(map.importedInlineDecls.size(), 1000u);
   589→    EXPECT_EQ(map.newExternalDecls.size(), 1000u);
   590→
   591→    map.Clear();
   592→
   593→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
   594→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.importedInlineDecls.empty());
   595→    EXPECT_TRUE(map.newExternalDecls.empty());
   596→}
   597→
   598→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   599→// Section 16: Determinism Tests
   600→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   601→
   602→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, StateTransitionsAreDeterministic)
   603→{
   604→    // Same sequence of operations should produce same state.
   605→    for (int trial = 0; trial < 3; ++trial) {
   606→        TestCIFixture f;
   607→        EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsASTReleased());
   608→        EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   609→        EXPECT_FALSE(f.ci->IsCacheWritten());
   610→        f.ci->SetResultsSaved(true);
   611→        EXPECT_TRUE(f.ci->IsResultsSaved());
   612→    }
   613→}
   614→
   615→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, PackageCodeGenInfoVectorOrdering)
   616→{
   617→    // Verify that CodeGenPkgInfos preserves insertion order.
   618→    std::vector<CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo> infos;
   619→    for (int i = 0; i < 5; ++i) {
   620→        CompilerInstance::PackageCodeGenInfo info;
   621→        info.fullPackageName = "pkg" + std::to_string(i);
   622→        info.isEmpty = (i % 2 == 0);
   623→        infos.push_back(std::move(info));
   624→    }
   625→    EXPECT_EQ(infos.size(), 5u);
   626→    for (int i = 0; i < 5; ++i) {
   627→        EXPECT_EQ(infos[i].fullPackageName, "pkg" + std::to_string(i));
   628→        EXPECT_EQ(infos[i].isEmpty, (i % 2 == 0));
   629→    }
   630→}
   631→
   632→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   633→// Section 17: Cross-Component Integration Tests
   634→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   635→
   636→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, AllManagersClearInSequence)
   637→{
   638→    // Simulate the Phase 3 cleanup sequence: managers cleared in order.
   639→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   640→    TypeManager typeManager;
   641→    GlobalOptions opts;
   642→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   643→    PackageManager pm(importManager);
   644→
   645→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg1"] = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   646→    pm.packageToOtherSccMap["pkg1"] = {"dep1"};
   647→
   648→    // Phase 3f: ImportManager clear
   649→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   650→
   651→    // Phase 3g: PackageManager clear
   652→    pm.ClearASTReferences();
   653→
   654→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageInfoMap.empty());
   655→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageToOtherSccMap.empty());
   656→}
   657→
   658→TEST(ASTReleaseFunctional, CachedMangleMapAndPackageManagerClearTogether)
   659→{
   660→    // Simulate IncrementalCompilerInstance cleanup sequence.
   661→    CachedMangleMap cacheMangles;
   662→    cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.emplace("removed_1");
   663→    cacheMangles.importedInlineDecls.emplace("inline_1");
   664→
   665→    DiagnosticEngine diag;
   666→    TypeManager typeManager;
   667→    GlobalOptions opts;
   668→    ImportManager importManager(diag, typeManager, opts);
   669→    PackageManager pm(importManager);
   670→    pm.packageInfoMap["pkg1"] = std::make_unique<PackageInfo>("pkg1");
   671→
   672→    // Incremental-specific cleanup
   673→    cacheMangles.Clear();
   674→    EXPECT_TRUE(cacheMangles.incrRemovedDecls.empty());
   675→
   676→    // Then base class cleanup
   677→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   678→    pm.ClearASTReferences();
   679→    EXPECT_TRUE(pm.packageInfoMap.empty());
   680→}
   681→
