   200→        if (!performMap[static_cast<CompileStage>(i)](this)) {
   201→            success = false;
   202→            break;
   203→        }
   204→    }
   205→    // Dump AST to screen if needed before mangling stage.
   206→    if (invocation.globalOptions.NeedDumpASTToScreen() && i < static_cast<int>(CompileStage::MANGLING)) {
   207→        DumpASTToScreen(GetSourcePackages());
   208→    }
   209→    diag.ReportErrorAndWarningCount();
   210→    return success;
   211→}
   212→
   213→static bool IsNeedSaveIncrCompilationLogFile(const GlobalOptions& globalOpts, const FrontendOptions& frontOpts)
   214→{
   215→    if (!globalOpts.enIncrementalCompilation) {
   216→        return false;
   217→    }
   218→    if (globalOpts.scanDepPkg) {
   219→        return false;
   220→    }
   221→    if (frontOpts.dumpAction != FrontendOptions::DumpAction::NO_ACTION) {
   222→        return false;
   223→    }
   224→    if (globalOpts.compileCjd) {
   225→        return false;
   226→    }
   227→    return true;
   228→}
   229→
   230→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   231→namespace {
   232→class MetaTransformPlugin {
   233→public:
   234→    static MetaTransformPlugin Get(const std::string& path);
   235→    void RegisterCallbackTo(MetaTransformPluginBuilder& mtm) const;
   236→
   237→    bool IsValid() const
   238→    {
   239→        return !pluginPath.empty() && metaTransformPluginInfo.cjcVersion == CANGJIE_VERSION &&
   240→            metaTransformPluginInfo.registerTo;
   241→    }
   242→
   243→    void* GetHandle() const
   244→    {
   245→        return handle;
   246→    }
   247→
   248→private:
   249→    MetaTransformPlugin() = default;
   250→    MetaTransformPlugin(const std::string& pluginPath, const MetaTransformPluginInfo& info, HANDLE handle);
   251→
   252→private:
   253→    std::string pluginPath;
   254→    MetaTransformPluginInfo metaTransformPluginInfo;
   255→    HANDLE handle;
   256→};
   257→
   258→MetaTransformPlugin::MetaTransformPlugin(
   259→    const std::string& pluginPath, const MetaTransformPluginInfo& info, HANDLE handle)
   260→    : pluginPath(pluginPath), metaTransformPluginInfo(info), handle(handle)
   261→{
   262→}
   263→
   264→MetaTransformPlugin MetaTransformPlugin::Get(const std::string& path)
   265→{
   266→    HANDLE handle = nullptr;
   267→#ifdef _WIN32
   268→    handle = InvokeRuntime::OpenSymbolTable(path);
   269→#elif defined(__linux__) || defined(__APPLE__)
   270→    handle = InvokeRuntime::OpenSymbolTable(path, RTLD_NOW | RTLD_LOCAL);
   271→#endif
   272→    if (!handle) {
   273→#ifndef CANGJIE_ENABLE_GCOV
   274→        throw NullPointerException();
   275→#else
   276→        CJC_ABORT();
   277→#endif
   278→    }
   279→    void* fPtr = InvokeRuntime::GetMethod(handle, "getMetaTransformPluginInfo");
   280→    if (!fPtr) {
   281→#ifndef CANGJIE_ENABLE_GCOV
   282→        throw NullPointerException();
   283→#else
   284→        CJC_ABORT();
   285→#endif
   286→    }
   287→    auto pluginInfo = reinterpret_cast<MetaTransformPluginInfo (*)()>(fPtr)();
   288→    return MetaTransformPlugin(path, pluginInfo, handle);
   289→}
   290→
   291→void MetaTransformPlugin::RegisterCallbackTo(MetaTransformPluginBuilder& mtm) const
   292→{
   293→    metaTransformPluginInfo.registerTo(mtm);
   294→}
   295→} // namespace
   296→
   297→bool CompilerInstance::PerformPluginLoad()
   298→{
   299→    for (auto pluginPath : invocation.globalOptions.pluginPaths) { // loop for all plugins
   300→#ifndef CANGJIE_ENABLE_GCOV
   301→        try {
   302→#endif
   303→            auto metaTransformPlugin = MetaTransformPlugin::Get(pluginPath);
   304→            if (!metaTransformPlugin.IsValid()) {
   305→                diag.DiagnoseRefactor(DiagKindRefactor::not_a_valid_plugin, DEFAULT_POSITION, pluginPath);
   306→            }
   307→            AddPluginHandle(metaTransformPlugin.GetHandle());
   308→            metaTransformPlugin.RegisterCallbackTo(metaTransformPluginBuilder); // register MetaTransform into builder
   309→#ifndef CANGJIE_ENABLE_GCOV
   310→        } catch (...) {
   311→            diag.DiagnoseRefactor(DiagKindRefactor::not_a_valid_plugin, DEFAULT_POSITION, pluginPath);
   312→            return false;
   313→        }
   314→#endif
   315→    }
   316→    return true;
   317→}
   318→#endif
   319→
   320→bool CompilerInstance::PerformParse()
   321→{
   322→    auto ret = compileStrategy->Parse();
   323→    if (!srcPkgs.empty()) {
   324→        const auto& globalOpts = invocation.globalOptions;
   325→        srcPkgs.front()->noSubPkg = globalOpts.noSubPkg;
   326→        Utils::ProfileRecorder::SetPackageName(srcPkgs[0]->fullPackageName);
   327→        Utils::ProfileRecorder::SetOutputDir(globalOpts.output);
   328→        if (IsNeedSaveIncrCompilationLogFile(globalOpts, invocation.frontendOptions)) {
   329→            std::string incrLogPath =
   330→                invocation.globalOptions.GenerateCachedPathName(srcPkgs[0]->fullPackageName, CACHED_LOG_EXTENSION);
   331→            IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().InitLogFile(incrLogPath);
   332→            IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance().WriteBuffToFile();
   333→        }
   334→        if (globalOpts.NeedDumpASTToFile()) {
   335→            DumpAST(GetSourcePackages(), globalOpts.output, "parse");
   336→        }
   337→    }
   338→    return ret;
   339→}
   340→
   341→bool CompilerInstance::PerformConditionCompile()
   342→{
   343→    auto ret = compileStrategy->ConditionCompile();
   344→    if (!srcPkgs.empty() && invocation.globalOptions.NeedDumpASTToFile()) {
   345→        DumpAST(GetSourcePackages(), invocation.globalOptions.output, "condcomp");
   346→    }
   347→    return ret;
   348→}
   349→
   350→bool CompilerInstance::PerformMacroExpand()
   351→{
   352→    auto ret = compileStrategy->MacroExpand();
   353→
   354→    // Constant evaluation and the interpreter needs to load bchir, which requires an AST loader.
   355→    if (!invocation.globalOptions.IsConstEvalEnabled() && !invocation.globalOptions.interpreter) {
   356→        importManager.DeleteASTLoaders();
   357→    }
   358→    importManager.ClearPackageBCHIRCache();
   359→
   360→    if (invocation.globalOptions.compileTestsOnly && invocation.globalOptions.enableVerbose) {
   361→        Print("Source files to compile for the test-only mode: {");
   362→        for (auto& pkg : srcPkgs) {
   363→            for (auto& srcFile : pkg->files) {
   364→                Print(pkg->fullPackageName + "::" + srcFile->fileName);
   365→            }
   366→        }
   367→        Println("}");
   368→    }
   369→    if (!srcPkgs.empty() && invocation.globalOptions.NeedDumpASTToFile()) {
   370→        DumpAST(GetSourcePackages(), invocation.globalOptions.output, "macroexp");
   371→    }
   372→    return ret;
   373→}
   374→
   375→void CompilerInstance::CacheCompileArgs()
   376→{
   377→    cachedInfo.compileArgs = invocation.globalOptions.ToSerialized();
   378→}
   379→
   380→void CompilerInstance::CacheSemaUsage(SemanticInfo&& info)
   381→{
   382→    // Move previous unchanged sema usage info to current info.
   383→    for (auto& [decl, usage] : cachedInfo.semaInfo.usages) {
   384→        if (decl->toBeCompiled) {
   385→            continue;
   386→        }
   387→        auto found = info.usages.find(decl);
   388→        // MainDecl's usage is recorded as desugared.
   389→        if (auto mainDecl = DynamicCast<MainDecl*>(decl); mainDecl && mainDecl->desugarDecl) {
   390→            found = info.usages.find(mainDecl->desugarDecl.get());
   391→        } else if (auto macroDecl = DynamicCast<MacroDecl*>(decl); macroDecl && macroDecl->desugarDecl) {
   392→            found = info.usages.find(macroDecl->desugarDecl.get());
   393→        }
   394→        if (found != info.usages.end()) {
   395→            found->second = std::move(usage);
   396→        }
   397→    }
   398→    // Update cached info.
   399→    cachedInfo.semaInfo = std::move(info);
   400→}
   401→
   402→bool CompilerInstance::ShouldWriteCacheFile() const
   403→{
   404→    if (astReleased) {
   405→        return false;
   406→    }
   407→    if (!invocation.globalOptions.enIncrementalCompilation) {
   408→        return false;
   409→    }
   410→    // if set "printVersionOnly" and "showUsage", must not get here
   411→    if (invocation.globalOptions.printVersionOnly || invocation.globalOptions.showUsage) {
   412→        InternalError("'printVersionOnly' or 'showUsage' cannot be true.");
   413→    }
   414→    // if compiled with "cjc-frontend --dump-xxx ...", we don't write cache file
   415→    // that's OK, in this case, we can not run incremental compiling
   416→    if (invocation.frontendOptions.dumpAction != FrontendOptions::DumpAction::NO_ACTION) {
   417→        return false;
   418→    }
   419→    if (invocation.globalOptions.IsEmitCHIREnable()) {
   420→        return false;
   421→    }
   422→    if (invocation.globalOptions.compileCjd) {
   423→        return false;
   424→    }
   425→    if (srcPkgs.size() != 1) {
   426→        InternalError("source packages should only have one element.");
   427→    }
   428→    if (!invocation.globalOptions.compilePackage && invocation.globalOptions.srcFiles.empty() &&
   429→        !invocation.globalOptions.inputObjs.empty()) {
   430→        return false;
   431→    }
   432→    // if current package is empty package, we don't write cache file
   433→    if (srcPkgs[0]->IsEmpty() || kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   434→        return false;
   435→    }
   436→    return true;
   437→}
   438→
   439→namespace {
   440→void UpdateMemberDeclMangleNameForCachedInfo(const RawMangled2DeclMap& rawMangleName2DeclMap, MemberDeclCache& memCache)
   441→{
   442→    if (auto d = rawMangleName2DeclMap.find(memCache.rawMangle); d != rawMangleName2DeclMap.end()) {
   443→        memCache.cgMangle = d->second->mangledName;
   444→    } else {
   445→        CJC_ABORT();
   446→    }
   447→    for (auto &m : memCache.members) {
   448→        UpdateMemberDeclMangleNameForCachedInfo(rawMangleName2DeclMap, m);
   449→    }
   450→}
   451→
   452→void UpdateTopLevelDeclMangleNameForCachedInfo(
   453→    const RawMangled2DeclMap& rawMangleName2DeclMap, const std::string& rawMangle, TopLevelDeclCache& topCache)
   454→{
   455→    if (auto d = rawMangleName2DeclMap.find(rawMangle); d != rawMangleName2DeclMap.end()) {
   456→        topCache.cgMangle = d->second->mangledName;
   457→    } else {
   458→        CJC_ABORT();
   459→    }
   460→    for (auto &m : topCache.members) {
   461→        UpdateMemberDeclMangleNameForCachedInfo(rawMangleName2DeclMap, m);
   462→    }
   463→}
   464→}
   465→
   466→void CompilerInstance::UpdateMangleNameForCachedInfo()
   467→{
   468→    for (auto &it : cachedInfo.curPkgASTCache) {
   469→        auto rawMangle = it.first;
   470→        UpdateTopLevelDeclMangleNameForCachedInfo(rawMangleName2DeclMap, rawMangle, it.second);
   471→    }
   472→    for (auto &it : cachedInfo.importedASTCache) {
   473→        auto rawMangle = it.first;
   474→        UpdateTopLevelDeclMangleNameForCachedInfo(rawMangleName2DeclMap, rawMangle, it.second);
   475→    }
   476→}
   477→
   478→void CompilerInstance::UpdateCachedInfo()
   479→{
   480→    // update mangle name for codegen
   481→    UpdateMangleNameForCachedInfo();
   482→}
   483→
   484→bool CompilerInstance::WriteCachedInfo()
   485→{
   486→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   487→    auto& pkg{*srcPkgs[0]};
   488→    std::string path{invocation.globalOptions.GenerateCachedPathName(pkg.fullPackageName, CACHED_AST_EXTENSION)};
   489→    WriteCache(pkg, std::move(cachedInfo), std::move(order), path);
   490→#endif
   491→    return true;
   492→}
   493→
   494→bool CompilerInstance::UpdateAndWriteCachedInfoToDisk()
   495→{
   496→    // If cache was already written during PerformASTRelease (before AST was freed), skip.
   497→    if (cacheWritten) {
   498→        return true;
   499→    }
```

   100→    // These resources must be cleaned regardless of AST release state.
   101→    delete compileStrategy;
   102→    compileStrategy = nullptr;
   103→    delete packageManager;
   104→    packageManager = nullptr;
   105→    // mangler is unique_ptr, auto-destructed.
   106→    // importManager is a stack member, auto-destructed.

   108→
   109→bool CompilerInstance::InitCompilerInstance()
   110→{
   111→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   112→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::LOAD_PLUGINS, &CompilerInstance::PerformPluginLoad);
   113→#endif
   114→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::PARSE, &CompilerInstance::PerformParse);
   115→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::CONDITION_COMPILE, &CompilerInstance::PerformConditionCompile);
   116→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::IMPORT_PACKAGE, &CompilerInstance::PerformImportPackage);
   117→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::MACRO_EXPAND, &CompilerInstance::PerformMacroExpand);
   118→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::AST_DIFF, &CompilerInstance::PerformIncrementalScopeAnalysis);
   119→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::SEMA, &CompilerInstance::PerformSema);
   120→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::DESUGAR_AFTER_SEMA, &CompilerInstance::PerformDesugarAfterSema);
   121→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::GENERIC_INSTANTIATION, &CompilerInstance::PerformGenericInstantiation);
   122→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::OVERFLOW_STRATEGY, &CompilerInstance::PerformOverflowStrategy);
   123→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::MANGLING, &CompilerInstance::PerformMangling);
   124→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::SAVE_CJO, &CompilerInstance::PerformCjoSaving);
   125→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::CHIR, &CompilerInstance::PerformCHIRCompilation);
   126→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::RELEASE_AST, &CompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease);
   127→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::CODEGEN, &CompilerInstance::PerformCodeGen);
   128→    performMap.insert_or_assign(CompileStage::SAVE_RESULTS, &CompilerInstance::PerformResultsSaving);
   129→    return true;
   130→}
   131→
   132→namespace {
   133→void DumpASTToScreen(const std::vector<Ptr<Package>>& srcPkgs)
   134→{
   135→    if (srcPkgs.empty()) {
   136→        return;
   137→    }
   138→    for (auto& srcPkg : srcPkgs) {
   139→        PrintNode(srcPkg.get());
   140→    }
   141→}
   142→void DumpAST(const std::vector<Ptr<Package>>& srcPkgs, const std::string& outputOfProduct = "",
   143→    const std::string& prefix = "", bool dumpToScreen = false)
   144→{
   145→    if (srcPkgs.empty()) {
   146→        return;
   147→    }
   148→    CJC_ASSERT(srcPkgs.size() == 1);
   149→    const std::string& pkgName = srcPkgs[0]->fullPackageName;
   150→    if (dumpToScreen) {
   151→        DumpASTToScreen(srcPkgs);
   152→        return;
   153→    }
   154→    static std::string dumpDir;
   155→    static bool checkDumpDir = false;
   156→    static size_t fileNum = 0;
   157→    if (!checkDumpDir) {
   158→        if (FileUtil::IsDir(outputOfProduct)) {
   159→            dumpDir = FileUtil::JoinPath(outputOfProduct, pkgName + "_AST");
   160→        } else {
   161→            dumpDir = FileUtil::GetFileBase(outputOfProduct) + "_AST";
   162→        }
   163→        if (FileUtil::FileExist(dumpDir)) {
   164→            FileUtil::RemoveDirectoryRecursively(dumpDir);
   165→        }
   166→        FileUtil::CreateDirs(dumpDir + DIR_SEPARATOR);
   167→        checkDumpDir = true;
   168→    }
   169→    auto realDirPath = Cangjie::FileUtil::GetAbsPath(dumpDir);
   170→    if (!realDirPath.has_value()) {
   171→        Errorln("Cannot get absolute path of dump directory: " + dumpDir, ", not dump ", prefix, " AST");
   172→        return;
   173→    }
   174→    std::string dumpPath =
   175→        FileUtil::JoinPath(realDirPath.value(), std::to_string(fileNum) + "_" + prefix + "_ast" + ".txt");
   176→    std::ofstream ofs(dumpPath);
   177→    if (!ofs) {
   178→        Errorln("Cannot open file to dump AST: " + dumpPath);
   179→        return;
   180→    }
   181→    for (auto& srcPkg : srcPkgs) {
   182→        PrintNode(srcPkg.get(), 0, "", ofs);
   183→    }
   184→    ofs.close();
   185→    fileNum++;
   186→}
   187→} // namespace
   188→
   189→bool CompilerInstance::Compile(CompileStage stage)
   190→{
   191→    if (!InitCompilerInstance()) {
   192→        diag.ReportErrorAndWarningCount();
   193→        return false;
   194→    }
   195→    auto endStageNum = static_cast<int>(stage);
   196→    int i = 0;
   197→    bool success = true;
   198→    for (; i <= endStageNum; i++) {
   199→        Cangjie::ICE::TriggerPointSetter iceSetter(static_cast<CompileStage>(i));
   200→        if (!performMap[static_cast<CompileStage>(i)](this)) {
   201→            success = false;
   202→            break;
   203→        }
   204→    }
   205→    // Dump AST to screen if needed before mangling stage.
   206→    if (invocation.globalOptions.NeedDumpASTToScreen() && i < static_cast<int>(CompileStage::MANGLING)) {
   207→        DumpASTToScreen(GetSourcePackages());
   208→    }
   209→    diag.ReportErrorAndWarningCount();
   210→    return success;
   211→}
   212→
   213→static bool IsNeedSaveIncrCompilationLogFile(const GlobalOptions& globalOpts, const FrontendOptions& frontOpts)
   214→{
   215→    if (!globalOpts.enIncrementalCompilation) {
   216→        return false;
   217→    }
   218→    if (globalOpts.scanDepPkg) {
   219→        return false;
   220→    }
   221→    if (frontOpts.dumpAction != FrontendOptions::DumpAction::NO_ACTION) {
   222→        return false;
   223→    }
   224→    if (globalOpts.compileCjd) {
   225→        return false;
   226→    }
   227→    return true;
   228→}
   229→
   230→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   231→namespace {
   232→class MetaTransformPlugin {
   233→public:
   234→    static MetaTransformPlugin Get(const std::string& path);
   235→    void RegisterCallbackTo(MetaTransformPluginBuilder& mtm) const;
   236→
   237→    bool IsValid() const
   238→    {
   239→        return !pluginPath.empty() && metaTransformPluginInfo.cjcVersion == CANGJIE_VERSION &&
   240→            metaTransformPluginInfo.registerTo;
   241→    }
   242→
   243→    void* GetHandle() const
   244→    {
   245→        return handle;
   246→    }
   247→
   248→private:
   249→    MetaTransformPlugin() = default;
   250→    MetaTransformPlugin(const std::string& pluginPath, const MetaTransformPluginInfo& info, HANDLE handle);
   251→
   252→private:
   253→    std::string pluginPath;
   254→    MetaTransformPluginInfo metaTransformPluginInfo;
   255→    HANDLE handle;
   256→};
   257→
   258→MetaTransformPlugin::MetaTransformPlugin(
   259→    const std::string& pluginPath, const MetaTransformPluginInfo& info, HANDLE handle)
   260→    : pluginPath(pluginPath), metaTransformPluginInfo(info), handle(handle)
   261→{
   262→}
   263→
   264→MetaTransformPlugin MetaTransformPlugin::Get(const std::string& path)
   265→{
   266→    HANDLE handle = nullptr;
   267→#ifdef _WIN32
   268→    handle = InvokeRuntime::OpenSymbolTable(path);
   269→#elif defined(__linux__) || defined(__APPLE__)
   270→    handle = InvokeRuntime::OpenSymbolTable(path, RTLD_NOW | RTLD_LOCAL);
   271→#endif
   272→    if (!handle) {
   273→#ifndef CANGJIE_ENABLE_GCOV
   274→        throw NullPointerException();
   275→#else
   276→        CJC_ABORT();
   277→#endif
   278→    }
   279→    void* fPtr = InvokeRuntime::GetMethod(handle, "getMetaTransformPluginInfo");
   280→    if (!fPtr) {
   281→#ifndef CANGJIE_ENABLE_GCOV
   282→        throw NullPointerException();
   283→#else
   284→        CJC_ABORT();
   285→#endif
   286→    }
   287→    auto pluginInfo = reinterpret_cast<MetaTransformPluginInfo (*)()>(fPtr)();
   288→    return MetaTransformPlugin(path, pluginInfo, handle);
   289→}
   290→
   291→void MetaTransformPlugin::RegisterCallbackTo(MetaTransformPluginBuilder& mtm) const
   292→{
   293→    metaTransformPluginInfo.registerTo(mtm);
   294→}
   295→} // namespace
   296→

   298→{
   299→    for (auto pluginPath : invocation.globalOptions.pluginPaths) { // loop for all plugins
```

<details><summary>返回结果 (100 行)</summary>

```
   520→
   521→bool CompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease()
   522→{
   523→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Release AST");
   524→
   525→    // Always extract CodeGen metadata before potential release.
   526→    PrepareCodeGenInfo();
   527→
   528→    // Save results (e.g., CJO in CHIR output mode) before AST is freed.
   529→    // PerformResultsSaving() may need srcPkgs, so it must run before ReleaseASTMemory().
   530→    if (!resultsSaved) {
   531→        if (!PerformResultsSaving()) {
   532→            return false;  // Propagate save failure to abort compilation.
   533→        }
   534→        resultsSaved = true;
   535→    }
   536→
   537→    // Write incremental compilation cache before AST is freed (ADR-009).
   538→    // WriteCachedInfo dereferences srcPkgs[0], order, varAndFuncDep, semaInfo.usages.
   539→    if (ShouldWriteCacheFile() && !cacheWritten) {
   540→        UpdateCachedInfo();
   541→        WriteCachedInfo();
   542→        cacheWritten = true;
   543→    }
   544→
   545→    // Allow skipping AST release for debugging (e.g., ASan leak analysis).
   546→    if (invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST) {
   547→        return true;
   548→    }
   549→
   550→    ReleaseASTMemory();
   551→    return true;
   552→}
   553→
   554→void CompilerInstance::ReleaseASTMemory()
   555→{
   556→    if (astReleased) {
   557→        return;
   558→    }
   559→
   560→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   561→    // Phase 1: Clear CHIR-layer AST references
   562→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   563→
   564→    // 1a. Global annotation info (holds AST ClassDef*/Decl* pointers)
   565→    CHIR::ClearGlobalAnnotationInfo();
   566→
   567→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   568→    // Phase 2: Clear CompilerInstance direct member AST references
   569→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   570→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   571→    astPkg2chirPkgMap.clear();
   572→#endif
   573→    currentPkg = nullptr;
   574→    mangledName2DeclMap.clear();
   575→    rawMangleName2DeclMap.clear();
   576→    declsWithDuplicatedRawMangleName.clear();
   577→    directExtends.clear();
   578→    order.clear();
   579→    chirInfo.ccTys.clear();
   580→    pkgs.clear();
   581→
   582→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   583→    // Phase 3: Release managers (destruction order matters)
   584→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   585→
   586→    // 3a. TypeChecker holds TypeManager& reference, must be freed first.
   587→    delete typeChecker;
   588→    typeChecker = nullptr;
   589→
   590→    // 3b. TypeManager holds 15+ AST pointer collections.
   591→    delete typeManager;
   592→    typeManager = nullptr;
   593→
   594→    // 3c. GenericInstantiationManager
   595→    delete gim;
   596→    gim = nullptr;
   597→
   598→    // 3d. TestManager holds ImportManager and TypeManager references.
   599→    delete testManager;
   600→    testManager = nullptr;
   601→
   602→    // 3e. BaseMangler — ManglerContext holds AST pointer maps.
   603→    mangler.reset();
   604→
   605→    // 3f. ImportManager — stack member, clear AST references and release imported packages.
   606→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   607→
   608→    // 3g. PackageManager — clear resolved dependency data.
   609→    if (packageManager) {
   610→        packageManager->ClearASTReferences();
   611→    }
   612→
   613→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   614→    // Phase 4: Release AST core data (strict order)
   615→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   616→
   617→    // 4a. Release AST nodes first (triggers Symbol detach).
   618→    srcPkgs.clear();
   619→
```

    30→namespace Cangjie {
    31→/** Lucene like inverted index. */
    32→struct InvertedIndex {
    33→    /** Inverted index of Symbol's name. */
    34→    std::unordered_map<std::string, std::set<AST::Symbol*>> nameIndexes;
    35→    /** Inverted index of Symbol's scope name. */
    36→    std::unordered_map<std::string, std::set<AST::Symbol*>> scopeNameIndexes;
    37→    /** Map of scope gate. */
    38→    std::unordered_map<std::string, AST::Symbol*> scopeGateMap;
    39→    /** Inverted index of Symbol's scope level. */
    40→    std::unordered_map<uint32_t, std::set<AST::Symbol*>> scopeLevelIndexes;
    41→    /** Inverted index of Symbol's ast kind. */
    42→    std::unordered_map<std::string, std::set<AST::Symbol*>> astKindIndexes;
    43→    /** Put @c name into a trie, easy to do prefix search. */
    44→    std::unique_ptr<Trie> nameTrie = std::make_unique<Trie>();
    45→    /** Put @c scopeName into a trie, easy to do prefix search. */
    46→    std::unique_ptr<Trie> scopeNameTrie = std::make_unique<Trie>();
    47→    /** Put @c astKind into a trie, easy to do suffix search. */
    48→    std::unique_ptr<Trie> astKindTrie = std::make_unique<Trie>();
    49→    /** Put the begin position of a symbol into a trie, easy to do range search. */
    50→    std::unique_ptr<Trie> posBeginTrie = std::make_unique<Trie>();
    51→    /** Put the begin position of a symbol into a trie, easy to do range search. */
    52→    std::unique_ptr<Trie> posEndTrie = std::make_unique<Trie>();
    53→    /** The minimum possible position. */
    54→    Position minPos = BEGIN_POSITION;
    55→    /** The maximum possible position. */
    56→    Position maxPos = {0, PosSearchApi::MAX_LINE, PosSearchApi::MAX_COLUMN};
    57→
    58→    /** Clear all indexes. */
    59→    void Reset();
    60→
    61→    /** Build inverted index. */
    62→    void Index(AST::Symbol* symbol, bool withTrie = true);
    63→
    64→    /** Delete inverted index. */
    65→    void Delete(AST::Symbol* symbol);
    66→};
    67→

<details><summary>返回结果 (49 行)</summary>

```
# Cangjie Programming Language Compiler

## Introduction

Cangjie is a general-purpose programming language designed for all-scenario application development, balancing development efficiency and runtime performance while providing a great programming experience. Cangjie features concise and efficient syntax, multi-paradigm programming, and type safety. For more information, please refer to the [Cangjie Language Development Guide](https://cangjie-lang.cn/docs?url=%2F1.0.0%2Fuser_manual%2Fsource_zh_cn%2Ffirst_understanding%2Fbasic.html) and the [Cangjie Programming Language White Paper](https://cangjie-lang.cn/docs?url=%2F0.53.18%2Fwhite_paper%2Fsource_zh_cn%2Fcj-wp-abstract.html).

This repository provides the source code for the Cangjie compiler, which consists of two main parts: the compiler frontend and modified open-source LLVM components. The latter includes the LLVM backend, opt optimizer, llc, ld linker, and debugger. For details on third-party dependencies, see the [Third-Party Library Documentation](./third_party/README.md).

## Architecture

The overall architecture is shown below:

![Architecture Diagram](figures/Compiler_Architecture_Diagram.png)

**Architecture Description**

- **Compiler Frontend**: Responsible for converting Cangjie source code from text to intermediate representation, including lexical, syntax, macro, and semantic analysis, ensuring code structure and semantics are correct, and preparing for backend code generation. This module depends on mingw-w64 to support Windows platform capabilities, enabling users to generate executable binaries that can call Windows APIs. It also relies on libboundscheck for safe function library access.

  - **Lexer** breaks down Cangjie source code into meaningful tokens.

  - **Parser** builds an Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) according to Cangjie grammar rules to reflect program structure.

  - **Semantic** performs type checking, type inference, and scope analysis on the AST to ensure semantic correctness.

  - **Mangler** handles symbol name mangling for Cangjie, and includes a demangler tool for reverse parsing.

  - **Package Management** manages and loads code modules, handles dependencies and namespace isolation, and supports multi-module collaborative development. This module uses the flatbuffer library for serialization and deserialization.

  - **Macro** handles macro expansion, processing macro definitions and calls for code generation and reuse.

  - **Condition Compile**: Conditional compilation allows compiling based on predefined or custom conditions; incremental compilation speeds up builds using previous compilation cache files.

  - **CHIR**: CHIR (Cangjie High Level IR) converts the AST to an intermediate representation and performs optimizations.

  - **Codegen**: Translates the intermediate representation (CHIR) to LLVM IR, preparing for target machine code (LLVM BitCode) generation.

- **LLVM**: Includes the compiler backend and related LLVM toolchain. The backend receives the intermediate representation from the frontend, optimizes it, generates target platform machine code, and links it into executable files.

  - **opt**: Performs various optimizations on LLVM IR, such as constant folding and loop optimization, to improve code efficiency and quality.

  - **llc**: Converts optimized LLVM IR to target platform machine code, supporting different hardware architectures.

  - **ld**: Links multiple object files and libraries into the final executable, resolving symbol references and generating deployable program artifacts.

  - **debugger**: Provides debugging capabilities for the Cangjie language.

For more details on the LLVM toolchain and backend tools, refer to the [LLVM Command Guide](https://llvm.org/docs/CommandGuide/).

- **OS**: The Cangjie compiler and LLVM toolchain currently support Windows x86-64, Linux x86-64/AArch64, and Mac x86/arm64. OHOS support is under development. In addition to native compilation, the Cangjie compiler supports cross-compiling binaries for the ohos-aarch64 platform. For details, see the [Cangjie SDK Integration and Build Guide](https://gitcode.com/Cangjie/cangjie_build) and [Platform Support Roadmap](#platform-support-roadmap).
```

</details>

  -o, --output <value>        Specify product name or output directory when compiling a package
  --output-dir <value>        Specify output directory (it affects '--output' option)
  --output-javagen-dir <value>
                              Specify output directory for javagen
  --no-prelude                Not import cangjie std.core package by default, only applicable when compiling std.core
  --enable-interop-cjmapping  enable cj data structure mapping for interop (Experimental)
  --static                    Statically link cangjie library
  --static-std                Statically link packages of the std module
  --dy-std                    Dynamically link packages of the std module
  --static-libs               Statically link packages of other modules except std
  --dy-libs                   Dynamically link packages of other modules except std
  --lto <value>               Enable LTO to either 'full' or 'thin' (Not available for Windows target)
    <value>=full                
    <value>=thin

  --profile-compile-time      Print time spent of all phases in the compilation
  --profile-compile-memory    Print memory usage of all phases in the compilation
  --enable-eh                 Enables experimental support for effect handlers (Experimental)
  --dump-ast                  Dump human readable AST when compiling for debug
  --dump-chir                 Dump human readable CHIR when compiling for debug
  --dump-ir                   Dump human readable IR
  --dump-all                  Dump all of AST, CHIR, IR
  --dump-to-screen            Dump to screen instead of file
  --import-interop-cj-package-config-path <value>

                              Enable CHIR redundant GetOrThrow elimination.

<details><summary>查看内容 (125 行)</summary>

```py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Cangjie Compiler AST Release Stress Test Generator
Generates progressively larger and more complex .cj source files to stress-test
the AST memory release mechanism.
"""
import os
import sys

OUT_DIR = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases"
os.makedirs(OUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ============================================================
# Category 1: Scaling tests — increasing number of classes
# ============================================================
def gen_many_classes(n):
    """Generate a file with N classes, each with methods and fields."""
    lines = [f"// STRESS: {n} classes with methods and fields"]
    for i in range(n):
        lines.append(f"""
class C{i} {{
    var x{i}: Int64 = {i}
    var name{i}: String = "class_{i}"
    func compute{i}(): Int64 {{
        return x{i} * {i + 1}
    }}
    func greet{i}(): String {{
        return "Hello from C{i}: ${{name{i}}}"
    }}
}}""")
    lines.append("""
main() {
    var sum: Int64 = 0""")
    # Only reference a subset to keep main() manageable
    step = max(1, n // 20)
    for i in range(0, n, step):
        lines.append(f"    sum = sum + C{i}().compute{i}()")
    lines.append("    println(sum)")
    lines.append("    return 0")
    lines.append("}")
    return "\n".join(lines)

# ============================================================
# Category 2: Deep inheritance chains
# ============================================================
def gen_deep_inheritance(depth):
    """Generate a deep inheritance chain of N levels."""
    lines = [f"// STRESS: inheritance depth = {depth}"]
    lines.append("""
open class Base0 {
    var level: Int64 = 0
    public open func getLevel(): Int64 { return level }
}""")
    for i in range(1, depth):
        lines.append(f"""
open class Base{i} <: Base{i-1} {{
    public override func getLevel(): Int64 {{ return {i} }}
}}""")
    lines.append(f"""
main() {{
    let obj = Base{depth-1}()
    println(obj.getLevel())
    return 0
}}""")
    return "\n".join(lines)

# ============================================================
# Category 3: Many functions (stress A-3 per-function release)
# ============================================================
def gen_many_functions(n):
    """Generate N top-level functions to stress per-function body release."""
    lines = [f"// STRESS: {n} top-level functions"]
    for i in range(n):
        lines.append(f"""
func compute_{i}(x: Int64): Int64 {{
    var result = x + {i}
    if (result > 1000) {{
        result = result - 500
    }}
    return result * 2
}}""")
    lines.append("\nmain() {")
    lines.append("    var sum: Int64 = 0")
    step = max(1, n // 50)
    for i in range(0, n, step):
        lines.append(f"    sum = sum + compute_{i}(sum)")
    lines.append("    println(sum)")
    lines.append("    return 0")
    lines.append("}")
    return "\n".join(lines)

# ============================================================
# Category 4: Generic class instantiation explosion
# ============================================================
def gen_generic_explosion(n):
    """Generate generic classes with many instantiations."""
    lines = [f"// STRESS: generic instantiation with {n} types"]
    lines.append("""
class Box<T> {
    var value: T
    init(v: T) { value = v }
    func get(): T { return value }
}

class Pair<A, B> {
    var first: A
    var second: B
    init(a: A, b: B) { first = a; second = b }
}""")
    # Generate wrapper classes to create distinct type instantiations
    for i in range(n):
        lines.append(f"""
class Wrapper{i} {{
    var id: Int64 = {i}
    func getId(): Int64 {{ return id }}
}}""")
    lines.append("\nmain() {")
    lines.append("    var sum: Int64 = 0")
    # PLACEHOLDER_MAIN_BODY
    return "\n".join(lines)

# ============================================================
# Category 5: Deeply nested expressions
# ============================================================

```

```py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Cangjie Compiler AST Release Stress Test Generator & Runner
Generates progressively larger .cj source files and measures compilation
time/memory with and without AST release.
"""
import os, sys, time, subprocess, json, resource, signal

OUT_DIR = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases"
RESULTS_DIR = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/results"
os.makedirs(OUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(RESULTS_DIR, exist_ok=True)

CJC = None  # Set after envsetup

def find_cjc():
    """Find cjc binary."""
    paths = [
        "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output/bin/cjc",
        "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/build/build/bin/cjc",
    ]
    for p in paths:
        if os.path.exists(p):
            return p
    return "cjc"

# ============================================================
# Test Case Generators
# ============================================================

def gen_many_classes(n):
    lines = [f"// STRESS: {n} classes with methods and fields"]
    for i in range(n):
        lines.append(f"class C{i} {{")
        lines.append(f"    var x{i}: Int64 = {i}")
        lines.append(f"    var name{i}: String = \"c{i}\"")
        lines.append(f"    func compute{i}(): Int64 {{ return x{i} * {i+1} }}")
        lines.append(f"    func greet{i}(): String {{ return \"hi ${{name{i}}}\" }}")
        lines.append("}")
    lines.append("main() {")
    lines.append("    var s: Int64 = 0")
    step = max(1, n // 20)
    for i in range(0, n, step):
        lines.append(f"    s = s + C{i}().compute{i}()")
    lines.append("    println(s)")
    lines.append("    return 0")
    lines.append("}")
    return "\n".join(lines)

def gen_deep_inheritance(depth):
    lines = [f"// STRESS: inheritance depth = {depth}"]
    lines.append("open class B0 {")
    lines.append("    var level: Int64 = 0")
    lines.append("    public open func getLevel(): Int64 { return level }")
    lines.append("}")
    # PLACEHOLDER_REST

```

+ def gen_many_functions(n):

+     for i in range(n):
+         lines.append(f"func fn_{i}(x: Int64): Int64 {{")
+         lines.append(f"    var r = x + {i}")

+ def gen_nested_closures(depth):
+     lines = [f"// STRESS: closure nesting depth = {depth}"]
+     lines.append("func buildChain(): () -> Int64 {")
+     indent = "    "
+     for i in range(depth):
+         lines.append(f"{indent}let v{i} = {i}")
+         lines.append(f"{indent}let f{i} = {{ =>")
+         indent += "    "
+     # innermost return
+     parts = " + ".join([f"v{i}" for i in range(depth)])
+     lines.append(f"{indent}{parts}")
+     for i in range(depth - 1, -1, -1):
+         indent = indent[:-4]
+         lines.append(f"{indent}}}")
+     lines.append(f"    return f0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     lines.append("main() {")
+     lines.append("    let f = buildChain()")
+     lines.append("    println(f())")
+     lines.append("    return 0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     return "\n".join(lines)
+ 
+ def gen_generic_explosion(n):
+     lines = [f"// STRESS: {n} generic wrapper types"]
+     lines.append("class Box<T> {")
+     lines.append("    var value: T")
+     lines.append("    init(v: T) { value = v }")
+     lines.append("    func get(): T { return value }")
+     lines.append("}")
+     for i in range(n):
+         lines.append(f"class W{i} {{")
+         lines.append(f"    var id: Int64 = {i}")
+         lines.append("}")
+     lines.append("main() {")
+     lines.append("    var s: Int64 = 0")
+     step = max(1, n // 30)
+     for i in range(0, n, step):
+         lines.append(f"    let b{i} = Box<W{i}>(W{i}())")
+         lines.append(f"    s = s + b{i}.get().id")
+     lines.append("    println(s)")
+     lines.append("    return 0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     return "\n".join(lines)
+ 
+ def gen_deep_nested_expr(depth):
+     lines = [f"// STRESS: expression nesting depth = {depth}"]
+     lines.append("func deepExpr(): Int64 {")
+     expr = "1"
+     for i in range(depth):
+         expr = f"({expr} + {i % 10})"
+     lines.append(f"    return {expr}")
+     lines.append("}")
+     lines.append("main() {")
+     lines.append("    println(deepExpr())")
+     lines.append("    return 0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     return "\n".join(lines)
+ 
+ def gen_many_enums(n):
+     lines = [f"// STRESS: {n} enum types"]
+     for i in range(n):
+         lines.append(f"enum E{i} {{")
+         for j in range(5):
+             lines.append(f"    | V{j}")
+         lines.append("}")
+     lines.append("main() {")
+     lines.append(f"    let e = E0.V0")
+     lines.append("    println(e)")
+     lines.append("    return 0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     return "\n".join(lines)
+ 
+ def gen_malformed_input(kind):
+     """Generate intentionally malformed inputs to test error recovery."""
+     if kind == "unclosed_braces":
+         return "// MALFORMED: unclosed braces\nclass A {\n  func f() {\n    if (true) {\n      let x = 1\n"
+     elif kind == "type_errors":
+         lines = ["// MALFORMED: type errors everywhere"]
+         for i in range(100):
+             lines.append(f"func bad{i}(): Int64 {{ return \"not_int_{i}\" }}")
+         lines.append("main() { return 0 }")
+         return "\n".join(lines)
+     elif kind == "syntax_garbage":
+         return "// MALFORMED: syntax garbage\n" + "}{}{}{class @@@ func !!! 123abc\n" * 50
+     elif kind == "huge_string_literal":
+         return f'main() {{ let s = "{"A" * 100000}"; println(s.size); return 0 }}'
+     elif kind == "recursive_type_ref":
+         lines = ["// MALFORMED: mutually recursive type references"]
+         for i in range(50):
+             j = (i + 1) % 50
+             lines.append(f"class R{i} {{ var next: R{j} = R{j}() }}")
+         lines.append("main() { return 0 }")
+         return "\n".join(lines)
+     return "// empty"
+ 
+ # ============================================================
+ # Test Runner
+ # ============================================================
+ 
+ def run_compile(src_path, extra_flags=None, timeout_sec=300):
+     """Compile a .cj file and measure time + memory."""
+     out_path = src_path.replace(".cj", "")
+     cmd = [CJC, src_path, "-o", out_path, "--profile-compile-time", "--profile-compile-memory"]
+     if extra_flags:
+         cmd.extend(extra_flags)
+ 
+     result = {
+         "cmd": " ".join(cmd),
+         "src_file": src_path,
+         "src_size_bytes": os.path.getsize(src_path),
+         "success": False,
+         "exit_code": None,
+         "wall_time_sec": 0,
+         "stdout": "",
+         "stderr": "",
+         "crashed": False,
+         "timeout": False,
+     }
+ 
+     start = time.monotonic()
+     try:
+         proc = subprocess.run(
+             cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_sec,
+             env={**os.environ, "CANGJIE_HOME": "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output"}
+         )
+         result["wall_time_sec"] = round(time.monotonic() - start, 3)
+         result["exit_code"] = proc.returncode
+         result["stdout"] = proc.stdout[-4000:] if len(proc.stdout) > 4000 else proc.stdout
+         result["stderr"] = proc.stderr[-4000:] if len(proc.stderr) > 4000 else proc.stderr
+         result["success"] = proc.returncode == 0
+         result["crashed"] = proc.returncode < 0  # negative = signal
+         if proc.returncode < 0:
+             result["crash_signal"] = -proc.returncode
+     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
+         result["wall_time_sec"] = timeout_sec
+         result["timeout"] = True
+     except Exception as e:
+         result["error"] = str(e)
+ 
+     return result
+ 
+ def parse_profile_output(stderr):
+     """Extract profile data from --profile-compile-time/memory output."""
+     profile = {}
+     for line in stderr.split("\n"):
+         line = line.strip()
+         if "time:" in line.lower() or "memory:" in line.lower() or "peak" in line.lower():
+             profile[line.split(":")[0].strip()] = line
+     return profile
+ 
+ # PLACEHOLDER_MAIN
```

</details>

+     path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, "many_classes_100.cj")
+     times = []
+     for i in range(20):
+         r = run_compile(path)
+         times.append(r["wall_time_sec"])
+         if r["crashed"]:
+             print(f"  CRASH on iteration {i}!")
+             break
+     if times:
+         avg_t = sum(times) / len(times)
+         max_t = max(times)
+         min_t = min(times)
+         stddev = (sum((t - avg_t)**2 for t in times) / len(times)) ** 0.5
+         repeat_result = {
+             "test_name": "repeated_compile_100classes_x20",
+             "category": "repeated_compilation",
+             "param": 20,
+             "iterations": len(times),
+             "avg_time": round(avg_t, 3),
+             "min_time": round(min_t, 3),
+             "max_time": round(max_t, 3),
+             "stddev": round(stddev, 3),
+             "success": True,
+             "wall_time_sec": round(sum(times), 3),
+         }
+         print(f"  avg={avg_t:.3f}s min={min_t:.3f}s max={max_t:.3f}s stddev={stddev:.3f}s")
+         all_results.append(repeat_result)
+ 
+     # ── Category 10: Parallel compilation flag ──
+     print("\n=== Category 10: Parallel vs Serial ===")
+     path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, "many_funcs_1000.cj")
+     if os.path.exists(path):
+         for jobs in [1, 2, 4, 8]:
+             r = run_compile(path, extra_flags=[f"-j{jobs}"])
+             r["test_name"] = f"parallel_j{jobs}_1000funcs"
+             r["category"] = "parallel"
+             r["param"] = jobs
+             print(f"  [j={jobs}] {'OK' if r['success'] else 'FAIL'} time={r['wall_time_sec']}s")
+             all_results.append(r)
+ 
+     # Save all results
+     results_path = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, "stress_test_results.json")
+     with open(results_path, "w") as f:
+         json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2, default=str)
+     print(f"\nResults saved to {results_path}")
+     return all_results
+

+     lines.append("func buildChain(): Int64 {")
+     indent = "    "

+         lines.append(f"{indent}let v{i}: Int64 = {i}")
+         if i < depth - 1:
+             lines.append(f"{indent}let f{i} = {{ =>")
+             indent += "    "

+     parts = " + ".join([f"v{i}" for i in range(depth)])
+     lines.append(f"{indent}var result: Int64 = {parts}")

+     for i in range(depth - 2, -1, -1):
+         indent = indent[:-4]
+         lines.append(f"{indent}}}")
+     if depth > 1:
+         lines.append(f"    return f0()")
+     else:
+         lines.append(f"    return v0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     lines.append("main() {")
+     lines.append("    println(buildChain())")
+     lines.append("    return 0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     return "\n".join(lines)

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



Good, simple lambdas work. The issue is with nested lambdas — the inner lambda returns a lambda, not Int64. Let me simplify the approach:

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



**🔧 Edit**


<!-- chunk-boundary -->


✏️ 编辑文件: `/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/stress_test.py` (20 行修改, -6 行)

<details><summary>查看变更 (20 行修改, -6 行)</summary>

```diff
- def gen_nested_closures(depth):
-     lines = [f"// STRESS: closure nesting depth = {depth}"]
-     lines.append("func buildChain(): Int64 {")
-     indent = "    "
-     for i in range(depth):
-         lines.append(f"{indent}let v{i}: Int64 = {i}")
-         if i < depth - 1:
-             lines.append(f"{indent}let f{i} = {{ =>")
-             indent += "    "
-     # innermost expression
-     parts = " + ".join([f"v{i}" for i in range(depth)])
-     lines.append(f"{indent}var result: Int64 = {parts}")
-     lines.append(f"{indent}result")
-     for i in range(depth - 2, -1, -1):
-         indent = indent[:-4]
-         lines.append(f"{indent}}}")
-     if depth > 1:
-         lines.append(f"    return f0()")
-     else:
-         lines.append(f"    return v0")
-     lines.append("}")
-     lines.append("main() {")
-     lines.append("    println(buildChain())")
-     lines.append("    return 0")
-     lines.append("}")
-     return "\n".join(lines)
+ def gen_nested_closures(depth):
+     """Generate deeply nested closures that capture variables from outer scopes."""
+     lines = [f"// STRESS: closure nesting depth = {depth}"]
+     lines.append("func buildChain(): Int64 {")
+     # Declare all variables at the top level of the function
+     for i in range(depth):
+         lines.append(f"    let v{i}: Int64 = {i}")
+     # Build nested closures, each capturing all variables
+     # f0 = { => v0 + { => v1 + { => v2 + ... }() }() }
+     # Simpler approach: chain of closures each calling the next
+     lines.append(f"    let f{depth-1} = {{ => v{depth-1} }}")
+     for i in range(depth - 2, -1, -1):
+         lines.append(f"    let f{i} = {{ => v{i} + f{i+1}() }}")
+     lines.append(f"    return f0()")
+     lines.append("}")
+     lines.append("main() {")
+     lines.append("    println(buildChain())")
+     lines.append("    return 0")
+     lines.append("}")
+     return "\n".join(lines)
```

</details>

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



Excellent results! Key finding: `deep_inherit_500` timed out at 300s — that's a performance cliff. The jump from depth=200 (19.7s) to depth=500 (timeout) suggests super-linear complexity in the inheritance chain handling. Let me now run targeted follow-up tests to pinpoint the exact threshold and gather memory profiling data:

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



**🔧 Write**


<!-- chunk-boundary -->


📝 写入文件: `/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/followup_tests.py` (129 行)

<details><summary>查看内容 (129 行)</summary>

```py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Targeted follow-up stress tests:
1. Pinpoint deep inheritance performance cliff
2. Memory profiling with --profile-compile-memory
3. Larger scale tests for categories that passed easily
4. AST release memory savings measurement
"""
import os, sys, time, subprocess, json

sys.path.insert(0, "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests")
from stress_test import *

CJC = find_cjc()
OUT_DIR = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases"
RESULTS_DIR = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/results"

all_results = []

def run_and_record(name, path, category, param, extra_flags=None, timeout_sec=300):
    r = run_compile(path, extra_flags=extra_flags, timeout_sec=timeout_sec)
    r["test_name"] = name
    r["category"] = category
    r["param"] = param
    status = "OK" if r["success"] else ("TIMEOUT" if r.get("timeout") else "FAIL")
    print(f"  [{name}] {status} time={r['wall_time_sec']}s")
    all_results.append(r)
    return r

# ── 1. Pinpoint deep inheritance cliff ──
print("=== Deep Inheritance: Pinpointing Performance Cliff ===")
for depth in [150, 175, 200, 225, 250, 275, 300, 350]:
    name = f"deep_inherit_{depth}"
    path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        f.write(gen_deep_inheritance(depth))
    run_and_record(name, path, "deep_inherit_cliff", depth, timeout_sec=120)

# ── 2. Memory profiling: compare with/without AST release ──
print("\n=== Memory Profiling: AST Release Savings ===")
for gen_func, gen_name, params in [
    (gen_many_classes, "classes", [100, 500, 1000]),
    (gen_many_functions, "funcs", [500, 2000, 5000]),
    (gen_generic_explosion, "generics", [100, 500, 1000]),
]:
    for n in params:
        name = f"mem_{gen_name}_{n}"
        path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
        with open(path, "w") as f:
            f.write(gen_func(n))
        # With AST release (default)
        r1 = run_and_record(f"{name}_release", path, "memory_profile", n)
        # Without AST release
        r2 = run_and_record(f"{name}_no_release", path, "memory_profile_no_release", n,
                           extra_flags=["--no-release-ast"])

# ── 3. Extreme scale tests ──
print("\n=== Extreme Scale Tests ===")
# 5000 classes
name = "many_classes_5000"
path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(gen_many_classes(5000))
print(f"  Generated {name}: {os.path.getsize(path)} bytes")
run_and_record(name, path, "extreme_scale", 5000, timeout_sec=600)

# 10000 functions
name = "many_funcs_10000"
path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(gen_many_functions(10000))
print(f"  Generated {name}: {os.path.getsize(path)} bytes")
run_and_record(name, path, "extreme_scale", 10000, timeout_sec=600)

# 200 nested closures
name = "nested_closures_200"
path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(gen_nested_closures(200))
run_and_record(name, path, "extreme_scale", 200, timeout_sec=120)

# 500 nested closures
name = "nested_closures_500"
path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(gen_nested_closures(500))
run_and_record(name, path, "extreme_scale", 500, timeout_sec=120)

# Deep expressions 2000, 5000
for d in [2000, 5000]:
    name = f"deep_expr_{d}"
    path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        f.write(gen_deep_nested_expr(d))
    run_and_record(name, path, "extreme_scale", d, timeout_sec=120)

# 2000 enums
name = "many_enums_2000"
path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"{name}.cj")
with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(gen_many_enums(2000))
run_and_record(name, path, "extreme_scale", 2000, timeout_sec=120)

# ── 4. Parallel scaling with large file ──
print("\n=== Parallel Scaling with 5000 Functions ===")
path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, "many_funcs_5000.cj")
if os.path.exists(path):
    for jobs in [1, 2, 4, 8, 16]:
        run_and_record(f"parallel_j{jobs}_5000funcs", path, "parallel_scaling", jobs,
                      extra_flags=[f"-j{jobs}"])

# ── 5. Emit-CHIR mode (tests PerformResultsSaving before AST release) ──
print("\n=== Emit-CHIR Mode Tests ===")
for gen_func, gen_name, n in [
    (gen_many_classes, "classes", 500),
    (gen_many_functions, "funcs", 1000),
]:
    name = f"emit_chir_{gen_name}_{n}"
    path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, f"mem_{gen_name}_{n}.cj")
    if os.path.exists(path):
        run_and_record(name, path, "emit_chir", n,
                      extra_flags=["--emit-chir"])

# Save results
results_path = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, "followup_results.json")
with open(results_path, "w") as f:
    json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2, default=str)
print(f"\nResults saved to {results_path}")

```

</details>


<!-- chunk-boundary -->

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



Excellent data! Key findings so far:

1. **Deep inheritance: clear O(n²) or worse complexity** — 150→7.7s, 200→19.9s, 250→44.3s, 300→88.1s, 350→timeout. This is a performance cliff.
2. **deep_expr_5000 failed** — need to check why
3. **Nested closures scale super-linearly** — 200→5.9s, 500→48.1s
4. **Parallel scaling works well** — j1=33.5s → j16=15.0s for 5000 functions

Let me check the deep_expr failure and get memory profiling data:

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



**🔧 Bash**


<!-- chunk-boundary -->


💻 执行命令 (12 行)

```bash
source /root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output/envsetup.sh 2>/dev/null
# Run and capture all output including any profile files
cjc /tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases/many_classes_100.cj -o /tmp/test_mem_prof --profile-compile-memory --profile-compile-time -Woff unused
echo "exit: $?"
# Check for any profile output files
ls -la /tmp/test_mem_prof* 2>/dev/null
ls -la /tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases/*.profile* 2>/dev/null
ls -la /tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases/*.json 2>/dev/null
# Check current dir
ls -la *.profile* 2>/dev/null
ls -la compile_time* compile_memory* 2>/dev/null
find /tmp -name "*profile*" -newer /tmp/test_mem_prof -maxdepth 2 2>/dev/null
```

-rwxr-xr-x 1 root root 1360192 Feb 27 04:35 /tmp/test_mem_prof

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



The profile flags don't produce visible output in this build. Let me use `/proc` to measure memory directly:

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



**🔧 Write**


<!-- chunk-boundary -->


📝 写入文件: `/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/memory_profile.py` (113 行)

<details><summary>查看内容 (113 行)</summary>

```py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Memory measurement wrapper: uses /proc/PID/status to track peak RSS
during compilation, comparing with and without --no-release-ast.
"""
import os, sys, time, subprocess, threading, json

CJC = "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output/bin/cjc"
RESULTS = []

def measure_compilation(src_path, label, extra_flags=None, timeout_sec=300):
    """Run cjc and track peak memory via /proc/PID/status."""
    out_path = src_path.replace(".cj", "_bin")
    cmd = [CJC, src_path, "-o", out_path, "-Woff", "unused"]
    if extra_flags:
        cmd.extend(extra_flags)

    peak_rss_kb = 0
    samples = []
    stop_event = threading.Event()

    proc = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                           env={**os.environ, "CANGJIE_HOME": "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output"})

    def monitor():
        nonlocal peak_rss_kb
        while not stop_event.is_set():
            try:
                with open(f"/proc/{proc.pid}/status", "r") as f:
                    for line in f:
                        if line.startswith("VmRSS:"):
                            rss = int(line.split()[1])
                            if rss > peak_rss_kb:
                                peak_rss_kb = rss
                            samples.append(rss)
                            break
            except (FileNotFoundError, ProcessLookupError):
                break
            time.sleep(0.05)  # 50ms sampling

    monitor_thread = threading.Thread(target=monitor, daemon=True)
    start = time.monotonic()
    monitor_thread.start()

    try:
        stdout, stderr = proc.communicate(timeout=timeout_sec)
    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
        proc.kill()
        stdout, stderr = proc.communicate()

    elapsed = time.monotonic() - start
    stop_event.set()
    monitor_thread.join(timeout=2)

    result = {
        "label": label,
        "src_file": os.path.basename(src_path),
        "src_size_kb": round(os.path.getsize(src_path) / 1024, 1),
        "exit_code": proc.returncode,
        "wall_time_sec": round(elapsed, 3),
        "peak_rss_mb": round(peak_rss_kb / 1024, 1),
        "samples": len(samples),
        "success": proc.returncode == 0,
    }
    return result

def main():
    sys.path.insert(0, "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests")
    from stress_test import gen_many_classes, gen_many_functions, gen_generic_explosion, gen_nested_closures

    cases_dir = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases"

    test_configs = [
        ("many_classes", gen_many_classes, [100, 500, 1000, 2000]),
        ("many_funcs", gen_many_functions, [500, 1000, 2000, 5000]),
        ("generics", gen_generic_explosion, [100, 500, 1000]),
        ("closures", gen_nested_closures, [50, 100, 200]),
    ]

    print(f"{'Label':<40} {'Size(KB)':>8} {'Time(s)':>8} {'PeakRSS(MB)':>12} {'Status':>8}")
    print("-" * 82)

    for category, gen_func, params in test_configs:
        for n in params:
            path = os.path.join(cases_dir, f"mem_{category}_{n}.cj")
            with open(path, "w") as f:
                f.write(gen_func(n))

            # With AST release
            r1 = measure_compilation(path, f"{category}_{n}_release")
            print(f"{r1['label']:<40} {r1['src_size_kb']:>8} {r1['wall_time_sec']:>8} {r1['peak_rss_mb']:>12} {'OK' if r1['success'] else 'FAIL':>8}")
            RESULTS.append(r1)

            # Without AST release
            r2 = measure_compilation(path, f"{category}_{n}_no_release", extra_flags=["--no-release-ast"])
            print(f"{r2['label']:<40} {r2['src_size_kb']:>8} {r2['wall_time_sec']:>8} {r2['peak_rss_mb']:>12} {'OK' if r2['success'] else 'FAIL':>8}")
            RESULTS.append(r2)

            # Memory savings
            if r1['success'] and r2['success'] and r2['peak_rss_mb'] > 0:
                savings = r2['peak_rss_mb'] - r1['peak_rss_mb']
                pct = (savings / r2['peak_rss_mb']) * 100 if r2['peak_rss_mb'] > 0 else 0
                print(f"  -> AST release savings: {savings:.1f} MB ({pct:.1f}%)")
            print()

    # Save results
    with open("/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/results/memory_profile.json", "w") as f:
        json.dump(RESULTS, f, indent=2)
    print(f"\nResults saved to /tmp/cjc_stress_tests/results/memory_profile.json")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



Interesting — the peak RSS difference between with/without AST release is minimal (< 1%). This is because peak RSS measures the high-water mark, and the AST release happens after the peak (during CodeGen, LLVM backend uses most memory). The AST release benefit would show in post-CHIR memory, not peak RSS. Let me measure the memory at different stages more precisely, and also run the deep inheritance complexity analysis:

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



**🔧 Write**


<!-- chunk-boundary -->


📝 写入文件: `/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/detailed_memory.py` (127 行)

<details><summary>查看内容 (127 行)</summary>

```py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Detailed memory timeline: sample RSS every 50ms during compilation
to see the memory curve and identify where AST release takes effect.
Also compute complexity analysis for deep inheritance.
"""
import os, sys, time, subprocess, threading, json

CJC = "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output/bin/cjc"

def measure_memory_timeline(src_path, label, extra_flags=None, timeout_sec=300):
    out_path = src_path.replace(".cj", "_bin")
    cmd = [CJC, src_path, "-o", out_path, "-Woff", "unused"]
    if extra_flags:
        cmd.extend(extra_flags)

    timeline = []
    stop_event = threading.Event()

    proc = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                           env={**os.environ, "CANGJIE_HOME": "/root/ace/cangjie_compiler/output"})

    def monitor():
        t0 = time.monotonic()
        while not stop_event.is_set():
            try:
                with open(f"/proc/{proc.pid}/status", "r") as f:
                    for line in f:
                        if line.startswith("VmRSS:"):
                            rss_kb = int(line.split()[1])
                            timeline.append((round(time.monotonic() - t0, 3), rss_kb))
                            break
            except (FileNotFoundError, ProcessLookupError):
                break
            time.sleep(0.05)

    monitor_thread = threading.Thread(target=monitor, daemon=True)
    start = time.monotonic()
    monitor_thread.start()
    try:
        stdout, stderr = proc.communicate(timeout=timeout_sec)
    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
        proc.kill()
        stdout, stderr = proc.communicate()
    elapsed = time.monotonic() - start
    stop_event.set()
    monitor_thread.join(timeout=2)

    peak_rss = max(t[1] for t in timeline) if timeline else 0
    # Find memory at 90% of total time (roughly post-CHIR)
    late_samples = [t[1] for t in timeline if t[0] > elapsed * 0.85]
    late_rss = sum(late_samples) // len(late_samples) if late_samples else 0

    return {
        "label": label,
        "wall_time_sec": round(elapsed, 3),
        "peak_rss_mb": round(peak_rss / 1024, 1),
        "late_rss_mb": round(late_rss / 1024, 1),
        "exit_code": proc.returncode,
        "n_samples": len(timeline),
        "timeline_summary": {
            "t25_rss_mb": round(timeline[len(timeline)//4][1]/1024, 1) if len(timeline) > 4 else 0,
            "t50_rss_mb": round(timeline[len(timeline)//2][1]/1024, 1) if len(timeline) > 2 else 0,
            "t75_rss_mb": round(timeline[3*len(timeline)//4][1]/1024, 1) if len(timeline) > 4 else 0,
            "final_rss_mb": round(timeline[-1][1]/1024, 1) if timeline else 0,
        }
    }

def main():
    sys.path.insert(0, "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests")
    from stress_test import gen_many_classes, gen_many_functions
    cases_dir = "/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/cases"

    print("=== Memory Timeline: 2000 classes ===")
    path = os.path.join(cases_dir, "mem_many_classes_2000.cj")
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        f.write(gen_many_classes(2000))

    r1 = measure_memory_timeline(path, "2000_classes_release")
    r2 = measure_memory_timeline(path, "2000_classes_no_release", extra_flags=["--no-release-ast"])

    print(f"  WITH release:    peak={r1['peak_rss_mb']}MB late={r1['late_rss_mb']}MB final={r1['timeline_summary']['final_rss_mb']}MB time={r1['wall_time_sec']}s")
    print(f"  WITHOUT release: peak={r2['peak_rss_mb']}MB late={r2['late_rss_mb']}MB final={r2['timeline_summary']['final_rss_mb']}MB time={r2['wall_time_sec']}s")
    print(f"  Late-stage savings: {r2['late_rss_mb'] - r1['late_rss_mb']:.1f} MB")
    print(f"  Timeline WITH:    25%={r1['timeline_summary']['t25_rss_mb']}MB 50%={r1['timeline_summary']['t50_rss_mb']}MB 75%={r1['timeline_summary']['t75_rss_mb']}MB")
    print(f"  Timeline WITHOUT: 25%={r2['timeline_summary']['t25_rss_mb']}MB 50%={r2['timeline_summary']['t50_rss_mb']}MB 75%={r2['timeline_summary']['t75_rss_mb']}MB")

    print("\n=== Memory Timeline: 5000 functions ===")
    path = os.path.join(cases_dir, "mem_many_funcs_5000.cj")
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        f.write(gen_many_functions(5000))

    r3 = measure_memory_timeline(path, "5000_funcs_release")
    r4 = measure_memory_timeline(path, "5000_funcs_no_release", extra_flags=["--no-release-ast"])

    print(f"  WITH release:    peak={r3['peak_rss_mb']}MB late={r3['late_rss_mb']}MB final={r3['timeline_summary']['final_rss_mb']}MB time={r3['wall_time_sec']}s")
    print(f"  WITHOUT release: peak={r4['peak_rss_mb']}MB late={r4['late_rss_mb']}MB final={r4['timeline_summary']['final_rss_mb']}MB time={r4['wall_time_sec']}s")
    print(f"  Late-stage savings: {r4['late_rss_mb'] - r3['late_rss_mb']:.1f} MB")

    # Deep inheritance complexity analysis
    print("\n=== Deep Inheritance Complexity Analysis ===")
    inherit_data = [
        (10, 0.855), (50, 1.203), (100, 2.68), (150, 7.737),
        (175, 12.586), (200, 19.876), (225, 30.347), (250, 44.344),
        (275, 63.214), (300, 88.132),
    ]
    print(f"  {'Depth':>6} {'Time(s)':>8} {'Ratio':>8} {'~O(n^x)':>8}")
    for i in range(1, len(inherit_data)):
        d1, t1 = inherit_data[i-1]
        d2, t2 = inherit_data[i]
        if t1 > 0 and d1 > 0:
            import math
            ratio = t2 / t1
            n_ratio = d2 / d1
            if n_ratio > 1 and ratio > 0:
                exponent = math.log(ratio) / math.log(n_ratio)
            else:
                exponent = 0
            print(f"  {d2:>6} {t2:>8.3f} {ratio:>8.2f} {exponent:>8.2f}")

    results = {"timeline_2000classes": [r1, r2], "timeline_5000funcs": [r3, r4], "inherit_complexity": inherit_data}
    with open("/tmp/cjc_stress_tests/results/detailed_memory.json", "w") as f:
        json.dump(results, f, indent=2, default=str)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```

<!-- chunk-boundary -->



Excellent data! Key findings:

1. **AST release late-stage savings: ~80MB** for both 2000 classes and 5000 functions — the savings are real but show in late-stage memory, not peak RSS
2. **Deep inheritance complexity: O(n^3.5~3.8)** — this is a severe polynomial blowup, likely in type checking or vtable resolution
3. **Final RSS with release: 527MB vs 538MB without** — 11MB difference at process exit for 2000 classes

```
   521→bool CompilerInstance::PerformASTRelease()
   522→{
   523→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "Release AST");
   524→
   525→    // Always extract CodeGen metadata before potential release.
   526→    PrepareCodeGenInfo();
   527→
   528→    // Save results (e.g., CJO in CHIR output mode) before AST is freed.
   529→    // PerformResultsSaving() may need srcPkgs, so it must run before ReleaseASTMemory().
   530→    if (!resultsSaved) {
   531→        if (!PerformResultsSaving()) {
   532→            return false;  // Propagate save failure to abort compilation.
   533→        }
   534→        resultsSaved = true;
   535→    }
   536→
   537→    // Write incremental compilation cache before AST is freed (ADR-009).
   538→    // WriteCachedInfo dereferences srcPkgs[0], order, varAndFuncDep, semaInfo.usages.
   539→    if (ShouldWriteCacheFile() && !cacheWritten) {
   540→        UpdateCachedInfo();
   541→        WriteCachedInfo();
   542→        cacheWritten = true;
   543→    }
   544→
   545→    // Allow skipping AST release for debugging (e.g., ASan leak analysis).
   546→    if (invocation.globalOptions.noReleaseAST) {
   547→        return true;
   548→    }
   549→
   550→    ReleaseASTMemory();
   551→    return true;
   552→}
   553→
   554→void CompilerInstance::ReleaseASTMemory()
   555→{
   556→    if (astReleased) {
   557→        return;
   558→    }
   559→
   560→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   561→    // Phase 1: Clear CHIR-layer AST references
   562→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   563→
   564→    // 1a. Global annotation info (holds AST ClassDef*/Decl* pointers)
   565→    CHIR::ClearGlobalAnnotationInfo();
   566→
   567→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   568→    // Phase 2: Clear CompilerInstance direct member AST references
   569→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   570→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   571→    astPkg2chirPkgMap.clear();
   572→#endif
   573→    currentPkg = nullptr;
   574→    mangledName2DeclMap.clear();
   575→    rawMangleName2DeclMap.clear();
   576→    declsWithDuplicatedRawMangleName.clear();
   577→    directExtends.clear();
   578→    order.clear();
   579→    chirInfo.ccTys.clear();
   580→    pkgs.clear();
   581→
   582→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   583→    // Phase 3: Release managers (destruction order matters)
   584→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   585→
   586→    // 3a. TypeChecker holds TypeManager& reference, must be freed first.
   587→    delete typeChecker;
   588→    typeChecker = nullptr;
   589→
   590→    // 3b. TypeManager holds 15+ AST pointer collections.
   591→    delete typeManager;
   592→    typeManager = nullptr;
   593→
   594→    // 3c. GenericInstantiationManager
   595→    delete gim;
   596→    gim = nullptr;
   597→
   598→    // 3d. TestManager holds ImportManager and TypeManager references.
   599→    delete testManager;
   600→    testManager = nullptr;
   601→
   602→    // 3e. BaseMangler — ManglerContext holds AST pointer maps.
   603→    mangler.reset();
   604→
   605→    // 3f. ImportManager — stack member, clear AST references and release imported packages.
   606→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   607→
   608→    // 3g. PackageManager — clear resolved dependency data.
   609→    if (packageManager) {
   610→        packageManager->ClearASTReferences();
   611→    }
   612→
   613→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   614→    // Phase 4: Release AST core data (strict order)
   615→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   616→
   617→    // 4a. Release AST nodes first (triggers Symbol detach).
   618→    srcPkgs.clear();
   619→
   620→    // 4b. Release ASTContext (depends on AST nodes being destructed).
   621→    pkgCtxMap.clear();
   622→
   623→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   624→    // Phase 5: Mark completion
   625→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   626→    astReleased = true;
   627→}
```

   354→    void ClearASTReferences()
   355→    {
   356→        curPackage = nullptr;
   357→        cjoManager->ClearImportedPackages();
   358→        // Clear all maps holding AST Decl/Package pointers to prevent dangling references.
   359→        fileImportedDeclsMap.clear();
   360→        fileUsedMacroDeclsMap.clear();
   361→        importedDeclsMap.clear();
   362→        DeleteASTWriters();  // Must delete ASTWriter* before clearing to avoid memory leak.
   363→        directMacroDeps.clear();
   364→        declsImportedByNodeMap.clear();
   365→        declToTypeAlias.clear();
   366→        if (dependencyGraph) {
   367→            dependencyGraph.reset();
   368→        }
   369→    }
   370→
   371→    std::unordered_map<std::string, std::string> GetDepPkgCjoPaths() const
   372→    {
   373→        return cjoFilePaths;
```

<details><summary>返回结果 (120 行)</summary>

```
   354→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseFuncBody(const AST::Decl& decl)
   355→{
   356→    if (decl.astKind != AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL) {
   357→        return;
   358→    }
   359→    // const_cast is safe: we own the AST tree and are past the translation point for this decl.
   360→    auto& funcDecl = const_cast<AST::FuncDecl&>(static_cast<const AST::FuncDecl&>(decl));
   361→    if (funcDecl.funcBody != nullptr && funcDecl.funcBody->body != nullptr) {
   362→        funcDecl.funcBody->body.reset();
   363→    }
   364→}
   365→
   366→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseVarInitializer(AST::VarDeclAbstract& decl)
   367→{
   368→    if (decl.initializer != nullptr) {
   369→        decl.initializer.reset();
   370→    }
   371→}
   372→
   373→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(const AST::Package& /* pkg */)
   374→{
   375→    // Release method bodies from nominal decls (class/interface/struct/enum) after batch translation.
   376→    // Uses GetMemberDecls() which is the canonical way to access members across all nominal types.
   377→    auto releaseMethodBodies = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls) {
   378→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   379→            auto& memberDecls = decl->GetMemberDecls();
   380→            for (auto& member : memberDecls) {
   381→                ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   382→            }
   383→        }
   384→    };
   385→    releaseMethodBodies(nominalDecls);
   386→    releaseMethodBodies(genericNominalDecls);
   387→}
   388→
   389→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(const InitOrder& initOrder)
   390→{
   391→    for (auto& [file, decls] : initOrder) {
   392→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   393→            if (auto* varDecl = DynamicCast<AST::VarDeclAbstract*>(const_cast<AST::Decl*>(decl.get()))) {
   394→                ReleaseVarInitializer(*varDecl);
   395→            }
   396→        }
   397→    }
   398→}
   399→
   400→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies()
   401→{
   402→    for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   403→        if (NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   404→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   405→        }
   406→    }
   407→    for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   408→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   409→    }
   410→}
   411→
   412→void AST2CHIR::TranslateAllDecls(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   413→{
   414→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "TranslateAllDecls");
   415→    // step 1: translate nominal decls first (signatures only — method bodies are translated in step 3)
   416→    TranslateNominalDecls(pkg);
   417→    // NOTE: Do NOT call ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies() here.
   418→    // TranslateNominalDecls only translates signatures (types, params, attributes).
   419→    // Method bodies are translated in step 3 via globalAndMemberFuncs, and released there
   420→    // by ReleaseFuncBody (serial) or ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies (parallel).
   421→    // Releasing here would null funcBody->body before step 3 translates it,
   422→    // causing null pointer dereference in HasDelegatedThisCall / TranslateNestedFunc.
   423→
   424→    // step 2: translate initialization of global var
   425→    TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(pkg, initOrder);
   426→    ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(initOrder);
   427→
   428→    // do this after init of gv to ensure gvinit of CustomAnnotations go after real gv's
   429→    // this is always safe because such gvinit's are generated by CHIR and cannot be referenced in source
   430→    for (auto decl : annoOnlyDecls) {
   431→        CreateAnnoOnlyDeclSig(*decl);
   432→    }
   433→
   434→    // step 3: translate body of all funcs, the process can be run in parallel according to the compilation option
   435→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   436→    if (opts.GetJobs() > 1) {
   437→        TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel();
   438→        ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies();
   439→    } else {
   440→        for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   441→            if (!NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   442→                continue;
   443→            }
   444→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   445→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   446→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   447→            if (decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GLOBAL)) {
   448→                trans.CollectValueAnnotation(*decl);
   449→            }
   450→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   451→        }
   452→        for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   453→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   454→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   455→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   456→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   457→        }
   458→    }
   459→    // the parallel helper does not accept this type, use serialised translation
   460→    for (auto decl : annoFactoryFuncs) {
   461→        auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   462→        trans.SetTopLevel(*decl.first);
   463→        trans.TranslateAnnoFactoryFuncBody(*decl.first, *decl.second);
   464→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl.first);
   465→    }
   466→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   467→
   468→    // step 4: set `CompileTimeValue` for lambda — operates on CHIR IR, unaffected by AST release
   469→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   470→    for (auto func : package->GetGlobalFuncs()) {
   471→        if (func->TestAttr(Attribute::CONST)) {
   472→            SetCompileTimeValueFlagRecursivly(*func);
   473→        }
```

</details>

<details><summary>返回结果 (654 行)</summary>

    21→using namespace Cangjie::AST;
